

--- blocked.pdf ---

Blocked
Red Alert announced all over the area. As the rain increases, water level starts to
rise all over the roads. Roads were blocked, people who were stuck were being trans-
ported to relief camps.
A man's phone rings and is called to check for the drainage to check for any blocks
and find a solution. The man wears his badge with the post of "Drainage Specialist"
written on it. He sits on the boat, while being transported to the main, the man
falls asleep.
A glimpse of 2004 floods and 2019 kerala floods goes through his mind. People strug-
gling to go home, Snakes swimming through the water, Electric poles falling down.
The man wakes up reaching the drainage point where the issue started. The main wears
a swimsuit and oxygen cylinder and gets down the drainage hole. He finds plastic ac-
cumulated at the drainage grating to the main drainage blocked exactly where all
other pipelines connect causing the flood. The man tries to remove the contents but
the pressure kept building.
2013 uttarakhand floods, people start evaluating their homes as water starts to build
up and small earthquakes cause landslides. People's homes destroyed and debris
overflow.
Here, the man swims up, grabs a crowbar and swims back down. He breaks the drainage
grating. The floodwater begins draining rapidly after the grate is broken. The man
starts getting sucked into the drainage, so he pulls the rope signalling people on
the boat to pull him up. The crew starts pulling the man up. Streets slowly clear,
and rescue boats can move freely again. The man pulls himself out of the drain, ex-
hausted but relieved.
Few days later
The man walks of the street and finds a boy throwing a plastic wrapper on the floor.
The man runs towards the wrapper, picks it up. He looks at the boy, but he was gone.
He takes the wrapper and puts it in a dustbin.
“Floods don’t begin with rain. They begin with waste.”


--- Bloody Politics.pdf ---

Bloody Politics
Bangalore 2025
Vikas Shetty aged 32, the son of CM Ravindra Shetty starts a new party with the name
"UIA- United Indian Association". Ravindra Shetty in press meet "He is not my son
anymore! Let us see what he does! Whatever he does, we will win in this elections!".
Troll channels start to make father vs son videos viral. Vikas in the Inaugural
speech says "People thought my father will join this party before his press meet! But
I have come for you! The people! I am conducting a survey and we are on our way to
solve atleast 30% of your problems before the elections! I feel honesty towards the
people is the only way I can win! What I say will be truthful to all of you and
that's my promise!". On this note Vikas starts survey throughout the state. Vikas and
his team short list the survey for the most common and easily executable problems and
starts working on it. The primary problem was water scarcity, mainly in bangalore
which was the constituency he was standing in. So he decided to propose a canal join-
ing all the lakes of Bangalore. He along with few volunteers decide to clean the vr-
ishabhavathi river from the dried up areas in yeshwantpur to the innovative film City
stretching nearly 40kms. The cleaning campain was successful and people were happy
with what Vikas was doing. One day Ravindra calls Vikas to their house. Vikas enters
the house, meets his mother and his mother asks "How are you my son? Where were you
living all these days?". Vikas replies "I was fine, why did your Ravindra Shetty!
Your husband call me?". Vikas's mother says "He is your father, atleast give him that
respect!". Vikas turns his face and says "Call him! I have no respect for him!".
Suddenly from behind Ravindra with a knife stabs on vikas's back. Vikas shocked
turns, his eyes blur and says "Why? Why are you doing this to me?". Ravindra says
"You are putting my 55 years of political career in danger! The only thing I have
right now except Reputation is Power! I will not let you take it from me!". Vikas
shouts in pain. He gets up and pushes Ravindra. Ravindra asks his men to kill vikas.
Vikas runs out in pain, while Ravindra's men followed. Vikas is completely beaten up.
Vikas's mother asks Ravindra "Spare our son!". Ravindra replies "No! My experience in
politics is nearly twice his age! I won't let a insect be a issue to me. If you ask
him to spare once again! I will not hesitate to kill you too". Vikas's mother begs
Ravindra to spare him. Ravindra takes the knife and cuts his wife's throat killing
her. Vikas hearing his mother screaming pushes Ravindra's men and try to enter the
house. Ravindra's men kept pushing him out. Vikas in a fit of rage, takes a knife
from one of the henchmen and stabs each one of them. Holds his mother in his arms and
starts to cry. Ravindra comes back and grabs Vikas in his hands and says "You
shouldn't have left me!". Before Ravindra could do anything, Vikas stabs Ravindra and
kills him. One of Ravindra's men calls the press. Vikas slowly walks out of the
house, before he could leave, press arrive crowding at the house. A reported named
Vikram asks "Sir! Who killed your father and mother? Was it you? For your political
benefit?". Vikas closes his eyes and remembers his inaugural speech "I feel honesty
towards the people is the only way I can win! What I say will be truthful to all of
you and that's my promise!". Vikas says to Vikram "I got a phone call from someone
from here that my father and mother was in danger. When I arrived, this was the situ-
ation! Please leave me alone, as I suffering from a lot of pain, not about my father
but my innocent mother!". Vikas folds his hands and asks everyone to leave crying.
Ravindra's political party's men join Vikas knowing what the truth was.
Vikram on his Press channel says on Live "This statement was given by UIA leader Mr
Vikas Shetty 'I feel honesty towards the people is the only way I can win! What I say
will be truthful to all of you and that's my promise!' but he has been lying to us
the whole time saying 'I got a phone call from someone from here that my father and
mother was in danger. When I arrived, this was the situation!' This is false as we
have cross examined his call history and no such calls have come. We also have a CCTV
footage of the house where Shetty is clearly seen killing his father Ravindra Shetty
and Ravindra Shetty who had killed his wife Mrs Anuradha Shetty. Vikas Shetty was
clearly seen killing Ravindra Shetty and his men! How can we hand our state to such
criminals? Are the police sleeping?". Vikas throws the TV remote on the floor listen-
ing to this. Vikas asks his men "I was turned into a politician at that point of
time! But who is this guy?". Vikas calls the commissioner "I want that news re-
porter!". UIA party members among themselves "He has the real power now! That's why
he has become the real politician which he was not before! He has slowly turned into
his father". Commissioner gets into the press company named News 3.42 to arrest
Vikram. Vikram resists the arrest without knowing what he was being charged for. The
commissioner named Raj says "We will charge you with more, if you don't come with
us". Vikram turns towards the camera which was being pointed at them Live and says
"Common people have no rights to raise voice against politicians, then what demo-
cratic country are we in?". Vikas starts to sweat looking at the news. People who
thought that Vikas wouldn't have killed his parents also started to turn against him.
Vikram was pulled at taken into custody by Raj. Mid way they take a turn and goes to
an old abandoned factory and points a gun at him. Few black cars arrive at the scene
and from that comes Vikas. Vikram says "I knew, you were behind it!". Vikas says "I
agree I killed my father and his men, but what can I do?". Vikram says "It is not
only about killing Ravindra, it is about Zach medics!". Vikas starts to sweat and
asks "What is that?". Vikram says "How can you forget the Drug Bust in Zach medics
for which you were arrested 6 months back, but was cleared of charges with your
father's power! You studied in Canada, so people didn't know you were Ravindra's son.
But your father threw you out and then you became power hungry! You destroyed even
the lives of the youth volunteers who came for the vrishabhavathi river cleaning camp
by giving them free juice with drugs mixed in it!". Vikas says "So! You know it all?
But what is the use? You are going to die!". Vikram says "You kill me now, the de-
tails are in the computer I use, the next person replacing me will get that. So he
will access the files and your history will come to surface!". Vikas says "No! I
can't afford it!". Vikram says "Then to get it you will have to release me!". Vikas
says "Why will I release you? I only need the password which can be retrieved by a
hacker and laptop will be brought by my assistant!". Vikas calls a hacker to the fac-
tory and asks his men to get Vikram's laptop. Vikram says "Then kill me! You have ar-
ranged all these right?". Vikas says "I am not a fool! If the hacker is unable to re-
trieve it, then what?". Vikram says "I thought, you will be like the old style fool-
ish villain. But you are better!". Vikas asks "better?". Just then, The hacker and
his men arrive at the factory. Vikas gives Vikram's laptop to the hacker and says
"You have to open this laptop and delete all the files!". The hacker opens the laptop
and says "This laptop has a feature! It will not let the laptop to be hacked within
the lockscreen and the lock can be only entered thrice, if not it will self de-
struct!". Vikas says "If it self destructs, then all the data will go! Then I don't
need to worry!". The hacker puts wrong password 3 times and the screen goes blank.
Vikram starts laughing. Vikas shocked asks "your data is deleted, why are you laugh-
ing?". Vikas says "Which fool called this guy a hacker? It was not a self destruct
program. It was a File sending program. It sends all the files through my social me-
dia handle and don't think internet is not connected. My Hotspot in my phone is on!".
Vikas calls the commissioner to remove the files, but the commissioner Raj rejects
his call, as he too is under inspection from human rights commission. Vikram asks a
man to remove his hands which were tied. Vikram says "A fool and his foolish party.
You are actually like the old style villain!". Vikram walks, Vikas shouts "You will
die from my hands!". Vikram says "Your weapon is a gun, my weapon is my mouth! Words
spoken have more emphasis!".
[Interval]
Next day, Vikram goes to 3.42 office and asks the chief editor to add his points
along with the proof of Vikas's arrest in the Drug Bust, held 6 months ago. On Live
TV he exposed Vikas saying "A politician now, a drug lord before. Here is the proof.
My face looks beaten up? But the public was beaten with slippers because of people
like these. Youths were drugged during the vrishabhavathi river. Here is the proof.
We are having a proof talk today. If Vikas is seeing this! It's time to End!". Vikram
takes his bag and leaves the office. On his way back, Vikram's car is hit with a
truck and sandwiched within a tree. Ambulance arrive and Vikram is taken to hospital.
His shoulder bone and back had severe fractures. Vikas says to his party members
"Vikram is Down! Lets start the campain!". Vikas runs a free health supply campain
run by Zach Medics. It was a card for which people got free medicines made by Zach
medics. People were signed for organ donations along with the scheme papers. Zach
medics stock market goes sky rocketing. Enquiry was started on Vikas using the closed
down Zach medics. But before they could I anything, Zach medics had rebranded it's
logo and a new permission was made and for which the owner's name was Jennifer
Shetty, Vikas's wife. Meanwhile, Vikram was discharged and was taken home. He
couldn't walk and bend is back and required 2 months rest. Raj who was in suspension
was brought back by Vikas. Raj asks Vikas "What happened to Vikram?". Vikas says
"Vikram won't get up until the elections gets over in two months. We have full lib-
erty". Vikram calls his friends to his house and asks to check what medicines are for
which purpose. Out of which one was found for paralysing the lower body. Vikram says
"Vikas is trying to paralyse my lower body! This medicine! I won't spare him". Vikram
stops taking the medicine and starts to get cured. Within one and a half month,
Vikram starts to walk. Vikram goes to News 3.42 and starts a live. Vikram says
"Elections are coming this month. We already have a person in mind. Once close your
eyes and think, the person whom you're going to vote, has he done anything to you?
For example, If you have Vikas in your mind, he cleaned the vrishabhavathi river. But
did you get clean water? He conducted a medical camp. Did every medical shop have a
medicine from Zach medics? Did you guys even check the expiry date before buying this
medicines? Did the medicine cure your ailment? This is your final chance! The State's
Democracy is in your! No Our hands! If we loose it now! We will loose it forever!
Thank you!". The manager asks "That's all? For saying this you came all the way
here?". Vikram says "People will understand today! If not today then Tomorrow!".
Vikas watching the live shouts "How did he get cured so early? Why is he using me as
the example? I am! I am going to kill him!". Vikas takes a gun and gets into his car.
Raj stops him and says "Sir, already the election is out of your hand, this will
cause more damage!". vikas shouts "No! I won't win this elections, then why shouldn't
I kill him now! Driver take the vehicle!". Vikas on his way to Vikram's house is fol-
lowed by police. Vikas asks to stop the car and gets down. Vikas to the police "Thank
you all for following me, but I don't think you need to follow me before elections!".
Raj comes out of the police vehicle and says "You are not being given protection, you
are being arrested. Your charges are strong and putting all this charges aside, you
have deceived the election commission!". Vikas gets in his car and asks his driver to
go as fast as possible. Meanwhile the police kept on chasing him. Vikas takes his gun
and takes down each police vehicle shooting at its tyres one by one. Vikas laughs,
and reaches Vikram's house. Vikas finds the house locked. Suddenly a car's light
flashes on him and Vikram comes out. Vikas shoots Vikram but misses. Vikram gets in
his car and takes a reverse. Vikas runs and gets into his car and starts to follow
Vikram.
Vikas shoots the car's tyres, Vikram's car slides, he turns the car and takes a
person's bike and goes. Vikas kept on chasing him but, once Vikram got the bike he
raced forward. Vikas kicks his driver out and sits on the driver seat and says "I'll
do it myself!". Suddenly, the police starts to chase Vikram again. Vikram in frustra-
tion, changes the gear to reverse and reverse the car, on the police had reached
somewhat front, vikas pulls the hand brake and changes the gear, turns the vehicle
and goes. Vikas's car was a 4x4, he climbs over the divider and takes the opposite
lane and starts to chase, Vikram. Vikas says to himself "First I'll kill Vikram and
then deal with the police!". By this time, Vikas was long ahead of Vikram. Vikram fi-
nally finds Vikram, hits his bike and throws Vikram into Vikas's car. Takes him to
the old abandoned factory. Vikas grabs his gun, points at Vikram and says "Why? So
much chasing and all these things? I got tired". Vikram says "Shoot me!". Vikas says
"If you haven't planned something, then you wouldn't ask me to kill you!". Vikram
says "No! Nothing this time! Shoot me!". Vikas doubtful "Are you recording this with
a button camera? Your shirt's button is different from others!". Vikas tears open
Vikas's shirt and find the circuit connecting the camera. Vikram kicks Vikas and
Vikas falls down. Vikram gets up and says "You're done! Mr Vikas Shetty, Son of
Ravindra Shetty!". Vikas tries to shoot Vikram but he was out of bullets, since he
used them in shooting the police vehicle tyres. Vikram punches vikas. Vikas gets up
and kicks down Vikram and says "I don't need a weapon to destroy you!". Vikas contin-
uously punches Vikram. Vikram grabs a nearby metal rod and hits Vikas on his head.
Vikas calls down, Vikram calls and ambulance and is taken to hospital. One day before
elections,Vikram on News 3.42 Live "Not everything you get free is free. You get free
something here and loose something on the other side. This is the rule of the nature,
and this is what our democracy is about. People must understand their leader before
Understanding anything else!". Next day, elections take place smoothly. Vikas was in
coma. The election results are announced. Vikram on the news "UIA doesn't get any
seat in the state. It is quite usual for a new party. But it is unusual for a famous
person Mr Shetty standing in the elections. And in bangalore North constituency, NOTA
has played an important role and a re election will be held. This is Vikram signing
off for the day!".
One month after the elections
Vikas wakes up from coma and asks "Did we win the elections?". His wife Jennifer
replies "No! We lost in all the constituency we were standing in". Few days later,
Vikas asks his party members to come to the party office. Vikas walks to the flag and
removes it down and says "I am dissolving this party! We are not fit for ruling this
state or the country!". Vikram on News "Mr Shetty dissolves his party, removes the
flag. I have never seen such a good decision taken by any politician!". Vikas is sud-
denly shot with a gun in middle of this. Vikram says "This is going to be a problem".
Vikram turns off the live and gets into his car and goes to the party office. There,
people were running here and there, Vikram pushes the people and finds Vikas dead. He
looks at Jennifer and finds her unshaken, gun in her hands. Vikram asks Jennifer "Why
did you kill him?". Jennifer "I only want to live with people having power! Not
fools!". Vikram says "He is a changed man! Why are you like this now?". Jennifer says
"It's over! I am going back to Canada!". Vikram shouts "No! You will not! I have the
proof that you have killed vikas! And you will be arrested!". Vikram had the button
camera turned on. He sends it to the police. Police arrived at the scene and Jennifer
is taken to custody. Vikram later that day on Live "What is happening in Karnataka is
a Bloody Politics! And the Face of the Bloody Politics is 'The Shetty Family'!".
The End
Written by Nivedh Sunil


--- Clandestine.pdf ---

CLANDESTINE
Year 1996, New Delhi
Computers had entered into Indian markets. Emails had began to grow in India. One
could send an email to his son, brother, daughter, sister, wife, husband or friend
any family members who were somewhere around the world and could get an instant reply
or atleast a faster method of mailing. Pay to use computer shops had began and people
started making email ID's and joining into the new world of networking. Dev Singh aka
computer Dev aka Devji aged 37 was a early retired businessman who came from America
and kept a shop of pay to use computers in Delhi. He had most trust in his locality.
He had a son named Ethan aged 5. His wife had passed away due to some unknown ill-
ness. Dev had a book in which he had written everyone who created a email id and
their password as most of them either didn't know to use a computer or few had bad
memory. Even though few knew their password and Id Dev kept a record of it.
Year 2023, New Delhi
As India advances to become more network or internet dependent from cash to UPI,
shops to online websites all have come in the swipe of our hands. Before even start-
ing to operate a smartphone people are asked for their email id and password. Emails
have become more centric in using a phone. Linking all bank accounts to email id and
using the same email for UPI payments.
All emails in Delhi has been hacked. Including police officers control room id. UPI
linked with these accounts have deposited their full amount to an unknown bank ac-
counts all over India. All bank accounts in Delhi has deposited cash to multiple ac-
counts. Panic has hit the public and people have started filing FIR in all stations
across Delhi. More than 25 lakh people have lost their money and more than 10 lakh
people have lodged complaint for the same. Government hands over the case to the
Cyber Crime Division under CBI. Officer Ethan is given charge of the case. Ethan de-
cides to catch all the people who are involved in cyber crime who have hacked bank
servers. Ethan catches 4 people namely Joseph, Xavier, Venkat and Ashraf. The hackers
Joseph, Xavier, Venkat, and Ashraf were initially arrested because they were sus-
pected of being involved in the cybercrime that led to the hacking of emails, UPI ac-
counts, and bank servers. They were used to work in this field except Venkat. They
were already once caught During a previous cyber crime. During interrogation Joseph
says "I do this kind of work but my computer only can hack about 2-3 bank accounts at
once. I cannot hack more than this and such a huge online robbery needs at least a
huge computer setup and an intelligent brain". Ethan replies to Joseph saying "You
are saying you are not intelligent enough (smiles). (Looks at another officer) send
him back". Xavier says "I have the same kind of computer Joseph just said about. But
my job is different. I usually hack people's email and send mails to other email ID's
asking for money. I need big computers because I mass send the emails to at most
reach". Venkat says " I am still learner in hacking. I don't have experience much to
handle so many people at once". Ashraf says "I usually hack international accounts.
This is out of my reach. Indian currency has less exchange but my dealings are in us
dollars". After hearing all these, Ethan goes to the director of CBI and says "Sir,
this case is not going anywhere. People's cash has gone. There is no way to get it
back. Without proper information and proof whom can we take to custody?". Director
Mohan Sharma says "I know it is a difficult job but understand the seriousness of
this case. Even the police control room's email id was hacked". Mohan's eyes turns
towards the TV where news was running. It said "People have started a riot in the
streets of Delhi. People demand their cash back and are asking the government to re-
fund the tax they have levied from the people for so many years and giving no bene-
fits from it". Mohan says to Ethan "Now do you understand why I am giving you outmost
pressure is because of this. Now politicians will start calling us and we have to get
ready with answers. That's why you must find the culprits". Ethan walks out of the
CBI headquarters when people start throwing stones at him asking for giving back
their money which was taken. The misconceptions rose to peak level. Ethan asked offi-
cials to always keep an eye on Joseph, Xavier, Venkat and Ashraf. Ethan gets in his
car and drives towards Legislative assembly of Delhi. Ethan meets the CM Ahmed. Ethan
says to Ahmed "Sir, I am Ethan Singh from Cyber Crime Division, CBI. People in the
state have started riots and are demanding tax returns. We are trying to keep the
public under control though we can't for longer time. We must have to do something
immediately". Ahmed replies "I know that this is an high stake issue in Delhi. That
is why I called RBI immediately as soon as the online robbery news reached me. RBI
said that even their Accounts has been hacked. Now only cash could be transferred in
cash until this situation comes under control. Nowadays, Even beggars have UPI. Even
they don't have much Currency in circulation. Though, RBI could trace only 4 bank ac-
counts that has been registered in Delhi and online payments have been working. And
the names are ( grabs a paper) , Joseph, Xavier, Venkat and Ashraf. I guess you could
get more information if you trace them". Ethan replies "I already have them on cus-
tody". Ethan runs and gets into his car and leaves back to CBI headquarters. Ethan
reaches the headquarters. They 4 were still at the HQ. Ethan goes in front of them
and says "You 4 cannot do a robbery alone because you already told me those con-
straints. Though you 4 can do this together because there you don't have a con-
straint". Venkat says "I really don't understand what you are saying!. We have been
here for one whole day without food or anything to drink and you are suspecting us 4
to do the crime together?". Ethan says "It is obvious and look at this sheet from RBI
who keeps a record of each and every transaction till date made online. Only you 4
people's accounts have used for online payment after the bank accounts were hacked.
You are talking about food and water for today, many people are starving after their
accounts were hacked and many are going to starve more. Their hard earned money has
gone!". Xavier says "Ok I agree what doubt you have. We 4 are friends. But when the
incident had happened, we were in Lucknow. We had gone for a trip. Venkat is learning
from us 3. We are going to start a company soon". Ashraf breaks in and says "The on-
line payments you saw were done after reaching delhi. At the borders of Delhi. And
for your confirmation we still have our money!". Ethan was not convinced completely.
He asks the CBI officials to check whether what they were telling us actually true.
And infact it was. They were in Lucknow when the incident had occurred. Ethan asks
them "What is going to be the name of your company?". Joseph says "Delhi and Co.".
Ethan asks them to leave. There was a shower of stones being thrown at the CBI head-
quarters and legislative assembly". Ahmed immediately arranges a press meet. Ahmed
says "I request you to stop the riot as the delhi government has decided to do tax
return for the public depending on how much tax they have paid. If taxes have not
been filed by a person, they would not be benefited from this scheme. This scheme
will be implemented within 2 days. The respective bank will be sending sms on date
and time slot to collect the amount. Payment of taxes will be waved for a period
which will be intimated later. If no message has been sent they can enquire the re-
spective bank for further queries". Ethan looks at the press meet in TV and says
"Will people actually benefit from this. Many of the tax we pay just go to the pock-
ets of people like Ahmed. Ahmed himself is coming and saying that he is waving the
tax doesn't seem right". Dev Singh right next to him "He just wants people's vote in
the next election after that again these taxes will go to his own pocket. He has con-
nections directly with the RBI". Ethan says "Who would be that hacker who is taking
revenge against this politician who has another face which many have not seen?". Dev
says "It is your job son. It will be interesting to hear you say your crime stories
to me later"
[Interval]
Ahmed calls Mohan and says "I want the culprits to be caught before the scheme
starts. We are out of funds. We need immediate arrest of the culprits and return
their money back to people. consider it pressure or whatever. I want the culprits im-
mediately". Mohan calls and tells Ethan what Ahmed had told him and come to HQ imme-
diately. Ethan gets in his car and sees that the petrol was over. He didn't have cash
too. Devji comes out of his house from his garage he takes Ethan's old cycle. Ethan
takes the cycle and rides it till HQ. Ethan enters the HQ to see all staring at
Ethan. Ethan goes to Mohan and asks "What happened sir?, why are everyone staring at
me?". Mohan replies "CM is dead. I wanted to let you know that we had got a video ba-
sically cryptic stating that CM is going to die. He had a black mask on. Video
glitched. Why were you late". ( Ethan looks at the video) Ethan replies "My car was
out of fuel. I had no cash to refuel and hence, took my old cycle and came to HQ
which is 12km from my home. We can try tracing the sender's address". Mohan says "we
already tried that. No results". Ethan goes to the place where Ahmed was killed.
Ahmed was shot on head by the same guy in the video. Now not only the CBI but also
the police were under the pressure. Next day, Atm's cash was missing. Banks were
robbed overnight. Ethan understood that this is not a play of 4 people or 10 people.
Atleast a gang of 50 should have robbed the banks. While he was with the police at
the bank during investigation, he sees Venkat and Ashraf going down the street. Ethan
silently follows them. They reach at a small door near which Joseph and Xavier were
standing. They enter inside. Ethan silently slide into the room to see tha cash
robbed from the banks. Ethan shouts "I didn't expect this from you guys". Venkat says
"We have a Boss. Look there ( points towards devji)". Dev walks towards Ethan and
says "I want the tax repayment to happen to all. People's hard earned money going to
waste and politicians pocket is not good. No development in many places. We pay even
taxes for a small 10 rupee packet of juice to our 10-20 lakh salary. What we get in
return is nothing. Let them get the tax amount back and we shall give them back the
money. And about this cash from bank robbery, it is to increase the intensity and de-
crease the waiting period for tax returns". Ethan says "If we return now also, it is
possible to get the tax money dad!". Dev says "It is the misconceptions you have on
the political system. Once you give the cash back, not politicians even banks won't
look at your face to do tax repayment". Ethan says "This is wrong!". Dev says "You
learnt to be an ethical hacker but later changed paths to Cyber Crime Division of
CBI. I have people's email id and password with their trust. I had to break the
trust". Police slams opens the door of that room. They see Dev and Ethan along with
Joseph, Xavier, Venkat and Ashraf standing next to the piles of cash robbed from the
banks.
How police had come
When Ethan goes behind Venkat and Ashraf, A police was following him the whole time.
He recorded Dev and Ethan's conversation. Now, police asks to surrender. Dev looks at
Ethan and says "I have currently no idea to go to Jail". Dev whistles. Joseph drops a
sack of powder on the police. Police vision was blurred. They leave the cash there
and go to refugee. Next day all over news "The hackers responsible for Delhi's most
biggest cyber crime Ethan, the head of cyber crime division of CBI had his father
Dev, ex-businessman along with 4 hackers named Joseph, Xavier, Venkat and Ashraf with
the money robbed from banks. They have gone for hideout and police is on their
search". People start rioting for the scheme to be started faster as the economy was
coming down. In social media "#Bringbackjusticetogovernment after hearing the conver-
sation between Dev and Ethan, Dev was right. We need tax repayment back to us" this
statement goes viral. People start showing support to Dev. The deputy CM announces
the tax return scheme to begin in two days. Dev makes a video saying "World is devel-
oping faster. Technology is developing day by day. But Indian political system is not
evolving. It must evolve from a corrupt community to an organisation working for the
people not for their benefit. Yes! You heard it right! Government is a corrupt commu-
nity!. We have set an example using Ahmed, Chief minister of Delhi. Use the tax we
pay properly!. Develop India!. Government is not politics. Politicians make politics.
Before this goes to massacre, start the process! ( starts laughing) I didn't hack the
Bank accounts. And you don't have to search for me anywhere because I didn't do any
crime except the ATM robbery. And I have already given it back without even taking a
single rupee. You can check. I am in my home waiting for the police!". After seeing
this the public starts showing support. People gather together asking the police and
CBI to not arrest Dev as he was innocent. Ethan asks the CBI to raid his house and
catch Dev. Gets in the CBI car and reaches his house. Ethan takes a gun and enters
his house and asks the others to wait out side. Ethan walks to the living room where
Dev was sitting on the chair. Ethan closes the curtains and points gun at Dev.
Joseph, Xavier, Venkat and Ashraf walk inside the Living room to see Ethan pointing
gun at Dev. Dev looks at them and shoots all the bullets in the gun up, left, right,
down and rest randomly. CBI outside were in panic. Ethan looks at Dev, laughs and
says "What an acting! What an acting! What a plan. Today is the last day the tax re-
turns will be given. Start the redistribution of the money to all bank accounts
Joseph and team!". Joseph says "yes sir!". Ethan says "The CBI are only at the front
door. You guys leave from the back door jump the wall. I have kept cars ready". Dev ,
Joseph and team get in the car and leave. Ethan opens a gas cylinder. Ethan comes out
and asks the CBI to move back in hurry. The gas leaks and when it hits the flame of
the lighter, the gas cylinder blasts. Ethan's house is completely destroyed.
Everybody's phones start pinging. All had got their money back.
2 days later
Mohan says to Ethan "Ethan why are you leaving the CBI? The CBI needs you". Ethan
replies "My father is after all a robber, keeping this in mind, i can't continue and
it is not right even though he is dead now. I could not even complete my mission
properly. It is not right if i continue here". Ethan takes his resignation letter and
leaves. A CBI officer comes to mohan and says "SIR! who would be that hacker?". Mohan
replies saying "Whose ever plan it was, I hope it was not Ethan's plan". The officer
staying in confusion while mohan laughs and walks towards his cabin. Ethan drives to-
wards Ooty. In Ooty, his father Dev had disguised as a tea seller and opened a new
cafe or so called tea stall. Ethan enters Dev's house. Ashraf asks "I understand the
Bank account hacking and the plans made by you, Ethan. You were too great at acting.
Son is a greater Hacker who lead our team, and Father a great actor. But why was
Ahmed killed?". 4 years back, Ethan's wife worked under the Income tax Department.
Ahmed had many pending taxations. When she approached Ahmed, he threatened her and
eventually killed her. Since then he made a solid plan along with Joseph to finish
the game of Ahmed and bring back people's money back to them. When Dev got to know
about Ethan's plan he eventually joined them and finished the mission. After the ATM
robbery, Ethan knowingly brought the police behind him and create a drama using Dev
and increase suspicion on Dev rather tha Ethan. Ethan was the master mind, MegaMind
of the whole mission and the hackers and his dad Dev were just the puppets of his. He
asked the four hackers to go to Lucknow to avoid suspicious activity and their ac-
counts to be safe. In Lucknow the hacking in Delhi took place while Ethan was
Coordinating them around staying in Delhi using a laptop where the hackers made ap-
plication for voice call such that no call records are generated.
Few months later
Mohan arrives at Ooty for a family function when he sees Dev, Joseph, Xavier, Venkat
and Ashraf in the tea stall. Mohan understood they were a team. A man comes to take
Mohan's order. When mohan looks closely at the waiter, it was none other than, Ethan.
Mohan looks at Ethan and smiles. Mohan says "So, Ethan How is you new business?".
Ethan says "Nothing Going good sir, why are you here sir?". Mohan's and the rest of
the people in the tea stall's phone starts pinging. When they look at their phone,
their bank accounts had been hacked and their balance was gone. Mohan looks at Ethan.
Ethan says "Can we start this from first?". Mohan keeps his phone in his pocket and
says "Let the investigation begin again". Mohan looks at Ethan and winks.

Fortitude
Present Day, Bangalore
A Car being driven at high speed, looses control, hits the divider and crashes.
Ambulance Arrives, a female and Male is identified in the car and is taken to hospi-
tal. The police checks the car and it was owned by the female named Gayathri aged 26
and a wallet of the man named Ravi, aged 26 and a driving License of a man named Jay,
aged 28.
Few days ago
Ravi waits at a petrol bunk filling petrol in his bike. Suddenly a car pulls over and
a man shouts "Hey Ravi! How are you man?". Ravi replies "David! How are you?". After
filling the petrol, they go to a tea stall to speak. David asks "How is your school
time crush Gayathri?". Ravi replies "She is fine. She and I work at IBM!". David asks
"Didn't you propose her yet?". Ravi replies "She is a really good friend of mine! I
cannot express that to her!". David pats Ravi, due to a meeting David leaves. Ravi
goes to his office, Gayathri was sitting in front of her laptop. Ravi sits beside
her. Gayathri asks "Why were you late?". Ravi says "I met David, our classmate. We
stopped for a tea and dispersed!". Gayathri asks Ravi "I gave my car for service, you
have to drop me home after our shift". On their way back, they have dinner speak for
sometime about their work. Ravi drops Gayathri, before entering into her home,
Gayathri says "I want to say you something. I always share you everything and I don't
want to keep it a secret. I'll say you someday later!". Ravi shouts "Yay!!". Gayathri
is shocked and asks "You won a bet in my name?". Ravi says "No!". Gayathri asks "Then
why are you yelling?". Ravi manages the situation and goes back home. He is unable to
sleep that night thinking ways in which Gayathri will propose him. Next day, Gayathri
asks Ravi to take her to Cubbon Park. Gayathri walks in front of Ravi checking her
bag. Ravi thinks she is going to take out a ring to propose him. Suddenly Gayathri
takes out her phone and makes a phone call. Ravi day dreaming walks behind her.
Suddenly, Gayathri turns towards Ravi, Ravi stops and looks at her. Gayathri says "I
told you I wanted to say something, This is Jay!". Jay walks towards them and shakes
hands with Ravi. Gayathri says "I am dating him and some how, we are trying to con-
vince our parents. Can you help me?". Ravi is shocked, he sits on a bench, Gayathri
gives him some water, he drinks it and looks at Gayathri. Suddenly a man with a gun
shoots at them. Gayathri and Ravi move back and hide behind the bench. Jay pulls out
a gun from his back and shoots the goon. Ravi asks "Is he a police officer?".
Gayathri says "No! He is a gangster's son!". Ravi starts to sweat, he thinks to him-
self "If I don't help them, death confirm!". A man jumps at Jay to punch him. Jay
grabs his hand pulls out a knife from his pocket and stabs it onto the man's chest.
Jay says "It's all clear, come out guys!". Jay wipes the blood from the knife of
Ravi's shirt rudely says "We will go to Gayathri's home after watching a movie. You
have 3 hours to convince her parents!". Gayathri says "Give him some time!". Ravi
scared nods saying yes. Jay suddenly smiles and says "No need! He will convince them
within 3 hours!". Gayathri and Jay leave for a movie, Ravi takes his bike and leaves
to Gayathri's house. On his way he remembers.
15 years ago
David and Ravi sit beside eachother for the first day of their 6th standard class.
Gayathri was a new joinee and sits in front of Ravi and David. That afternoon, while
leaving back home, Ravi says to David "Bro, I guess I have a crush on Gayathri!".
David says "Then you should say her!". Ravi says "It's not the right age. I'll be
with her till my death!". Ravi tries to propose her many time, but couldn't say it to
her.
Few hours Before the Accident
Ravi reaches Gayathri's home. Chandran, Gayathri's father and Mother Rukmini Ask Ravi
to sit. Ravi says "I want to tell you something important!". Chandran says "No! No!
You need not say! I know you would have proposed to Gayathri, from many years I knew
you both were dating and Now you want to get married!". Ravi stops Chandran annoyed
and says "No Uncle! I'm not dating Gayathri, She is Dating Jay, Jay Prakash!".
Rukmini drops the plate she was taking and coming coffe for Ravi. Chandran asks "Jay
Prakash, Son of Prakash, that don?". Ravi nods saying yes. Chandran says "I cannot
give my daughter to a stranger and that too, son of a don!". Rukmini comes and says
"Would you give your sister, if you would have had one?". Ravi says "Jay saved my and
Gayathri's life after some Goons shot at us! He is a very good guy! Trust me!".
Chandran says "Many goons will be behind him, what if something happens to my daugh-
ter? He is not superman to save her all the time!". Ravi says "If he doesn't arrive,
I'll arrive for my friend! Just trust me!". After sometime Gayathri and Jay reach
home and comes inside. Gayathri opens the door, seeing everyone sitting seriously on
the sofa. Jay enters inside along with Gayathri keeping his hand on her shoulder.
Gayathri immediately push it out. Chandran asks "In front of how many people do you
want marriage?". Gayathri says "Around 500-1000 people!". Rukmini asks "How many peo-
ple do you want to complete your engagement?". Gayathri says "Me, Jay, Dad, Mom and
Ravi!". Ravi looks at her and shows a thumbs up and says quietly "Done!". Chandran
gets up and says "This bastard doesn't let me be serious also" and starts laughing.
Chandran asks Ravi to give their engagement rings as they exchange and complete their
engagement within their home. Chandran asks Ravi to take Gayathri's car and speak
with Prakash. Ravi sits on the driver seat and Gayathri arrives and says "I'll
drive!". Ravi gets out, he knew Only Gayathri drew her car and she didn't allow any-
one else. Jay says he'll drive but Gayathri was adamant. Jay meets Prakash and speaks
with him regarding this. Once again, in front of Prakash they exchange their rings.
One of the gang member goes near Ravi and asks "You're her bestie? If you are then.."
and shows a knife. Ravi says "No! I'm her childhood friend".
Present day
Jay and Gayathri bid goodbye to Prakash and get into their car. It had become dark.
On their way Jay says to Ravi and Gayathri "Shall we go to a fancy restaurant or
club?". Ravi says "You both enjoy, drop me in the side of the road, I'll take an
auto!". Gayathri stops in the side, Ravi gets out. Jay and Gayathri start moving.
Ravi checks his pocket and remembers he kept his wallet in the car. The car hadn't
gone far. Suddenly a shooting sound is heard. Ravi turns, the bullet hits the car
tyre and it tumbles. Ravi shouts "No!" And runs towards the car. Few people we're ap-
proaching the car with guns, but when the find Ravi running towards the car, they
move back. Ravi reaches the car and tries to open the door, but it was jammed. Tears
start dripping from his face. Ravi calls the ambulance. Ravi removes his shoe, which
was a boot and had a hard tip. He hits the glass window continuously. After continu-
ous try, the window breaks and Ravi opens the door and takes out Gayathri and Jay.
Jay in subconscious says "I don't know to cry or plead. But, Don't say Gayathri was
driving! Say it was me!". The ambulance arrives and they are taken to the hospital.
The police finds Jay's driving license, Car in the name of Gayathri and Ravi's wal-
let. Ravi says what all had happend and to save Gayathri says "After they left me
here, Jay sat in the driver seat and suddenly, someone shot the tyre and approached
the car with a gun but, when they saw me the went back!". Ravi then calls Chandran,
Rukmini and Prakash to the hospital. Prakash arrives at the hospital and asks Ravi
what had happened, after listening about the gun shot and people. Prakash says to
Ravi "It must be the work of my rival Aditya Shekhar!". Prakash calls his men and or-
ders them to find Aditya and kill his men who are responsible for the accident. The
doctor comes out and says "The Patient Named Jay is fine, but the girl, Gayathri has
a glas shard in her kidney which has caused infections. We need to find a kidney
donor immediately!". Chandran says "you can check mine, but I have drank some alco-
hol!". Rukmini didn't speak anything, Chandran goes to speak with her about donating
her kidney, but Ravi goes to the doctor and asks to check if his kidney would work.
Tests are done and Ravi's kidney was perfect for Gayathri. The doctor prepares for
the procedure and asks Ravi to sign the sheet. Ravi signs it and is taken to the op-
eration room. Ravi's kidneys are surgically removed and placed in Gayathri.
[Interval]
Few days later
Gayathri couldn't walk after the accident. Gayathri asks Rukmini "what happened to
me, why are there stitches on my back?". Rukmini says "Your kidney was trans-
planted!". Gayathri asks "Whose kidney? Dad's?". Rukmini says "No! It was Ravi!".
Gayathri insists on meeting Ravi. Ravi was sleeping in his ward at the hospital.
Rukmini and Chandran request the doctor to make Gayathri meet Ravi and arrange for a
wheelchair. Gayathri meets Ravi, Ravi slowly gets up and asks "How are you?". Jay
didn't have much impact and survived with a scar and a small fracture on his collar
bone. Jay comes to the ward and says to Ravi "If you wouldn't have been there at that
time, I don't know if Gayathri and me were Alive!". Ravi says "I and Gayathri know
eachother for 15 years, studied together and work together! She's my best friend! If
I wouldn't save her, who else will?". Jay hugs Ravi, Ravi moves forward, Gayathri too
joins but just keeps her hand on their back. After a week, they are discharged. The
police finds out that the attack was infact done by Aditya Shekhar and Gang. The po-
lice go to prakash's house to say Jay about the culprit. When the polic says about
Aditya, Jay says "We don't have any case against anyone!". The police agree and leave
back. Jay goes to enter his car when Prakash asks "Where are you going?". Jay says
"I'm going to kill Aditya!". Prakash says "Go and come son! Any legal issue, I'll
deal it for you!". Meanwhile, Ravi gets to know about Aditya Shekhar. Aditya Shekhar
gets to know that Jay has got to know he was behind the accident and takes some of
his men with him to kill Gayathri. Ravi follows Aditya, and is shocked to see them go
to Gayathri's house. Ravi puts his bike aside and jumps the compound wall and enters
into Gayathri's house. He asks Gayathri, Chandran and Rukmini to stay inside a room
and locks it from outside. Aditya knocks the door, Ravi slowly opens the door. It's
starts to rain outside heavily with thunder. Aditya's men take out their guns. One of
them in the front points the gun at Ravi. Ravi kicks him, grabs the gun and randomly
shoots at the men killing a few until the bullets get over. Aditya hides behind the
sofa. A man takes a knife and throws it at Ravi. Ravi dodges it and it gets stuck on
the wall. Ravi takes out the knife and runs towards the men. He randomly starts mov-
ing his hand stabbing many of the people. A man with a rusted knife stabs Ravi.
Aditya takes out his gun and points at Ravi. Aditya says "Keep the knife down and sit
on your knees!". Ravi sits on his knees, takes out a gun from the body at shoots at
Aditya's hand. He shoots as many as people possible and walks to Aditya and says
"Your Rivalry is Between Prakash and not his son or his son's fiancee! You kill
prakash! I don't care! If anything happens to anyone else, your one hand is gone,
your whole head will blast and shatter next time! Understood?". Aditya nods saying
yes. Before Aditya left the house, Ravi shouts "Take your men's body and clean the
house!". Aditya orders few of his men who were slightly injures from the knife to
take the bodies and clean the room. Once they had cleaned it, Ravi opens the door
letting out Gayathri and family. Jay goes to Aditya's place. Aditya with a bandage on
his hands walks towards Jay. Jay asks "I know you are the person who caused the acci-
dent! But what happened to your hand?". Aditya says "I'm sorry for the accident, I
won't come for you again! I'll only deal with your father from now on!". Jay was
amused with what Aditya said and asks "Why a sudden mind change?". Jay says what hap-
pened to him when he had gone to Gayathri's house. Jay says "He is truly a good guy,
that's why you are alive!". Jay tries to find who was the man who beat them up, at
first he thought it might be Ravi, but he also remembered that he hid behind the
bench during the shootout in Cubbon Park. A few days later, Ravi goes to a doctor af-
ter the man had stabbed him with a rusted knife. The doctor says "Your kidney is not
growing back again. Infections have been formed near the place we took out your kid-
ney from!". Ravi says "Is this serious doctor?". The doctor says "50-50 we cannot as-
sure you! We can try medications to reduce it. If it doesn't work, you have a very
less time to live if the infections pass over to your internal organs. If we try to
surgically remove it again, your death is sure!". The doctor prescribes Ravi few
medicines to reduce the infection. Gayathri kept trying to walk, slowly she starts to
walk with a stick. A month later, Gayathri starts to walk and run, bringing her life
back to normalcy. Prakash comes to Gayathri's house. Prakash says to Chandran "Let's
keep their marriage next month!". Chandran agrees and fix the marriage. Meanwhile,
Aditya plans to kill Prakash in the coming days. Gayathri calls Ravi and says happily
"Because of you, My marriage is fixed! Next month! I'm inviting you as the first per-
son!". During this call, Ravi was at the hospital. Ravi says "Sure! I'll be there!".
After cutting the call, the doctor says "The medicines are not reacting, you have
very less time to live!". Ravi says "I just want to live one more month, see my
friend Gayathri's marriage!".
Full-fledged Invitations start. Gayathri asks Ravi to call all of their school and
college mates for her marriage. Ravi goes to David's home to call him. David thinks
he is the groom and asks "When did you propose her?". Ravi says "I didn't, Gayathri
is marrying Prakash's son Jay!". David says "Don't you have any feelings about it?".
Ravi says "She is my best friend dude!". Suddenly Ravi vomits blood, David takes his
phone to call an ambulance but is stopped by Ravi. Ravi says the condition he is hav-
ing. David asks "Does Gayathri know about your condition?". Ravi says "No! I have a
very few days to live! I just want to stay until her marriage!". David asks "How are
you living with this pain?". Ravi asks "The kidney one or Gayathri one?". David says
Gayathri one. Ravi says "My life was just to matchmake them I guess!".
Marriage Day
Everyone arrive at the marriage. Jay goes knot on Gayathri. David also comes with his
family and their batch take photos of them in their marriage. Aditya, alone arrives
at the marriage. He takes out a gun and shoots Prakash. Jay removes the garland from
his neck and runs to Prakash. The bullet had hit Prakash's arm. Jay gets angry and
removes the buttons of his tuxedo to beat Aditya. Ravi stops him and says "It's your
marriage!". Ravi says to Aditya "I guess, What I told you didn't come to your hearing
properly!". Aditya shoots at Ravi, but Ravi takes a cover under a sofa. Ravi jumps
and punches Aditya. Aditya shouts in pain and kicks Ravi. Ravi falls down, Prakash's
men arrive with guns. Ravi runs and grabs a gun from the men and shoots Aditya point-
blank. A doctor who was attending the party, remove the bullet from Prakash's hand
and bandages it. Ravi goes to the alcohol section and starts drinking continuously.
Fully drunk, Ravi starts to dance. Between the Dance, Ravi vomits blood and falls
down. The doctor checks his pulse and finds out, Ravi was dead. Jay runs upto Ravi
and shouts "Brother wake up! Wake up!". David says to Gayathri "After that accident,
he had an infection the kidney site. The doctor told he is going to live only for a
few days!". Tears start dripping from her face. Gayathri says to David "We share ev-
erything! Why didn't he tell me this!". David says "What do you know about him?".
Gayathri is wakes up. David says "He beat up few guys in the school time who made fun
of you! Do you know that?". Gayathri says "He told me, David- you beat them up!".
David says "No! He always had a crush on you and never could propose to you! More
than the infection, your marriage hurt him!". Gayathri starts to cry, hugs Ravi. Jay
says "He must have actually married you, He threatened Aditya that day and today he
fought alone for you!". Tears start to drip from his eyes too. Prakash was shocked,
he had never seen Jay cry after a certain age. Chandran says "The day he told, you
both were dating, we always wanted Ravi to be your groom. But he told, Even if Jay is
a don's son, he is great from heart!". Everyone in the marriage mourn at Ravi.
Few Years later
Jay and Gayathri are living a happy life. They have a son named Ajay. Ajay asks Jay
"Dad, Who is that in the photo?", pointing at Ravi's photo hanging on their living
room wall. Jay says "It's your mom's friend. If he wasn't there me and your mom
weren't alive today and you wouldn't have born too!". Gayathri burns a lamp in front
of his photo showing they will remember him forever.
The End

GONE WRONG KALYANAM
Chethan Raj, a 27 year old software engineer at IBM in Bangalore, stands tall at 6
feet. He is the son of Raj and Reema. In the same city, Priya Mohan, a 24 year old
professional working at HP, stands at an impressive 5 feet 9 inches. She is the
daughter of Mohan and Meena. Chethan and Priya met two years ago on a flight to
Mumbai. Coincidentally, they stayed at the same hotel. Both had meetings at the HP
office in Mumbai. Chethan was there for taking in HP computers as their client hard-
ware for IBM, and Priya was there to discuss transferring technical operations to
Bangalore. While leaving to Bangalore, both were in the same flight sitting beside
eachother. After Landing in Bangalore, both exchanged their numbers as their Love
Blossomed. Current Day, Chethan messaging Priya "My Parents are looking for a bride
for me. I can't tell them I have a girlfriend, they are Old people with old mental-
ity". Priya replies "Same here, They have started looking for a groom for me too!".
Chethan comes up with an Idea "We will do one thing, we both will make a profile in a
matrimony app and make this as an arranged marriage. We can add similar personalities
and it will match us directly!". Priya agrees to this Idea. Chethan Finally replies
"I Love You!". Next day both make a profile in matrimony app. Chethan and Priya dis-
cuss and add similar personality traits. Priya's and Chethan's parents feel happy for
them to take their marriage initiative by themselves. Both the parents stumble upon
eachother's profile. Chethan and Priya are matched and have planned for initial meet-
ing in 2 days. Chethan had a younger brother named Shiva Raj, aged 21. Chethan was
speaking to Priya midnight when Shiva enters into Chethan's room. Chethan shouts
"What are you doing in my room this midnight?". Shiva replies "I was going to Drink
water when I heard noises from your room, that's why I came in to check". Chethan
replies angrily "Ok, now get out!". Shiva replies "You're speaking with a girl is
it?". Chethan replies "It's none of your business!". Shiva laughs closes the door and
leaves. Chethan tells Priya about his brother Shiva "He is a good boy, but sometimes
he a snitch!". Priya laughs and replies "I have told my sister about our matter and
she is full support". Priya's younger sister's name was Riya Mohan, aged 18. Priya
continues "Infact Riya is sleeping next to me listening to our conversation". Chethan
replies "If I tell my brother about this matter, the whole world would have got to
know about this in 2 days. Anyways we will meet in two days, see ya and Goodnight!".
Chethan cuts the call and sleeps dreaming about the meeting with Priya. Next day
morning, Raj comes into Chethan's room. Chethan was quite asleep when Raj wakes him
up and says "We have found a match for you, yesterday we forgot to tell you. Tomorrow
we are going to meet the girl". Chethan replies "Ok! Now let me sleep, I hardly get
two days for holiday. By the way, when are we going tomorrow?". Reema enters into the
room and says "Around 11am, take have a tea and wake up". Chethan wakes up, takes a
bath and takes keys of his Bike and leaves out. On his way, he picks Priya and go to
a shopping mall. On their way back home, they are stuck in a traffic. Priya looks to
a car waiting for the signal next to them. Inside the car was Mohan and Meena,
Priya's parents. Priya and Chethan were wearing helmet. Priya informs Chethan that
her parents are in the car beside them. Chethan asks Priya to get down from the bike
and walk for a distance. Chethan would come and pick her up after the signal from
there. After the signal started, chethan picks Priya and decide to go through the
longer route to home. On their way, they stop at another signal. Beside them was an
auto inside which Shiva was with a girl. Chethan informs this to Priya. Priya looks
inside the auto and finds out that the girl was Priya's sister Riya. Priya tells
slowly to Chethan "Your brother is with my sister!". Chethan head started turning. He
opens his helmet and looks onto Shiva's face. Shiva was speaking with Riya when he
suddenly looked at Chethan. As he saw, he started to sweat. Riya asks "Why are you
sweating so much?". Shiva replies "Look back, he is my brother!". Riya looks back and
finds Priya sitting behind her and replies to Shiva "The girl sitting behind him is
my sister!". Shiva pays the auto driver and comes out of the Auto. Chethan stops his
bike in the side and four of them Priya, Chethan, Riya and Shiva stood on the foot-
path. Chethan asks Shiva Tauntingly "You started so early?". Shiva replies "We both
study in the same engineering College!". Priya asks Riya "You could have told me
about this, when I told you about mine!". Riya replies "We are just Dating since a
year!". Chethan looks at Shiva and asks "A year!". Shiva replies "You're speaking
about me, what about you, you have arranged a meeting with a girl tomorrow and you
don't have shame agreeing for that?". Priya tells to Shiva "Brother, I am that girl,
we are dating for 2 years!". Shiva laughs from inside and replies "2 years brother?".
Chethan tells to everyone "Let's end the discussion now! And Shiva, you better don't
tell anyone about this!". Shiva agrees and tells to Riya and Priya "Well we'll meet
tomorrow! Bye!". Priya and Riya Catch an auto whereas Chethan Takes Shiva home in his
bike. When chethan and Shiva reach home Raj sitting outside asks "When did you both
brothers become so close? Chethan started picking his brother from college?". To
which chethan replies "No dad, I saw him on my way back and picked him up, why waste
money on auto?". Raj replies "Auto cost is less than petrol cost. Don't forget
that!". When Priya and Riya reach home Meena asks "Riya did you cut class and go to
mall with your sister?". Riya replies "No mom! She called me and said she will pick
me from college and picked up me later". Priya and Riya go to their room.
Next Day, Chethan and his family arrive at Priya's home for the initial meeting.
Mohan starts to boast about his daughter. Raj starts to boast about his son even
more. They start telling about each other's higher designations and offers for going
abroad. Finally Meena tells "Let the Boy and Girl go talk alone". Suddenly Riya and
Shiva stand up. They forgot they were talking about Priya and Chethan. Reema asks
"Why are you both standing?". Shiva replies "I wanted to get some water". Riya tells
"I was going to get him water". Reema replies to both "When did you ask for water
Shiva?". Shiva doesn't replies and they both sit down with shyness. Priya and Chethan
go inside a room. Priya tells to chethan "Your plan worked!". Chethan replies "I
don't know why our parents are boasting about us so much!". Priya agrees and tells
"Now they will ask us about our decision and we have to agree before which they have
to agree!". Both come out of the room. Reema says "We will let you know our decision
through phone". Chethan and family leave out. Shiva looks at Riya and shows his hand
in sign language to call him later. On their way back home Chethan asks Raj "Dad, why
did you boast about me so much?". Raj replies "If you want a bride, you must boast
about the groom!". Reema says "Same way you married me by boasting and didn't have

--- Joe.pdf ---

Joe
Somewhere in USA
It's a Christmas eve and the street was lit up with light. A man wearing a black
hoodie walks down the street. Snow flakes falling on his shoulders. Another man walk-
ing on the street bumps on him and an id with the name 'Joe' flashes, both apologise
and leave. Joe turns and police arrived at the scene pointing gun at him. Joe pulls
out his gun from his pocket. Heavy storm suddenly hits and the hoodie on his head is
removed and a flood light flashes on his face, showing a huge deep scar on his nose.
His beard made him look rugged and his medium short hair made him look like a lumber
jack. The snow starts to fall heavily as the storm started speeding up. Joe was un-
able to open his eyes clearly, but tries to aim his gun forward covers his eyes and
shoots.
INDIA, 15 years ago
Joe aged 17, standing still at his father's funeral. His sister runs out from a car
crying and falls on her father's feet. Joe's sister's name was Jennifer. Joe's mother
gets a stroke suddenly. Joe takes asks the ambulance driver "I'll pay you the cash
you want, take my mother to the best hospital around here!". By the time people lift
his mother and keep her in the ambulance, she was dead. Their relatives ask Jennifer
"Who is going to take care of Joe?". Jennifer replies "Me, my husband Harry and Joe
live in USA, Joe is studying there! He just came here for his holidays!". Harry cuts
the conversation and says "We can discuss this after the funeral!". Few days after
the funeral, a lawyer arrives at their house. Harry and the lawyer along with
Jennifer have a deep discussion and after some time calls Joe. The lawyer ask Joe
"Your sister wants to buy the family property, you will get as your heirloom. If your
willing to only! She has to pay your school and college fees in future, so it will be
helpful for you!". Joe replies "I'm 17 right now! In India, for any sale or rent, I
must be 18 right?". The lawyer agrees, and Joe continues "Then! I'll be 18 next
month, after that I'll let you know my decision!". Lawyer shakes hands with the boy
and walks to his car, calls Harry towards him and says "Next month, after the things
are done, don't forget my share of 60 Lakhs.
Next month, On Joe's 18 birthday evening, the lawyer arrives at their place. Harry
and the lawyer have a drink and call Joe. Joe says "What is your decision?". Joe
replies "Sir! My decision was clear on the day you asked me! I was a minor that day
and cannot speak to you in that manner. But today, I'd like to say to you that, keep
your 60 Lakhs of share deal away from me!". Jennifer cuts the conversation and says
"I'm just saying this for your benefit! I'll take care of you with that money!". Joe
replies "You haven't taken care of me when we were in the same house at USA and
should I expect you to take care of me after so much has happened?". Jennifer slaps
Joe and says "how could you speak to me like this!". Lawyer whispers to Harry "You
have to do that now!". Harry grabs Joe's hand and takes him into a room and locks the
door. Harry removes a sharp edged bracelet from his hand. Joe looks into Harry's
eyes. Harry keeps it on his knuckles and starts to punch Joe on his face. Joe com-
pletely defence less. Harry kept shouting again and again "You should have listened
to us!". After 15 minutes, Harry comes out of the room. Puts back his bracelet on
filled with blood. Harry's face covered in splashes of blood. Harry sets his hair and
says to the lawyer "He has agreed!". Joe walks to them, a huge deep cut on his nose,
his eyes red and face covered in blood. Harry says "I have a meeting at a hotel to-
day, I'll come as early as possible!". Harry gets into his car and leaves. The Lawyer
shows Joe two papers to sign and says "One is for getting your heirloom and the other
is the transfer of properties!". Joe goes towards the first paper and signs. The
Lawyer says "This one too!". Joe reads the document and looks at the lawyer and
Jennifer's face. Grips the pen his hand tightly and stabs the lawyer on his neck.
Pull out the pen and turns to Jennifer. Joe says "I saw you as my sister and you saw
me as an outsider. You tried to kill our father and eventually killing my mother
too!". Joe stabs Jennifer in her stomach and neck. The Lawyer and Jennifer start suf-
focating and eventually die. Joe checks if they are dead, tears the second document
and runs out of the house. After some hours, Harry arrive at the house, gets out of
his car. Walks inside to see, streams of blood flowing through the floor, jennifer
and the lawyer were killed. Harry reports it to the police and the police start to
find Joe. By that time, Joe had fled the country, according to the recordings of the
CCTV from the Airport.
15 Years Later
John, a DSP in India, special squad is assigned to find the serial murders that took
place all over Kerala, in the recent weeks. John briefs his case and the success of
it. Once it is over, John goes to the IG and says "Sir, Since our case is over, are
we going to Dissolve the team now?". IG says "I heard you are very interested in
finding murder cases! I have a very old case of mine. It is one of my oldest unsolved
case, when I was in your post 15 years ago". John says "15 years ago? How can you ex-
pect me to find the culprits after so many years and loss of evidence?". The IG
replies "I have a diary filled with the evidence, and details of the case with im-
ages. I am giving your team a leave for 45 days. In that you can do whatever you
want. But I want you to find atleast 1 clue that will be helping me to satisfy my-
self. I want you to finish atleast one case from this diary". John says "Sure sir!".
IG says "I would like a good news before my retirement next month!". John replies
reading the book "I'll start with the first case of the murder of a lawyer named
Jacob". IG says "Go on!". John had 4 members in his team Raj, Smith, Sam and Luna.
The first investigation was held in 2009, September. Since, digitalization had began
during that period, they searched for old and famous hotels and places which could
have a CCTV camera during that time, near to the crime scene. According to Post
mortem reports, Jacob's stomach consisted of iron substances which was pulled out us-
ing a magnet causing to his instant death. Luna goes to the crime scene which was a
house in ruins after the murder. They try to find the owner of the house. Smith in-
vestigates the details regarding that and finds out that, in September 2009, the
property was inherited to a person named Harry. During further investigation Raj,
gets to know that there were multiple disputes for the ownership change. Instead of
the original inheritors of the owner, who had a son and a daughter, the property was
inherited to the son in law of the owner. This property was auctioned for a cheap
price in the year 2013. John asks Luna to search for the owner's children, the son
and the daughter. Luna searches and gets to know their names were Joe and Jennifer
and Jennifer's husband was Harry. John asks "Where are they right now?". Luna replies
"Joe left to USA in September 2009. Jennifer was reported missing in October 2009 by
Harry". Joe says "Our primary suspect is Harry! Where is he?". Raj says "Harry is
dead!". John asks "What? When?". Sam replies "December 2009, In USA! He was killed
too!". John asks "Is Joe alive? What about jennifer?". Smith says "Joe's current de-
tails are not available. Jennifer was found dead in November 2009". Sam asks "Why are
you searching about them leaving our case about the lawyer Jacob?". Luna replies
"He's on the right track. In September 2009, Joe's father and mother died, Joe left
to USA, Harry inherited the properties and Jacob was murdered. Jennifer was reported
missing in October 2009 and Harry was killed in December 2009. Joe's current details
are not available". John replies "You're right, this makes a full circle. Either Joe
is the culprit or There is a man playing behind this whole family!". Raj suddenly
says "Sir, Jacob was the legal advisor for Harry and Joe's Father! And Sir, Harry has
a son, Peter".
In USA
Joe in a formal attire walking into the board room says "Let's start from the
scratch!".
[Interval]
USA
A 16 year old boy, getting driven to his school. While crossing the road, a car hits

photo. Joe looks at this photo and says "This is something, I don't like to remem-
ber!". John says "We came searching Peter, but didn't expect to see you here, after

fugitive! But I assure you that this investigation is not for arresting you!". Joe

pect me to do at that time?". John replies "I know about that, but why did you kill
Harry?".
USA, DECEMBER 2009
Harry secretly cremates, Jennifer's body and files a case she is missing. Before
that, Harry adds iron particles into Jacob's body, manipulating evidence. After a
month, Jennifer was reported missing. Eventually, Joe was considered a fugitive in
India. Harry and Jennifer had a son named Peter, whom they didn't bring to India,
when Joe's father died. Harry once reaching USA, starts to hunt Joe. Harry was the
Chairman of 'Harry Corp'. Using his authoritative power, he manipulates people and
goes to Joe's Hostel. He beats up people of the hostel and his college mates.
Finally, one day, he finds Joe in a subway. Joe was taken to the Harry Corp's head-
quarters. Harry says "sign it!", showing the document, which Joe had torn that day.
Joe refuses, Harry tie up Joe on a rope and starts beating him. Joe starts to spit

Later, all the assets was to be given to Peter and temporarily, given to the

Present day
John listens to this and says "You became the legal guardian of peter, for Harry's

the manager. Peter gets shocked and faints. The manager shouts in pain, tries to get

body? Huh?". The manager says "I have learnt value of a family from him! If he wasn't
there, I would have been no where!". Before the manager could say anything further,

being chased by John. John asks the local police for support.
It had started to snow, Joe gets down from his car and enters into a shop. It was the

his clothes. His ID was hanging in his pang, which he didn't notice. Snow flakes

Joe replies "I didn't see your rights when I took custody of him!". Haron says "I
never spoke to my brother after he left to USA! I didn't even know he had a son!".
John says "Sir! I'll not let you touch him! He is under my custody!". The local po-
lice surround them. Haron goes inside his car and takes an automatic rifle and starts
shooting the cops. Once, all the cops were down, he points the gun at John and says
"I have to do it!". Haron shoots John on his leg, keeps Joe at gun point and starts
beating him up. Haron stops when, Joe was exhausted and was soaked in blood. Haron
says "I kept you alive until, peter gets up and avenges the murderer of his parents".
Peter comes out of the car, Haron looks at him and says "You want to know who killed
your parents?". Peter nods saying 'yes'. Haron points at Joe. Joe looks at peter, pe-
ter looking into Joe's eyes. Peter in sign language asks "Who is this?". Joe says "He
is a bad man!". Haron asks "Why doesn't he speaks?". Joe says "He has speech-impair-
ment!". Haron says "Oh, so he is dumb!". Joe gets angry, he gets up and grabs the gun
in Haron's hand. Haron says "You were quiet, upto this time. What happened to you
suddenly?". Joe says "Why did you call him dumb?". Haron says "What else should I
call him?". Joe says "You should have called him that!". Haron says to Peter "He
killed your parents! Kill him!". Peter looks at Joe, then looks at Haron and nods his
head 'no'. Haron is shocked. Joe shoots Haron on his leg, then takes peter to his car
and makes him sit there. Haron says "Spare me!". Joe says "Too late Haron! You're

Few weeks later
Joe is standing in the USA court, for murder of Haron. The judge sentences "As an act

--- Karma On the Face of It.pdf ---

Karma: On The Face Of It
In News:"Many schools in Bangalore has recieved bomb threats in mails this Morning.
Police have reached the schools which have informed about the mail and is under con-
trol. According to the latest reports, A school was bombed and the students were
cleared from the building prior to the incident. Parents and teachers are in panic".
The school name is 'RJ public school' had recieved the mail but by the time they saw
the mail, it was too late. The road to the school was very narrowly built. The bomb
squad could not get their bus into the school premises. It would take them longer
time to get the machinery and come inside the school. The principal asks the teachers
to bring the students out of the campus building. A bomb blasts in the ground. A
Physics teacher named Dev Mohan asks the principal to take the students in the school
buses available and rest students inside a house nearby. By that time the Bomb squad
took the machinery and reached the place. Even Dev goes with the bomb squad to all
the corners of the school. There were 3 other bombs fitted in the school ground it-
self. 2 of them were diffused. The other one was going to blast. Dev calculates the
impact of the blast using the mass and size of the bomb and just as all the people
stand the distance at which Dev told them to the impact was nil. Due to the prior
bomb blast, there were few cracks on the school building which they patched up as
they gave the students 2 days of holiday due to the Bomb issue. Dev Mohan aka Physics
Mohan aka Dev sir, simply called Dev was the most celebrated teacher in the school.
All students liked him as he was ground to earth and taught using real life examples
rather than black board explanation. Even during the bomb blast time, the students in
the house nearby were having a experimental version of the chapter 'collisions', he
asked the bomb squad to let him to the experiment without harming or destroy anybody
or anything. Later He became a news all over social media as "The teacher who is
ready to do anything to teach his students". Few people took it in a good way, few
people started trolling him over social media "How can a teacher be so irresponsible
during a bomb threat while students are in danger?". The school didn't care about
these backlash on dev as they knew how good of a teacher he was. The police later
catches the criminal who had bombed the schools and rewarded the people who sent the
bomb threat mail for saving thousands of lives.
One day, A student from the school is taken home by his so called parents. Evening
the parents come into the School. The admin calls the class teacher who was Dev. The
parents say "My son Xavier has not reached home yet. We send him in the school bus.
It is already 5pm now". Dev interrupts and says "Sir, Xavier has gone home infact, We
got a receipt in which parents have come to pick up the child was given". The father
says "If we would have picked him up then why would we come here and ask you now. Our
second son already reached home, they both come together from school. You are the
same teacher who was blasting the bomb during the bomb threat in the school right?
How can a teacher and a school be se irresponsible for keeping such teachers and not
maintain safety standards for a student before doing security standard before letting
the parent who has come to pick a child". After hearing this, Dev ignores the comment
on the bomb blast matter and goes to the security department of the School and takes

The earliest form of the game that's now called chess can be dated back to
India in the sixth century. Like the modern game, this predecessor, called
chaturanga was played on an 8x8 grid and featured pieces generally similar to

drug war in the world is not going to end in the near future but it's our work to
catch them if found. Next day in the news Krishnamurthy sees "An end to the begin-
ning, the old mafia 'king' was dead few days back but according to the latest reports
a new King has arrived....... Along with......... A new Gold!". Krishnamurthy heads
towards the Headquarters. After immediate discussions Krishnamurthy and Mohan immedi-
ately head to Switzerland. According to Vedha's report they head to king's house.
Krishnamurthy and Mohan and welcomed inside by the guards. They both wait at the liv-
ing room for The new King and Gold to arrive. They are amused to see Shiva and
Diwakar still alive. Shiva Became the new King and Diwakar became the new Gold. (

vedha hold the bomb, before he could react the bomb blasts and Shiva goes to hiding.
During the gas blast Diwakar enters into the refrigerator helping him to survive the
blast while King Died) Krishnamurthy asks "So this doesn't end here?". Shiva replies
"The First Chapter of our story ended few days back. This is the beginning of the
Second chapter. The eradication of drugs for which you framed our beloved King and
Gold. We were the ones who gave the Attam gang and Ganesh gang jobs. We will see who
is going to win this game". Mohan tells "when are we starting the game?". Diwakar
replies "In the intricate web of conquest and domination, beginnings are the founda-
tion upon which empires rise. It is in the inception of our schemes that the seeds of
power are sown, and the path to supremacy is laid bare. While the world may celebrate
the pomp of the end, it is the cunning machinations of the start that truly shape our
reign. So, heed my words and grasp the significance of beginnings, for they hold the
key to unraveling the destiny that I, shall forge with iron will and unyielding
resolve".
The End

KING: THE TRIOLOGY
KING PART 1:SHIVA AND DIWAKAR
"India has been importing drugs for many reasons out of which 357 billion Indian ru-
