KING PART 2:GOLD
The earliest form of the game that's now called chess can be dated back to India in
the sixth century. Like the modern game, this predecessor, called chaturanga was
played on an 8x8 grid and featured pieces generally similar to those of modern chess.
The Game of Chess had just begun. One side was king whose face had been know by RAW
now. The other side is Gold. Gold was just another king in the game of Chess. Both
had the same power. Both did the same work. Both had similar positions between the
associates. Both had the Crime syndicate of Illegal drug dealings and Gold smuggling.
In the game of chess there are very few chances of the game becoming a draw. Only the
most powerful king wins. Winning is not killing the opponent but it is capturing the
opponent. The king who won the battle decides what happens to the opponent king. King
had a plan.
After asking the question king gives a pause and then replies "My name used to be
Vijay. But Vijay died on 2nd December 2007. That was the day king was born. To reach
this position...................... I don't want to waste your mood saying i did
hardwork and killed many gangsters for reaching this position but i will surely tell
that i killed many. Now it will be in your mind why i brought brought you here and am
i going to kill you. Your assumption is wrong" The window right behind king breaks. 4
men enter throught the window. King asks Diwakar to take the olympia rifle from the
cupboard. Diwakar throws it towards king. Diwakar gets a desert eagle will bullets
which he puts in his pocket and starts shooting the men. The men had G18. They were
continuously shooting and king and Diwakar. Both take cover using a table. King loads
the gun and head shots one man. The other 3 continuously shoot at the table. They
come near the table with their gun pointing towards the table. Diwakar takes his Gun
and shoots the 3 people to death. King and Diwakar come out of the room. Shiva was
trying to shoot more men coming inside through the door. They shoot all men leaving
one. King goes out. All of king's men who were for his security were dead. Only the
associates who were not in the compound were safe. King goes to the home of the dead
and give them money for the betterment and for their future. King after coming back
home tells Diwakar a story "I had a friend named Ajith. He had a family. We were an
associate to Prakash syndicate. They were the major drug lords at that time. Now they
are at the sky we can't touch. I was the one who added Ajith to this syndicate as an
associate. I didn't know that would cost his and his family's life. As i got caught
due to the largest drug trafficking in india the PM and court ordered to hang me to
death. As i got caught Ajith also was caught. We had a small fight in jail that his
family was going to starve because of me and the syndicate. The day of hanging came.
To save Ajith's family i replaced him and me with another people and they were
hanged. Ajith was missing after that. Ajith didn't know that i the one who saved him.
With the name of "Drug dealer's wife and children" unable to bear the pain of death
unknowing that he was not dead she does suicide. That's when i saw Ajith last. I
heard only one news after that. It was that Ajith was killed by Prakash. Ajith was
cut into 100's of pieces and thrown in different parts of the world. To take that re-
venge i left their syndicate and began my own syndicate and started to become a big-
ger syndicate but never able to cope up. That's when i got another Rival Gold. Like
Ajith and his family died because of me i don't want any other family to die because
of me". Shiva comes out and tells " The man we got has told that it was Gold's asso-
ciate who sent to kill king".

REQUITAL
A Night at a fancy restaurant, Robert looks at Ria and says "I DON'T WANT TO HIDE
THIS FROM YOU. I WAS IN JUVENILE WHEN I WAS 15 YEARS OLD. I HAD KILLED ONE GUY WHO
HAD TRIED TO KIDNAP MY FRIEND "MICHEAL" FROM SCHOOL! MY LIFE RESTARTED AFTER I BECAME
21!". Ria Holds Robert's hand and smiles.
15 years later, Ooty
Robert and Ria had married and have a daughter named "Tia" of age 10. Robert owned a
Tea and coffee estate along with a factory for processing. Robert takes Tia in his
Royal Enfield to school. Drops her and leaves for the factory. He loads a truck
filled with Dust tea for delivery, the next day and keeps the advance in the cash
counter. Evening takes his bike and goes to pick Tia from school and takes her home.
Next day, Early morning 6am, Robert's house door is knocked. Robert opens the door to
find a worker from a factory. The worker says "Sir, there was a robbery in our fac-
tory! One full load of Dust Tea and the cash from the counter is robbed!". Robert im-
mediately refreshes and leaves to the factory. Before, Robert could reach the fac-
tory, the police had been informed. Robert goes to the police station to give the
written statement regarding the robbery. The Sub-Inspector named "Rodrigo" enquires
"Did you lock the counter before leaving?". Robert answers "yes! I had written the
accounts and locked it! I remember!". Rodrigo then asks "Who knows that there was
cash in the counter?". Robert replies "All my workers know that I have kept the cash
in the counter as I keep the same, everyday!". Rodrigo says "I need to have a word
with your workers!". Robert and Rodrigo are yet to leave the station when Robert gets
a call from the place the dust tea should have been delivered. Robert picks the call
and the client says "Thank you for delivering it this fast! I had called your driver
yesterday night to deliver me the dust tea by 7am and he brought it in time". Robert
cuts the call and says to Rodrigo "The Dust Tea is delivered! But what about the
cash?". Rodrigo says "Anyway let's have a conversation with your workers". Robert and
Rodrigo upon reaching the factory ask the workers to assemble in front of them.
Rodrigo questions each one, one by one. Rodrigo then asks "Is anyone missing here?".
One of the worker shouts "The delivery driver is missing sir!". Rodrigo asks Robert
to call the driver. Robert tries to call him but doesn't pick the call. Rodrigo looks
at Robert and asks "Where is the key to the counter?". Robert says "It will be in the
jeans I wore yesterday! It's in my home!". Rodrigo says "Can you go and get the key?
Because, the robber has most probably made a duplicate as there are no marks of tam-
pering the lock!". Robert takes his bike and goes to his home. Meanwhile, the driver
named "Rahul" reaches the factory. Rodrigo enquires Rahul but he denies in seeing the
counter open while leaving for the delivery. Rodrigo finds that all the CCTV cameras
are off. Rodrigo asks Rahul "Who all have the access to the CCTV?". Rahul says "This
is a Wifi camera, it can only be controlled by Robert sir, there is only the option
to view all the CCTV camera from the office". Robert takes the key and comes to the
factory. Rodrigo asks Robert for his phone. Opens the CCTV camera app and on all the
cameras. Rodrigo asks Robert "Can I view the messages on your phone?". Robert accepts
on viewing the messages. Robert finds a message and says "I have found the robber!".
Rodrigo grabs Robert's collar and take him to custody. Robert asks "Why are you ar-
resting me?". Rodrigo says "I saw a message in your phone for paying the insurance
for your factory! You had off the CCTV and took the money as embezzlement and trying
to frame your workers for compensation amount! The Case charged on you is insurance
fraud and Embezzlement of funds". Robert says "I have not made any insurance claim! I
have the proof!". Rodrigo says "Your plan was to make an insurance fraud! Anyway
you're under arrest!". Rodrigo takes Robert to custody. Rodrigo asks the cyber cell
to check if there is any past cases in the name of "Robert Hauser". Robert looks at
Rodrigo and says "I am being framed!".
Meanwhile in the factory
The workers are confused on what had happened. Rahul says to the workers "Let me go
tell Ria madam about what has happened here today! She will be worried". Rahul takes
his bag from the delivery truck and takes his bike to a school. From his bag he takes
the money he stole from the counter and pays the fees for his son's education. The
previous day, Robert was looking at his phone when someone calls him outside his of-
fice. Robert keeps his phone open and comes outside. Rahul enters the office and off
all the CCTV inside the factory. He takes a clear picture of the key of the counter
and takes the measurements. Rahul then takes the image to create a 3D print of the
key with exact measurements. Makes a mould using the 3D print and melts iron and
pours into the mould making the duplicate of the key. Before leaving for delivery,
Rahul opens the counter and takes all the cash and leaves for delivery. Present time,
After leaving from school, Rahul goes to meet Ria and tells her that Robert was ar-
rested. Ria and Tia reach the police station. Rodrigo gets back a phone call from the
cyber cell, they tell "Sir, Nearly 25 years ago, Robert Hauser was in Juvenile for a
murder. I have sent you the details regarding the same". Rodrigo gets through the
file and goes to Robert "So, this is not your first time. A murder 25 years ago in
Bangalore and now, Robbery in Ooty?". Robert replies "I was sent to Juvenile 25 years
ago, but this time I am innocent!". Robert replies angrily "Do you think I look like
a fool? I have seen many people like you! I knew that we were connected through your
name. You were the person who murdered my father "David" 25 years ago". Robert is
shocked and says "I'm sorry for that but this is wrong!". Rodrigo says "I once came
to see you, for asking why you killed my father and you were a psychopath during that
time! And you called my father a 'kidnapper', I will make the people here call you a
'psychopath' like you were before. What will happen if I harm your wife and daughter
here?". Robert says "No! Don't do anything to them!". Rodrigo grabs Ria's hair and
pulls it. Robert in tough voice says "No! Leave her!". One of the constable looks at
Rodrigo's maniacal intent opens the door in which Robert was kept. Tia asks Rodrigo
to leave her mother but Rodrigo in turn slaps Tia. Robert comes out and lunches
Rodrigo. Rodrigo asks "Who let him outside!? If I find out that person, I kill him
with my own hands!". Robert's eyes teared grabs Tia and makes her to sit on a bench.
Rodrigo starts to slap Ria. Robert's face sweaty, breathing heavily and teary eyed
walks towards Rodrigo. From the wall grabs a heavy stick and starts to hit Rodrigo.
Rodrigo grabs another stick and runs towards Robert. Both hit eachother's stick and
Robert's stick breaks into two. Taking this chance Rodrigo starts to hit Robert on
his face using the stick. Robert's checks tear open with blood gushing out through
the tear and his nose. Rodrigo continuously kept on hitting Robert using the stick.
At one point of time, Robert hold the stick to avoid it hitting him. Both completely
tired decide to finish this fight. Rodrigo takes his service revolver and points it
on Robert. Robert kicks Rodrigo's leg making the revolver fall near Tia. Rodrigo gets
up and runs towards Robert. Rodrigo then kicks Robert down. Robert on falling kicks
back Rodrigo. Rodrigo gets up and sits on Robert's stomach. Rodrigo holds Robert's
hands using his legs. Rodrigo starts to squeeze and scratch Robert's face harshly.
Robert shouts in pain. Robert uses his knee to kick Rodrigo's back and helps himself
out of Rodrigo. Robert gets up and runs towards Tia and holds her in his arms.
Rodrigo runs towards Ria and starts to hold her hair and slap her and says "You sur-
render and I'll leave her!". Robert breathing heavily, tensed looks around and finds
the revolver fallen behind him. Robert takes the revolver and points at Rodrigo.
Rodrigo says "You murdered my father using a compass and a divider, not using a gun!
Stop doing this comedy and surrender!". Rodrigo continues slapping Ria. Robert closes
his eyes, still breathing heavily, Tia in his arms, removes the lock from the re-
volver. Opens his eyes and shoots. Rodrigo's three fingers from his right hand falls
down, blood dripping from his hand. Rodrigo shouts in pain. Robert shouts to Ria
"Run!". Rodrigo asks the police to call and ambulance and send an escort to Robert's
house. Robert takes a police car and drives to his home. The constable comes out of
the station and finds Rahul sitting outside weeping. The constable asks "What hap-
pened Rahul?". Rahul replies "Robert is my friend! I am not Rahul! I am Micheal!".
Robert reaches home and Rahul joins them there. Robert takes his car and drives out
along with Ria, Tia and Rahul, before the police could reach Robert's house.
Meanwhile, Rodrigo's hand is completely amputated.
[Interval]
Police start blocking all the exits leading out of Ooty. Rahul sits on the driver's
seat, makes Rahul and Family to hide inside the car. At the checkpost, the police
opens the door to check and finds large boxes kept on the seats and floor. The check-
post police asks "Do you have an ID for shifting?". Rahul takes his ID of the factory
and says "We have an important delivery today! My truck is sent for repair". The po-
lice then asks Rahul to leave. Inside these boxes were hiding Rahul and his family.
High alert had been sent all over Ooty. Robert asks Rahul "Why are you helping us?".
Rahul replies "I am Micheal, your childhood friend!". Robert shocked asks "Why are
you here! Working as a Driver? Your Father was very rich! And Why did you change your
name?". Rahul replies "After you were arrested, My father used all his money to get
you out! When that didn't happen due to your IED, they sent you to a psychiatrist and
the rest of the land and Houses were sold for that! So that you don't have an Issue.
My father fell in a debt trap and we couldn't repay it, this forced me to leave
Bangalore and to settle in ooty". Ria asks "IED? What's that?". Rahul replies "IED
for Intermittent explosive disorder, Robert had that and Rodrigo is having Bipolar
Disorder! You saw that Robert is calm due to the psychologist's treatment, but
Rodrigo is still having the same I believe. That's the reason Rodrigo called Robert a
psychopath". Ria asks "How do you know that about Rodrigo?". Rahul replies "Rodrigo
is Robert's cousin brother!". Ria shocked asks Robert "Why didn't you tell me about
IED and Rodrigo?". Robert replies "I felt like it was not that important!". Rahul
says "Ria, Rodrigo assaulted you and acted like a maniac because of his bipolar dis-

Silhouette
When humanity's faith in the divine waned, they turned to darker forces, and thus be-
gan the era of their own creation's tyranny.
2 years ago, there was a Riot in Bangalore for stopping that a man came, His name was
Henry Swedish. He was considered as an Illuminati, working in the shadows. Like the
shadows he was everywhere. Nobody saw him but He was the one who stopped the riot.
Rainy night in Bangalore, a street lit with a single lamp. A man running scared,
slips and falls down under the lamp. A man pulls out his sickle stabs the scared man
to death. The man with the sickle slowly walked down the street. Ram (Investigative
officer, CBI) aged around 40 6ft 4 inch tall, arrives at the crime scene and sends
the body for post mortem. The name of the victim was known to be Hung Lee. According
to the report, he was stabbed 3 times and one of stabs had reached the liver causing
his death. The doctor also exclaimed "The killer is not doing this for the first
time". DSP Shah and CBI analyst John, were also brought to the case and helped Ram.
John was working on Henry Swedish case. Ram goes through all the criminal records and
finds some cases having similar killing pattern. The primary suspect in all of them
was Mike, son of Gibson. Gibson was a drug mafia who involved in multiple human traf-
ficking cases and was arrested in the year 2020. In 2022, Gibson was found dead due
to overdose in amitriptyline, a drug used as antidepressant. After Gibson's death,
people thought Mike would take over Gibson's Empire but he didn't. Gibson's Empire
was taken over by Ron Jefferson, simply called Ron. He began double the drug distri-
bution and began to expand his empire. Mike, for not gaining the position he was sup-
posed to recieve started his own Mafia empire against Ron's. Only Ron and other few
people had seen Mike, There were no images of Mike but his name stood strong in all
other cases. According to insider information and reports, Gibson was killed by Shah.
Ram decides to go undercover to nab Mike. From the next day, Ram was finding ways to
enter into Mike's or Ron's underworld. Ram finds a friend of his Brent, working un-
dercover in Ron's Mafia empire. Ram starts to sell drug called fentanyl". One by one,
Ram establishes his status under Ron's Empire. Ram gets to know that Ron's main drug
deals are based on Morphine. Ram starts to sell Fentanyl within Ron's empire. Ron
didn't know about a business being held within his business. Soon, Ram befriends
Ron's syndicate members. Ram was then taken for drug deals, human trafficking and or-
gan trafficking. Ram overheard few people speaking about a drug deal going to be held
later this month. Ram takes his phone and calls to an unknown number and says
"India's biggest drug deal is on. Human trafficking from Mangalore port to Saudi.
Give me the orders". The voice on the phone said "Wait!". Next Day, Ram meets Ron in
Mangalore. Ron was 6ft, having medium long beard, wearing sunglasses and an overcoat.
Ron says to Ram "So you are the one who sells fentanyl. Brent told me about your
businesses. Would you like to partner with me?". The fentanyl Ram sold was from the
narcotic raids held in the country. The people whom Ram sold the drug was, his own
CBI colleagues. Ram shook hands with Ron and says "I sell Fentanyl, I would like to
know how much source of Morphine you're having". Ron replies "Isn't this too early
for me to give you answer for this question?". Ron laughs and says "I know you're
selling fentanyl to my members, I am staying quiet just because you can be a great
associate for me!". After saying this Ron walks off. Ram goes out, hides and calls
the same unknown number and says "Morphine!, According to the information, He has a
large amount of morphine!". The Voice on the other end replies "Wait!". Ron gets into
his helicopter. Ram gets into his car and starts to chase the helicopter. The heli-
copter stops in a harbour. Ron gets out and opens a container. The container was
filled with cash. Ram reaches the harbour, Hides and snaps the pictures of the con-
tainer and sends it to the unknown number. The number replied "Wait for further com-
mands!". The container is lifted and loaded into a ship and another container from
the ship is taken and brought in front of Ron. The container is opened and it was
filled with drugs. Ron asks a man to open another container in the dock. That con-
tainer had men, women and children. Ron asks them to load both the container to the
ship and enters his helicopter. As the helicopter moved, Ram ran towards the ship.
Enters into the ship. One of Ron's henchmen in the ship, finds Ram hiding behind a
container. He grabs a hammer and goes to hit Ram. Ram catches the Hammer, pulls the
man's hand and bangs the henchmen's head onto one of the containers. Another man runs
towards Ram. Ram slides, grabs the hammer and hits the man. The ship's captain starts
shooting. Ram hides behind a container. Pulls out his gun and headshots the captain.
Ram opens the container with the people in it being trafficked, Untie all of them.
The ship was in middle of the ocean and all four sides were covered with the blue
ocean. Ram enters into the hull. There were more henchmen there. A man punches Ram on
his face. Ram falls down unconscious. Ram wakes up, pushes the men, kicks one of
them. Jumps and pulls and axe in the corner. Takes the axe and starts to stab the men
one by one. He finds a compass with a man. Ram runs inside the bridge of the ship and
tilts the ship towards Mangalore port according to his calculations. He messaged the
number "On my way to Mangalore harbour". The number replied "More people to go!". At
first Ram couldn't understand. Then suddenly people start falling on the ship from a
helicopter. After everybody had entered the ship, the helicopter flew away. One man
enters the bridge. Ram grabs the man and throws him outside the ship through the win-
dow. Ram now understood what the message meant, more people were on their way to the

Ram runs towards the containers, the men had put the people behind transported
hostage at gunpoint. Ram catches a man using his axe, he stabs him. Ram surrenders to
the men. Suddenly a helicopter lands on the ship's helipad. Snipers come out of it

many times not to call me Sir!, Call me Mike!". It was infact Mike whom Ram was send-
ing messages in the name of unknown number. Ram replies "Ok Mike, those two contain-
ers are having cash and drugs, we need that!. Let's send these people back home in

formation about the information leak to police, not knowing the drugs isn't there in
the ship, he tries to stop it. He tries to call the people in the ship, but Nobody

CBI was shocked at the pathetic condition at which Brent was killed. The CBI assumed

the CBI and police go behind Ron, until then wait!".
[Interval]
During the "Great Riot of Bangalore", CBI had to intervene as the riot staged out of
scope for the police. Officer Ram's first mission began there. When it went out of

along with my guys, I am in the metro tunnel between Vidhan Soudha and Cubbon Park.

call is being recorded" makes a scream and cuts the call. Ron throws his phone down

men come near Ram and asks to remove the hoodie from his head for which Ram denies.
The man keeps his hand on Ram's head. Ram pulls the man and punches his face and
throws him on the window. Ron turns and asks his men to catch the man. Ram starts
running towards Ron. Ram punches a man and kicks his leg. Another man starts to shoot
at Ram. Ram pulls out his gun and shouts "Every one in the train!, Close your eyes!".
Ram headshots the man shooting at him. Ron gets scared and open the train with emer-
gency exit. Shah runs towards Ron. Ram gets out of the train. The driver starts to
drive the train. Ron stops and shouts to Ram "Open your hoodie and hit me after
that!". Ram remove the hoodie and the muffler. Ron looks at him and says "Ram? Why
are you doing this to me?". Ram replies "People whom you killed because of me were
your supporters, Your supporters have become against you and are joining Mike Gibson!
And I am an Undercover CBI agent". Ram headshots Ron and kills him. Ram turns towards
Shah. Shah tells "Mike Gibson? You are supporter of him?". Ram tells "Every action we
take ripples through the fabric of fate. You took a life, thinking yourself untouch-
able. But the universe seeks balance, and your arrogance has led us here. Justice is
not about restoring the past but ensuring a future where deeds do not go unpunished.
Your end is not brought by this bullet, but by the weight of your own sins. Remember
this as you face your reckoning. Actions have consequences, and today, the scales are
balanced". Shah asks "What did I do?". Ram replies "Killing my friend's Dad! Putting
him to struggle". Ram shoots Shah on head. Ram takes Shah's gun and shoots Ron. In
the Headquarters, he told "Me and Shah were discussing the case when Ron hijacked the
metro train. After a long shootout, when we went catching Ron, Shah was shot by Ron
and Shah shot Ron and I had to shoot Ron later. I tried to get Shah treatment but was
unsuccessful". Ram was being sent back for the undercover mission again, but Ram re-
fused and resigned his post from the CBI without providing necessary reports or de-
tails. Ram went to the river and took back the laptop and Destroyed it. Mike Gibson
was given back his father's empire. Ram sends a letter to Mike. Mike opens the letter

joined just 15 years back, in the CBI. Those 5 years were something different. I have

the palace. Suddenly from the sniper's walkie talkie, a gun shot is heard. John
shouts "I didn't ask you to shoot!". There was no reply. John runs back to the hotel
terrace and finds the waiters holding gun who had shot the snipers. John runs from
the waiters and comes out to look at the hotel board "HS" under that in very small
wordings "Henry Swedish". John runs along with his team inside the palace silently
through the first floor. Ram looks up and finds John running towards him. Ram runs
and pulls down a lever. The floor opened and Mafia bosses fell down on a cushion. And

STATE OF ANARCHY
“When the land of the Father of the Nation turns blind to truth and soaked in sin,
what power does the law have left?”.
India
Elections for the lok sabha had ended. The whole Country had this one question in
mind "Who will be our next prime minister?". There were two parties contesting in the
election DJI(Democratic and Justified Independence) party and MSP(Mitra Sena Party),
both parties usually have a clash. On the election day, DJI party wins. The DJI party
leader Azam in the press conference "I would like to announce the next Prime Minister
of India, Mr Victor Francis!". The whole country was shocked. Victor Francis became
an MP from a small constituency and it was the first time he was standing in an
Election. People start investigating who Victor actually was. Nobody could find any
information about him. MSP leader Faizan asks the news reporters to make false re-
ports on Victor. Finally the the day to pledge came. Pledging was going to be taken
in Gujarat in front of Sardar Vallabhai Patel statue. All over the news "Will it be a
beginning to a new India or a End! We will get to know about it sooner or later!".
Ahmedabad, Gujarat
CI Abraham was watching it all over the news. Abraham says to the constable"I still
have an unsolved case in the name of Victor Francis! If I bring it out, He will be in
danger!". The Constable Veer says "Then why not give a complaint to the election com-
mission?". Abraham replies "No! If we do that, he will come to take revenge on us and
that cycle will not end!". Veer nods and goes. Suddenly, Abraham gets a phone call "A
drug deal is taking place and the vehicle will reach Narol Checkpost today 11 pm".
Abraham closes the checkpost and checks all the vehicles passing through the check-
post from the surat port side entering Ahmedabad. Suddenly It starts to rain heavily,
all the vehicles start honking. A black car zoom past the checkpost from Ahmedabad
side going to Surat. The policemen had not barricades the other side. Abraham says
"Our police is as useless as a white pencil", gets inside his car and starts to chase
the black Car. The black car was going at an approximate speed of 160kmph. They had
to catch the vehicle before it reaches Bareja, since there are 3 diversions which
lead to Surat. Abraham chases the Car and finally makes the car visible in front of
him. Just before reaching Jetalpur, the black car was surrounded. The man in the
black car applies handbrake, the car was about to tumble, but it does a 360 and
stops. The man comes out of the car, raised up his arms and says "I surrender!".
Abraham opens the car's trunk and finds a bag with a lock. He asks the constable to
open the lock and goes towards the man and asks "What is your name?". The man replied
"Dominic George!". The constable shouts and Abraham goes towards him. To their shock
it had fentanyl, the most dangerous drug existing. Dominic runs inside his car,
starts it. But Abraham shoots the tyre and the car crashes. Suddenly, a strong gust
of wind blew towards Abraham along with a spotlight exactly facing Abraham. It was a
helicopter. The helicopter lands on the road and the PM of India Victor comes out of
the helicopter. Abraham salutes Victor. All the news channels arrive at the scene and
start capturing Abraham and Victor. Victor walks towards Abraham, Dominic comes out
of the car, hurt. Victor says to Abraham "Do you watch the news?". Abraham replies
"Yes Sir!". Victor replies "Then why is Dominic being arrested when there will be no
more police force in the country?". Abraham asks "What do you mean by that sir?". One
of the constable comes towards Abraham and says "Sir please watch this video!". In
the Video of a news channel Live "New Prime Minister Victor Takes pledge. As we told
sooner or later, we got it very much sooner! The first paper he signed was to remove
the police force! All the materials made, available will be free and India's Economy
is dipping towards 0. Dictator Rule Imposed! Democracy Dead!". Abraham looks at
Victor, Victor smiles and says "Now Get lost!". Abraham disappointed gets into the
car and leaves. A group of black cars come and Dominic enters inside it. Dominic is
taken and beaten up by Victor's men. After Sometime, Dominic was thrown on middle of
a highway.
The Poor and the Rich flock stores, take everything they need. The BPL people get
turned into APL. Everyone had what they needed and was available in the country.
India's stock market crashes to 0. Cash was considered just as a paper to the people.
People start constructing houses everywhere, removing a difference between the Rich
and the poor. Jails were closed, criminals released. The criminals thought "If every-
thing was to be given for free, why do crime?". Children started making paper boats
using the Indian currency and flowing it through the lakes and rivers. People start
walking happily, no worries that they are poor. Everyone stopped going to work.
People stayed home all the time and started getting lazy, just eating and sleeping at
the comfort of their house. The United Nations get to know about this issue going on
in India and calls upon the Interpol to start a covert operation in India. Interpol
chief Qadir calls Victor and says "What you are doing is wrong! You need to stop it
immediately!". Victor replies "I will stop it as soon as my mission is completed".
Victor cuts the call and leaves.
1 month later, PM's next press meet
People were overjoyed with what they had and they were giving full support to Victor.
Victor sits at the press meet and says "Did everyone get what they needed, when I
made everything in my country free?". People start shouting supporting Victor. Victor
comes forward and says "What I Imposed during my pledge will be reverted back and all
things will come back to normal. This was just an act to make even the poor have a
rich lifestyle. When you get things which are enough, you wouldn't need more! My
country is not poor anymore!". Abraham was watching the news, completely drunk.
Victor says in the meet "Police force will be called back! Lifestyle changes but our
country doesn't. Cash flow will remain the same!". People listening to the this run
outside, their kids playing with the cash and making paper boats. They snatch the
cash and starts to keep them safely again. People start flocking the companies they
used to work at. Many companies accepted to take them back and many rejected them and
started looking for new applicants. Abraham wears his uniform, gets into his car and
leaves to the police station. Dominic with his car, follows Abraham. Abraham com-
pletely drunk, drives towards the press meet. Abraham pushes the journalists and
walks onto the stage and says "I did a drug bust, you ruined it! What are you going
to do because I lost the criminal?". Abraham slaps Victor, enraged people pulls aside
Abraham and starts to beat him up. Victor looks at Abraham and says "I am the PM of
India for the next 5 years! How dare you slap me?". Dominic was standing near the
stage. Victor grabs a cleaver, all the camera's focusing on victor. Victor goes to
stab Abraham but suddenly Dominic goes in front and his shoulder is cut. Dominic
kicks Victor. Victor falls down. Dominic grabs Abraham, asks him to get into his car
and leaves. Dominic drives as fast as possible, even hurt. Abraham pulls the hand-
brake, the car does a 360 and stops facing Victor in the car standing in front of
them. Dominic and Abraham comes out of the car and walk towards Victor. People run
and rush behind Victor. No one standing behind Abraham and Dominic. The three of them
looking at eachother. Victor says "You're all alone in this Game!". Dominic says
"Your Support will reduce person by person! And I will show you how!". Victor turns
and the people come to attack Abraham and Dominic. Dominic and Abraham get inside the
car and locks the door. People fall onto the car and starts to scratch and open the
door. Victor gets into his car and leaves. Dominic holds the handbrake, turns the
car, holds the clutch, accelerates, leaves the handbrake and clutch. The car does a
360 and people on the car fall down. People still starts to attack the car. Dominic
accelerates moving forward, crushing and killing many people on the way. Dominic gets
a call from Victor "You told that you will take away my support one by one! But I
didn't expect you to kill and reduce my support!". Dominic says back "I am on my way!
Ready to kill many and to save many!". Abraham grabs the phone and tells "Till date I
decided not to get into the political loop! But now you forced me into it. We are on

Dominic was being treated by a doctor. Abraham slapping Victor had gone viral.

Abraham and team reach Bern, they call their ally Tobias Keller. Tobias says "This

route and Abraham turns towards Interlaken. Victor reaches half and an hour before

Party leader. Abraham reaches, and Mark shoots. The bullet hits Zayed. Victor grabs

earth". Stephen is arrested for murdering Victor and a charge sheet is filed on
Abraham for wrong dealing of ammunition.
Started from the land of the Father of the Nation — Gandhi, where truth was a weapon
and silence was strength, and ended in Switzerland, the land of serenity and neutral-
ity, where peace is not fought for but lived.
The End

The BBB
"I have seen the sunrise, sunshine and sunset. Today our sunsets but we will rise
again and Shine harder" says Manoj. Political science classroom filled with students
listening to their classmate Manoj eagerly. Manoj continues "Political science is all
about Rising and setting like a sun. My conversation ends here". The whole classroom
starts clapping. The Teacher appreciates Manoj saying "Each backbencher must be like
Manoj. He shows with his ability and not attitude". Manoj walks out and goes inside
the canteen. Few boys come inside the canteen in an angry face and stands in front of
Manoj. Manoj looks at them. The boys and Manoj burst out in laughter. Manoj tells
them "you know technology is developing day by day. We are getting full in our inter-
nals today. Thanks to AI Chats. I wore Bluetooth in my ear and our teacher didn't
find that too. Next is yours all the best!". Manoj, Varun, Kumar and Jay are the
backbenchers of 'EG college of Political Sciences'. They had one more member with
them previously who was rusticated from college for his behavioural actions. His name
was 'Xavier'. Xavier was considered as college don before he got rusticated. Now he
plays football for a local team. Manoj and his friends like to sleep during the
class, back answer the teacher and to go behind girls, if they didn't do that in a
day they come to college according to them they were not considered as a backbencher
then. The other students in the college kept the friends gang name as 'BBB- back-
bencher boys'. The college was situated in a town. All people in the college were lo-
cal to the area where the college was situated, so there were no hostels thankfully
for the college. If there were hostels the BBB would have made up a loss of nearly
20-30 lakhs for the college owner Mr.Rafi.
New academic year, The BBB had 1 year to pass the course and leave the college. The
New joined students were addicted to smoking, alcohol and Drugs. They had a new name
in the whole College 'DDD- Drug Dudes Democracy', their leader was so called Jacob
along with Dev, Joseph and Nakul. Jacob didn't like the BBB and The BBB's didn't like
the DDD because they had created their own democracy in the college. The first day
they arrive, Jacob goes to speak with BBB. Jacob says to Manoj "You are the BBB
should not involve in anything we do". The BBB's burst out laughter and Varun says
"BBB? What is that?". Jacob replies "You are the BBB's right the college people call
you with his name". Manoj stops Varun and says "Okay whatever you call us BBB or
something, why would we involve in what you are doing?, you think we don't have any
other work?". Manoj goes on and makes fun of Jacob. Jacob triggered come back
silently and tell the DDD's what Manoj had told him. Nakul asks the DDD's to plan for
a fight with the BBB's to take revenge on making fun of them. The BBB's never in-
volved in any fight after Xavier was rusticated. One evening when the college was
over, the DDD's call BBB's to a ground to play football. BBB's accept for a match and
arrive at the ground at 6pm. The match was 4v4, there was one goal keeper, one de-
fender and two forwards (one was acting defender too). The DDD's had brought a refree
too. The match start, mid match The DDD's start hitting the BBB's. Kumar never went
on fights was severely injured. Jay runs outside the ground and calls Xavier. Xavier
was on his way for football practice. Listening to what the DDD had done takes his
Bike and arrives at the ground with Jay. Xavier punches Jacob on his face. Kicks Dev
and threatens Nakul. Varun and Manoj starts to hit Joseph. The DDD's run for their
life. Xavier tells to Kumar "You called me from my football practice for this small
matter?". Manoj tells to Xavier "After you got rusticated from our college, we don't
have value in our campus. You never asked the principal sorry and take you back to
our college too". Xavier laughs and says "Past is Past, what was that AI quote
'Political science is all about Rising and setting like a sun' my political science
is like a sun setting in a moon". Xavier takes his bike and goes back to his practice
ground. On the way he remembers.
The day Xavier was rusticated
Xavier goes to the principal's office. He tells the principal Mr.Mohan "Sir, I need
TC". Principal shocked asks "Why do you want TC, why do you want to leave? You are
the proud Backbenchers of our college". Xavier replies "I want to do what I love, I
love playing football and want to become a football player. Thats why I want to drop
out". Principal replies "Ok I'll make it ready in a week". Xavier tells "Sir, I have
a request. As you know I am one of the 'Proud backbenchers of our college' just shout
you are rusticated as it will level up the backbencher in me. This is a request. Just
tell behavioural issue and I'll tell others the rest of the story". The principal
then shouts "You are rusticated! For behavioral issues" and winks at Xavier. Xavier
then tells his friends and teachers "The principal called me when I was passing
through his cabin. He told me as I am considered a backbencher I had to focus more on
scoring marks. I got angry because he called me a backbencher and it was like I am
not passing in any subject, my score though is average. I then shouted at the princi-
pal and he rusticated me". Everyone in the college believed this story.
Present
The DDD's decide to take revenge from Xavier and plan to hit him at his practice
ground. The DDD leave to the practice ground and when they reach there, there was a
local match taking place. Jacob goes and sits in a seat. Jacob shocked seeing
Xavier's performance starts to cheer up for their team. The BBB got to know DDD are
planning to hit Xavier. Suddenly in the match one forward player from Xavier's team
gets injured. There were no substitutes in Xavier's team due to budget constraints.
If they couldn't find a player, the match would be forfeited and Xavier's team would
be disqualified. Jacob gets up removes his shirt and runs towards the field. Manoj
runs to catch Jacob as he thought he might be going to start a fight. Running through
the crowd Jacob runs to Xavier and whispers something in his ears. Suddenly the com-
mentator announces "we have got a substitute for team 'Grey warriors' his name is
Jacob!". The whole crowd was shocked. Listening to this Manoj stopped chasing and
sits back in his seat. Jacob was an excellent forward player along with Xavier was a
midfielder. After a struggling score of 2-3 they come back to 4-5, there was only 10
minutes more for the match to end. Jacob finally scores a goal making draw of 3-3. 5
minutes was left for the match to end. As the match progressed, defending became
problematic for team 'Yellow winners'. Grey warriors struggled when Jacob was going
to score a goal at the last 2 min, the goal is blocked and the ball taken by yellow
winners. Yellow winners score a goal in the last 30 seconds and win the match. The
crowd cheered for Yellow winners. Jacob asks sorry to Xavier. Meanwhile, Nakul and
Manoj starts fighting in the crowd. Manoj stated that the fight was lost after taking

and drinking alcohol to focus in the game. The BBB and DDD join their hands for the

riors and in college they together were named as 'GFD- Great Football Dudes'. Next

[Interval]
Manoj asks Mohan "Sir, I understand you are our coach because I have seen some foot-

fact lied to you about the rustication and all was a made up story and I had TC and
not the rustication letter". On their way back home they find the DDD fallen in the
side of the road dead. They inform the police about this incident.
The police investigates and finds alcohol and drug content in their blood. Supposedly
they must have had suicidal tendency and jumped in front of a car together. On fur-
ther investigation they find out the fight between BBB and DDD and arrests Manoj.
Xavier tries to explain the police but the police arrests Xavier too. Both are ques-
tioned and sent back home. Varun and Jay come to the station and take Xavier and
Manoj back home. Xavier gets down at the field and asks them to go. Kumar was with
Mohan in the Field. Xavier takes breaks a bulb in anger and the bulb builds up fire
in the cloths and chairs in the field. Mohan and Kumar runs outside and asks Xavier
to come outside. Jay asks Varun and Manoj to stop seeing the fire in the field. Jay
takes his bike and goes to call the fire engine. The Fire was completely spread out.
Xavier stood in middle of the field safe unable to come outside. Varun understanding
Jay would take some time to come finds a water pump nearby connects the pipe with a
pressure head. And starts to reduce the fire. But was unable to stop it. Jay comes to
the field with fire engine and starts to extinguish the fire. Next day, Xavier was
arrested by the police charged for clearing evidence of the fight and the death of
DDD. Manoj tries to get bail for him by providing CCTV footage of the incident and
stating that Xavier had not done anything. Xavier was sent out on bail clear of
charges. Xavier missed 3 matches and the board had confusion whether to take back
Xavier into the team due to the ongoing cases. Xavier goes to the board and resigns
and ends his contract. Manoj suggests Xavier "Try reconsidering and completing your
degree. Atleast that will get you a job". Xavier joins back to EG college of
Political Sciences. The BBB abbreviation changed to 'Boring Backbencher Boys'. Varun
decides to make the whole team happy by adding their name in the college fest. Kumar,
Varun and Jay decide to train the team Mainly Xavier and Manoj. After few days of
preparation they were completely tired and didn't prepare for the last 2 days. On the
day of the fest morning behind the stage the BBB start practicing. Varun by mistake
hits a student while practicing. The student whose name was Ashok hits Varun. Varun
falls down on a box. Xavier apologises Ashok. Varun gets up and sees his pants having
a white powder in his back. They open the box to see drugs. Ashok asks them to leave
the box alone. Xavier tells Ashok "You know what happened to DDD and now you bring
these things again? You won't get this back now!". Ashok calls his friends and start
hitting BBB. Varun Takes the box and start to run around the college. Kumar takes the
wall banner and throws it on one student. Xavier punches Ashok and throws him to the
wall. Manoj catches one and throws him on the stage. The audience start thinking the

stage falls down. Jay takes his bike and calls the police and brings them to the cam-
pus. Xavier, Manoj, Kumar and Jay hand over Ashok to the police and gives them the

looking at those things. Now I don't feel guilty. Okay! Leave it. Next we are having
our dace right, let's prepare". They turn back and the see the stage completely de-
stroyed props broken the fest banner fallen down. The BBB call few people fix the
stage and continue the fest. After the fest they go to the canteen and begin to eat
as they were starving when the principal Mohan comes to Xavier and says "After you
left the team, we hardly won few matches because it was very tough to find a replace-
ment and you were out key midfield player. It's ok if you don't want to come but I
came to tell you that we need you!". Xavier declines the invitation and tells "I want
to get a degree and leave this town and look for a job!".
15 years later
Kumar qualifies upsc and is a collector now. He decides to call the BBB back to col-
lege for a reunion. After a long search he finds Manoj's number. Manoj was now a
philosopher and had multiple blogs. Varun had become a teacher and Xavier was un-
known. Jay infact had become a actor. The BBB try to find Xavier but could not find
him. They tried sending emails, mails and message to all the people he knows and
their addresses and no result. They decide to do the reunion without him. On the day
of reunion all were sad as they couldn't find Xavier. For their surprise Principal
Mohan too arrive at the reunion. Suddenly Manoj is called by someone. When Manoj goes
there he finds Xavier. Manoj hugs Xavier and says "We tried to find you for this re-
union. How did you get to know about this?". Xavier replies "My name is not Xavier
now, it's John Britto. Your mails were returned because of my name and my old mail id
no longer works. Mohan told me about this and I came. I am a football coach now. I
coach our state's football team". Manoj takes Xavier to the rest of the people. After
having a friendly chat. Manoj makes fun of Varun "You are a teacher now, a back-
bencher teacher" laughs. Varun replies "You too are not different you might be using
AI chat for your philosophy. Remember that 'I have seen the sunrise, sunshine and
sunset. Today our sunsets but we will rise again and Shine harder. Political science
is all about Rising and setting like a sun'. I didn't forget it still got free inter-
nal marks for this. While all speak about this Xavier says "Want to come with me to
my Football ground?". All get in Xavier's car and goes to the football field. A mod-
ern one with all amenities. Manoj comments "Xavier, this is and was your dream
ground! It's excellent". They all speaking about what all happened after they left

Day 1,
20th January 2016
JK Roy aka Writer Roy aka Roy, "I am going to create a new world.A world with
no corruption.A world with no sorrow.A world which will salute the great and
good.A world where Good is Dominant over the Evil". Roy wakes up.He looks at

the things he sees in his dreams in that Diary.He pulls his bag keeps the
diary in it fills ink in his fountain pen.He then sits on his bike and leaves
to work.
Roy used to live alone in an appartment.
He was a disciplined man.He used to leave for work daily exactly at 7am.He
used to reach home at 5pm.He was an introvert and a person who used to never
speak with anybody and only cared about his work.
SJ Raj aka Police Raj aka Raj, " Goa! Goa! Goa! what a beautiful Place.I
would live my whole life there".A police constable comes near Raj and
says"Some people have come to meet you". Raj stops scrolling the internet and
asks them to come inside.An old man with his son enters Raj's Cabin.The old
man says"Good morning sir,My son has a complaint".Raj takes the complaint and
starts to read it."My name is Jackson. I work in News 3.42. I have a boss

Police system. I resigned my job for that reason. Now, as i know about their

asks who shot him. Ram points at Raj. Ram dies on the way to hospital. Raj

It was a paradox

--- The Last Cut.pdf ---

The Last Cut
Midnight in a random street in India. A butcher shop's light glew in the dark. The
noise of meat being cut echoed through the quiet night. It started to drizzle. The
man cutting the meat put it into a garbage bag and stepped outside. He stood there,
holding the garbage bag in one hand and a backpack slung over his shoulder. A bus
stopped in front of the shop. The man got inside, taking the garbage bag and backpack
with him. As the bus moved he takes a seat next to a man wearing a police uniform.
The police man asks "Where are you going?". The man replied "I'm on my way to Manali,
what about you sir?". The police replies "I am on my way there too! This is a long
route bus, takes around 5 days for Manali!". The man replies "Yes, I know that!". The
police man tells his name to be Shivaram aka Shiva, Clean Shaved, medium hair, about
6ft tall. The man tells his name as Dev, long bearded, with long hairs, about 6ft
tall. The police was getting transferred to Manali as ACP. Dev told Shiva that he was
going to Manali as his butcher shop was too old and wanted to get some work in a
place far from his hometown. In the middle of the journey, the bus breaks down.
People in the bus were asked to get down. Dev goes forward and asks the driver "Can I
help you?". The driver harshly replies "Even I, as the driver cannot repair this bus.
It is too old for repairs". Dev insists in repairing and makes the bus run smoothly.
Shiva asks dev later on the bus "What all works do you know?". Dev replies "Anything
I get to work, I work at my best!". On reaching Manali, Shiva gives Dev his card with
his phone number. Shiva turns back and finds Dev searching something. Shiva goes back
to Dev and asks "What are you searching for?". Dev replies "I don't know whom to ask
for a job". Shiva asks Dev to come along with him. Dev was resistant but later agreed
to go with Shiva. Shiva takes him to his private police quarters and asks "feel free
to use whatever you want. I'll be going to the station to get done with my appoinment
order". Dev replies "Feel free? Should I pay you later?". Shiva replies "Never mind,
it's all yours and mine together, take it that way!". Shiva takes his appointment or-
der and leaves for the police station. Shiva asks the constable to meet the
Commisioner. The constable replies "Your joining date was postponed as the current
ACP is going to retire in two days and the commissioner has gone outside". Shiva de-
cides to return back to the quarters. When he arrives, Dev was no where to be found.
Shiva asks the security for Dev. The security replies "He just left to the Beas
River". Shiva's car and bike were yet to come. He takes an auto and asks the driver
to take him where the tourists go to see the Beas river. The driver takes him to the
river banks. Dev was standing in the banks of the river completely zoned out. Shiva
stands beside Dev and tells "I am free for more two days, you have any plans for
finding a job?, then I can help you!". Dev doesn't reply, turns back and starts to
walk to the quarters. Shiva comes behind Dev and asks him to say something. Dev
stops, grabs Shiva's hand and runs. Shiva turns back and finds people chasing them.
Both run inside the quarters. Dev opens his bag and takes out his cleaver. Shiva
falls down in shock and asks "Is this what you have in your bag?, then what do you
have in your trash bag?". Shiva looks around for the trash bag. Dev replies "It had
the body of their leader! And I just disposed it in the river!". Shiva locks the door
and looks out through the window. The men chasing them were blocked by the security.
One of them hits the security and enters into the compound. One of the henchmen
starts to knock the door. Dev tightens his grip on the cleaver. Shiva sits down, eyes
teared, scared in fear and face sweaty. Shiva pulls out his gun. Dev asks Shiva "Go
inside the room and lock yourself!". Shiva grabs his gun and replies "No!, after this
is over, I'll have to get you arrested!". The henchmen break the door and enter in-
side. Before Dev could do anything, the man stabs Dev in his stomach. Dev starts to
scream loudly. Shiva shoots the man who stabbed Dev. Dev takes out the knife from his
stomach and stabs it into another man. Dev takes his cleaver and starts to stab each
of the henchmen one by one. Finally, a man enters the room. Dev looks at him and
shouts "Rajeev?!, So it was you!, I killed Jaffer, Next is you!". Rajeev's legs
starts to tremble, he takes his sickle and tries to stab Dev. Dev dodges the stab and
stabs Rajeev with his cleaver. Rajeev dies instantly. Dev sits on Rajeev's body and
starts to stab him continuously like a maniac. Shiva looks around the room, com-
pletely messy with blood stains all over the wall. Glass and doors were broken. Shiva
asks Dev "Who are you?". Dev tells his past to Shiva.
Few years ago
Dev's full name was Devesh Sharma, clean shave, medium short hairs. He worked under
an atheist organisation and was an atheist. Dev was the face of the organisation,
participating in public debates and open talks. He had few friends working with the
organisation, One of them was Jenifer, Shiva's Fiancee and Dev's best friend. There
was a social media handle in which, the marketing head posted really bad things about
every religion hurting each religion's sentiment. This created a huge backlash among
the public. The public started attacking the organisation building. People from all
religions started to rush inside to hit the people who hurt their sentiments and
started a riot. Later, the police intervened to stop the riot. By the time, the riot
ended, many people from the organisation has lost their lives including Jenifer. The
main leaders were Rajeev shankar from Hindu society and Ismail Ibrahim from Muslim
society. Ismail's main follower was Jaffer. Dev couldn't bear the weight of the num-
ber of people he had seen dead goes into exile far from his hometown. Hiding himself
in a butcher shop. Dev had grown his hair and beard. One day, Jaffer comes into the
butcher shop to buy meat. Jaffer identifies Dev and calls his men to come to the
shop. Dev overhears the conversation and decides to confront Jaffer. When the night
arrived, jaffer comes into the butcher shop along with his men. Dev starts to pull
Jaffer using a rope and tieing it on Jaffer's neck. One by one Dev kills all Jaffer's
men. Thinking that it's not safe staying in the Butcher Shop anymore, decides to go
to another place far away. In the same night, Dev cuts the men into pieces and puts
them in a trash bag. Divides it into three bags. Disposed one in the shop, other in
the bus stand and one in the Beas river.
Present Day
Shiva gets to know about what happened to Jenifer and says "I knew Jenifer always
told to meet Devesh, and told he was a great man!, but great to what extent? You just
killed lives of many!". Dev replies "These lives I have taken may be a crime, but I
need to prove we are wrong! I need to find out who created that hateful message
against all communities!". Shiva replies "I! I did it!". Dev is shock and starts to
punch Shiva on his face. Shiva tells Dev "Please listen to me!". Dev doesn't listen
and starts to kick Shiva. Shiva punches Dev on his face. Dev grabs Shiva's collar and
jumps on his face and starts to slap Shiva on his face. Shiva shouts "I was forced to
change the post in the social media!". Dev stops and falls on the floor. Shiva tells
Dev "I was working as the police cyber head during that time!. I hated the place
where Jenifer worked and that's when Ismail came to my life. Ismail was a friend of
the Commisioner and the commissioner wanted me to help him. Ismail Ibrahim wanted to
close your atheist organisation, and asked me to hack into your social media handles
and to post such things!". Dev shouts "What did we do wrong?, my friends lost their
lives and my life was turned into ruins!". Shiva tells "What about mine?, I did it
thinking it as a benefit and later killed my love, my fiancee Jenifer!". Dev tells
"The villain of our story is Ismail!, I'll kill him and you can arrest me!". Shiva
tells "No! You wouldn't get arrested! I'll take care of the matters!". Dev and Shiva
Shake their hands. The quarters was a two storey building, so Dev shifts to the first
floor with his bag. Shiva makes a Call to somebody named "II" standing next to the
window when Dev is not around. Shiva tells "Ismail! Out community's Rajeev is Dead!
It would be great if we join hands together and kill Dev in public!". Ismail, Long
bearded 6ft long with short hairs, says "Mission Ram-Rahim is On!". Dev overhears
their conversation from the first floor window and smirks.
[Interval]
Two days later, Shiva joins to his post as ACP of Manali division. Red alert was de-
clared all over Manali as weather reports suggested heavy rainfall for a week. Ismail
takes his car and leaves to Manali without knowing about the notification. A small
landslide was hit near to Manali blocking the flow of Beas river and restricting the
water flow. Dev was in his room. Suddenly an avalanche broke out in the nearby moun-
tain and the snow rushed inside Shiva's police quarter. Dev was trapped inside the
snow. Rescue operations were started on full swing. Water levels started to raise in
the Beas river which was blocked due to the landslide. Manali was covered in an
avalanche on one side and landslide on the other. Rescue operatives could not find
Dev. Shiva calls Ibrahim and informs "Dev is dead!". Ibrahim replies "Let there be an
avalanche or a landslide! I am on my way to Manali to check if he is dead! We don't
want it to happen again, we thought all members of the organisation were dead but
this time we make sure he is dead". Two days after the landslide, Ibrahim stops his
car before the avalanche began and started to walk to the avalanche by making a fake
ID of himself as a rescue operative. The Beas river burst opens through the mud and
comes with full speed hitting the avalanche and the town of Manali. Rescue operations
could not be held further due to heavy water flooding the area. Shiva and Ibrahim re-
joiced as Dev could not be rescued and if he didn't swim up, he will die of suffoca-
tion, so in either of the way with cold or suffocation Dev would have died. Moments
before the flood began, the water hits the avalanche on full force. Dev was pulled
into the water and started to drown. He makes his way out of the quarters but with
the speed of the river, Dev is gushed outside Manali division and had reached Kullu,
40km away from Manali. There were minor floods in Kullu too, Dev is rescued by a res-
cue operative and taken to hospital. The doctor bandaged minor bruises but Dev's legs
were cold and numb and Dev was unconscious. Dev's legs were bandaged and physiother-
apy was being done. Fours days in hospital and Dev got his consciousness back. He
looked at his leg bandaged and asked the doctor "What happened to my legs!?". The
doctor named Safa replied "Your legs were numb due to cold. how did you end up in the
flood?". Dev thinking that Shiva and Ibrahim will be behind him he tells "I am a
fisherman from Dobhi! I was in my home when the river water gushed into my house up-
rooting it from ground!". A week later Dev was discharged. Avalanche was cleared and
flood had stopped in Manali in the meantime. Ibrahim and Shiva were in the police
quarters. Few men enter into the house. Ibrahim and Shiva together shout "Start to
hit him!", pointing at eachother. Few men were Ibrahim's community members and few
were from Shiva's community. They start hitting eachother. Nearby house members too
join the fight starting a religious riot in Manali. People were crowded from day to
night. During the night, Dev enters into the quarters. Ibrahim shouts "Your community
entered into our mosques and attacked our people!". Shiva shouts "Your community
broke out temples! What about that?". Dev limps and enters into the crowd fighting
for their own community. Slowly enters into the house and takes out his cleaver from
his bag. Dev starts to wash the cleaver having the blood of the people he had killed
previously, silently. He keeps the cleaver tucked into his pants. Silently goes out
and Removes petrol from a car stalled near the quarter and fills it into a can. Dev
then makes a hole in the can and spreads the petrol on the floor of the house. Later
burns the matchstick and burns the house. Makes a motolov cocktail and throws it near
the people fighting for religion and starts running. People fighting started to chase
Dev. Shiva and Ibrahim stop fighting and starts to chase behind the people. Shiva
turns back and finds his house burning. Shiva shouts at the people to help him extin-
guish the fire but nobody cared and were busy chasing Dev. Dev dials the firetruck
and they arrive at the scene. As they sprayed water the petrol started to float on
water and started to burn more as the petrol spread. Finnally the fire was extin-
guished with CO2 can. Shiva tries to take his car out and go behind the people to
find out whom they were chasing. When Shiva tries to start his car, it wasn't getting
started. When he checked the car was out of fuel. Dev comes out of the car and starts
to run till he could see the people. Dev reaches the banks of Beas river and finds
the people standing there. Dev gets to know that the person who threw fire at them
jumped into the river. People started blaming eachother stating that it was from
their opposite community who threw fire at them. People started to close the shutters
of the shops and started to burn down cars. Ibrahim stood without speaking anything
in one corner. All eyes went on him. They thought Ibrahim had threw fire at them and
that is why he is not acting for anything. People charged towards Ismail Ibrahim.
Ibrahim started to run. People now assumed that Ibrahim for sure was the person who
threw fire at them. The Muslim community tried to stop the Hindu community to go to-
wards Ibrahim. Dev swims out of the river. Shiva was still standing near the banks of
the river unknowing what it was. Dev punches Shiva from behind. Shiva couldn't under-
stand what was happening and finds Dev standing behind him. At the same time, a so-
cial media post of Ibrahim speaking bad about Muslim community comes out from an
anonymous account which was actually uploaded by Dev. One member who was helping
Ibrahim to run from Muslim community sees the post and tells everyone about it. Even
the Muslim community, now, starts chasing Ibrahim. Ibrahim starts running for his
life. Dev shows the video of Ibrahim speaking and tells Shiva "Public will give back
Ibrahim for his deeds. Now, you get back your deeds from me!". Dev takes out his
cleaver. Shiva couldn't react and slips and falls down. Shiva tells "what about your
deeds? Killing many people?". Dev replies "For my deeds, even being an atheist, I be-
lieve in karma. Karma will hit me back for my deeds!". Shiva tells "All have the same
thing! Why don't let me to karma?". Dev replies "You don't have a different karma! I
am the karma for you!". Dev charges towards Shiva with his cleaver. Shiva dodges the
stab. Dev falls down and rolls on the floor. Shiva and Dev get up and charges towards
eachother. Both hit eachother on heads and fall back. Dev grips his cleaver and cuts
Shiva's right hand. Dev takes the cut hand and throws it into the river. Shiva shouts
in pain and grabs Dev's neck with his left hand. Dev takes his cleaver and cuts
Shiva's left hand. Shiva tells "You could just slice open my throat! Why are you tor-
turing me like this?". Dev replies "That's right!". Dev takes the cleaver and slices
through Shiva's throat, killing him. Dev wipes the blood on the cleaver and throws it
towards the crowd who had surrounded Ibrahim. One Muslim man takes the cleaver and
kills Ibrahim.
Dev walks towards Manali bus stand and takes a bus to kullu. Reaches Kullu and meets
Doctor Safa. She tells "You are Devesh right? I have seen you! Now I am able to get a
good view of your face. Previously it had bandages and I couldn't Identify you". Dev
replies "Yes I am Devesh Sharma". Safa replies "You must have had a hard time after
that riot, right?". Devesh replies "Yes! Can you help me get a shelter here?". Safa
replies "You don't remember me don't you? I used to work as a medical advisor in your
organization! I resigned and shifted here before the backlash to the organisation".
Safa grabs Dev's hand and takes him towards her home. Dev hesitantly walked behind
her, knowing one day anyone who might know him as Devesh will catch up. Dev murmurs
to himself "In the clash between vengeance and justice, we often become the very
darkness we seek to destroy. I am the darkness that lives inside me, and I shall de-
liver my last cut!".
The End

The Last Relic
Bangalore
Night, A man 21 years old, slowly opens his room's door. With a bag on his shoulders,
he enters into the living room, opens the main door and the gate and leaves. He was
wearing a hoodie and a cap.
Four years later, Hyderabad
He books a dorm room, they ask for his ID with the name 'Harry Cook'. The
Receptionist asks "Room no. 204 Sir!". Harry nods and the receptionist notices a Cut
on his nose and asks "What happened to your nose?". Harry says "Mind your own
Business Lady!". Harry enters into the room and makes a call and says "I have the
Relic of Buddha!". The other side voice says "Get into the train to Bangalore tomor-
row morning, we will exchange the Relic within the train, you will recieve a phone in
the trash-can, you take the phone and get the instructions from it!". Harry removes
the sim from his phone and melts it. Harry unscrews his phone takes out the storage
unit. He throws the phone down, takes out a hammer from his bag and breaks it.
Meanwhile, Chandrashekhar aka Chandra, aged 58, is appointed to find the thief of the
Last Relic of Buddha. Chandra goes to the excavation site and enquires the chief
Archaeologist named Raman. Raman says "This area is a restricted part and we don't
allow anyone inside except students whom we use for our benefits. They help us in
searching the fossil and we provide them like a hands on experience while our work is
being done". Chandra asks "Anybody other than students who may have entered yester-
day?". Raman denies saying nobody like that has come.
Next day
Harry takes the phone and enters into a coach which was told on phone. Harry is in-
formed to keep the bag with the Relic on top of the bag of the girl sitting in front
of him. The girl was 23 years old as written in her pass. Harry does as said and
smiles at the girl. The train is stopped at a station and rush is filled. Harry is
asked to leave immediately throwing the phone out and the bag will be taken. The girl
notices Harry's bag on top of her bag and rushed to give him back. The girl squeezes
out as Harry gets down from the train, the girl too jumps out and shouts "Hey man!
You left your bag!". Harry runs to her amused and Runs towards her as the train
starts to move. The girl says "You left your bag!". Harry takes the bag, thanks her.
The girl looks at the train and tries to get inside but is unsuccessful. Harry con-
fused on what to do with the bag goes to her and asks "Your train left, What's your
plan?". The girl says "I don't know! I have to reach Bangalore, my family will be
waiting for me!". Harry asks the TC and says to the girl "Next train comes after 6
hours! Come we will go eat something!". On their way the girl introduces herself as
'Maya Thomas'. Maya asks "What do you do?". Harry replies "I am a Archeology
Student!". Maya replies "Your parents allowed you to do that? In my home they just
gave me two options 'Engineering and medicine' after sometime much requests they let
me take B.Com!". Harry smiles and asks "can I call you, Matchstick?". Maya says
"Sure, but why?". Harry laughs and says "Cause you look like one!". They enter into a
restaurant and have something. After sometime, they go back to the railway station.
Harry didn't have his phone to contact the buyer. Harry decides to go with Maya. As
the train arrives, Maya and Harry get into the train and leaves. Meanwhile,
Chandrashekhar takes the list of student and send it to the Cyber-cell to sort out
the phone numbers which are not in service. It sorts out to 5 students 'Harry',
'Christopher', 'Raj', 'Ganesh' and 'Altaf'. All of these 5 students numbers were un-
able to be traced Harry's last location was in a hotel in Hyderabad, Christopher in
Hyderabad Airport, Raj near charminar, Ganesh in Mumbai and Altaf's number in Delhi
and phone was in Dubai. Chandra doubts Altaf and tries to find sources to communicate
with Altaf.
Bangalore
Harry reaches Bangalore and Bids Maya goodbye. He goes to a old workshop and meets an
old man saying "Hassan Bhai, How are you?". Hassan turns and says "I'm fine! What are
you doing here?". Harry says "Just came to see my old City where I grew up!". Hassan
asks "Did you go to your home?". Harry says "No!, Bhai Can you arrange me a second-
hand phone and a sim?". Hassan gives Harry a phone. Harry kept the bag with the Relic
close to him. Hassan asks "What is in that bag?". Harry says "Nothing Bhai!". Harry
