--- The Midnight Murder.pdf ---

The Midnight Murder : Shattered Justice
It was a hot summer night, two men were walking on the road and suddenly the power
goes off. Next morning, Rahul aged 43, 6 feet long was going for a walk for the first
time. It was the previous day he and his family had shifted to their new locality G
Nagar. He had a trash bag in his hand which he drops it on the road during his walk.
Rahul hears police siren and turns. Few police men come out and asks Rahul to surren-
der. Not knowing what was happening Rahul surrendered. He was continuously asking the
police why he was being arrested but the police ignored to answer his question. Rahul
had not brought his phone for walking and had left it at home. His wife Tina starts
to get worried about him as he left house at 6.30am, now time was 10.30am and Rahul
had not returned home yet. Tina knew that, If Rahul had great mood he would walk from
6.30am to 10.30am but this time it was getting late. Tina was getting late for her
work, as Rahul was late Tina had dropped their son Rana to school. It was Rana's last
day of school, his 12th exams were over. Tina frustrated being late for work hands
over the house key to the neighbour and leaves. Tina and Rana had a daughter named
Priya had left to her college at 6.15am, usually she used to do her own work and used
to never inform anyone while leaving or coming back home. Sub-inspector Hari, aged
27, 6ft tall, is given charge of the case and starts to interrogate Rahul. Hari asks
"Today morning around 6.45am, you dropped a bag on the road near the garbage stand.
Is it true?". Rahul replies "Yes sir, that was the trash from my new house which I
shifted to yesterday". Hari continues "Do you mean human body is a trash for you?".
Rahul shocked asks "Sir, I think you have misunderstood me! By trash I mean plastics,
organic wastes. I don't know why I have been arrested. My wife would be waiting for
me, it's very late, they will be worried. I can't contact them, I don't have my phone
and don't know her number!". Hari takes out a laptop and shows them the CCTV footage
of the camera in the garbage stand. Rahul is seen placing the trash bag and walking
away. The body was found when a street dog climbing the trashcans dropped the bag
down. The Victim was cut into a million pieces. According to forensic report, the
Victim is found to be a Man of age gap between 35-40 years. No Man-missing cases were
registered at the nearby police station in the past month. Tina in office was worried
about Rahul, if he would have reached home, he would have either called or messaged,
both was not there. Tina asks permission and leaves back to home. Rahul frustrated
with the interrogation asks a police to give their phone to call his wife Tina. The
Policeman ignores Rahul and stood. Tina arrives at her house and checks if Rahul had
come. When she understands Rahul has not reached home, she leaves for the police sta-
tion to file a complaint. As soon as Tina enters the police station, she finds Rahul
sitting on the bench at the Police station. Rahul looks at Tina and says "I have been
framed for a murder! You remember the trash bag I took today morning, they found a
Dead body cut into pieces in it. They have CCTV footage also". Tina calls her
office's Legal advisor to come to the police station. Meanwhile, Tina understands all
the details about the case Rahul was framed for. Tina escalates the case as Rahul was
arrested without a warrant and Rahul is given a temporary bail. At night 10pm they
reach their home. Priya and Rana were at home waiting for them to come. Tina tells
Priya and Rana on what has happened that day. Rahul tells to Tina "We left our old
home because of those issues. Now, on the first day here, again there are issues. Our
life is filled with these issues". Rahul goes to his room to sleep. Tina asks her
children to go sleep. Tina calls Advocate Manish and brings out the whole sketch of
the case. Next Day Morning, News reporters and Press were waiting outside Rahul's
house. That day's headline was "A Psycopathic Murderer or a Cold-blooded Criminal,
Who is Rahul?". Priya takes a leave from her college. Tina Locked the doors and
closed the windows to avoid the press. Rahul stayed in his room. SI Hari comes to
Rahul's home to arrest him and Rahul is taken to court. The judge asks "Did you com-
mit the murder? if yes we will reduce your punishment". Suddenly there is a loud
shout from the crowd "I did it!". The judge asks the police to bring whomever it was.
To everyones shock it was Rana, Rahul's son. Rahul is taken to dock. Rahul is shocked
and faints, the police takes Rahul to the nearest hospital. Rana says "I killed him,
I killed John!".
Few Months ago
Rahul, Tina, Priya and Rana lived in a quiet surrounding area. There were trees and
houses nearby. There was a very mysterious man who only used to come to eat lunch and
dinner in the opposite house of Rahul's house. The opposite house owner was Joseph.
Tina had a Sister named Rina. Rina's husband was in military. Joseph and Rahul were
good friends. Joseph one night calls Rahul outside and tells "If You have seen a man
coming to my house every lunch and dinner, be careful of him. He is a murderer and
his name is John. He is eating lunch and dinner from my home everyday because he
threatened us that he will kill us if we tell anything to the cops. If you can please
help me by catching him outside this area" for which Rahul agreed. It was Rana's 18th
Birthday, Rina and her daughter Eva had come to Rahul's house. After the Party Rina
and Tina were speaking in the Living room. Rahul had an online meeting. Priya had a
project to complete. Eva was on her phone outside Rahul's house. Rana had gone to the
terrace with his friend. Suddenly Rana hears a scream and runs down. He goes inside
his house and they tell they didn't hear any noise. Rana asks where Priya and Eva
was. They tell Priya is inside completing her project and Eva was outside. Rana runs
outside and finds a Man tie Eva onto a tree. Rana runs and tears open the knot, Eva
falls down. He calls His mother Tina to come outside and starts running behind the
man. He ran as fast as he could. Suddenly, he slips over a pile of stones and falls
down and the man slowly getting far from his eyesight. The street light wasn't work-
ing. They had a camera in their house which had night vision and find the man was
John. Upon doctor's inspection, Eva was assaulted and killed. Rina falls unconscious
and dies of heart attack. Rina's husband comes to attend Rina's and Eva's funeral,
gives a case on John and asks Rahul to look after the case until he was back. Since
then Rahul had no sleep. Every night John used to come near Rahul's bedroom window
and shout loudly, sometimes he threw stones at the window. When Rina's husband re-
turned, he was murdered and Rahul decided to escalate the case further. Rahul was
threatened of being killed everyday. One night, Priya was on her way back home. Rana
was standing on the terrace without wearing a T-shirt. Suddenly he finds John running
towards Priya who was looking into her phone and walking. John catches Priya. Rana
Rana down stairs holding his T-shirt in his hand. When Rana started running, when he
turned back he saw behind him Joseph running. John leaves Priya down and started to
run. They chase him on all nearby roads until they lost sight of him. Rahul, getting
to know about this incident, decides to shift their home little far away. The night
they settled at G Nagar, John and one of his friend Ramesh turns of the Power in the
area and enters into Rahul's new home. John asks his friend to stay down and enters
into priya's room. John on's the torch light when he hits the light, he finds Rana
sitting looking at John on Priya's room. Rana catches John hits him with a hammer.
Slowly takes him to the room on the terrace. Pulls out a Cleaver and Cuts John into a
million pieces. Blood splashing all over his face. After this, he packs him in a bag.
He changes the Garbage bag with the bag having John's body. Rana then Runs to the
Terrace and cleans the room. Rana Looks up at the moon and shouts "This is the end of
people Like you!!!!!".
[INTERVAL]
Present Day
The Judge listens to the arguments made by Rana and convicts him. He was sentenced
for 7 days prison and the next verdict would be on the 8th day. Rahul is set free
though he could not leave the city as he was not completely out of the case. Rahul,
Tina and Priya leave for home whereas, Rana was sent to prison. Rahul plans on how to
rescue Rana. SI Hari and Advocate Manish arrive at Rahul's home. Hari briefs Rahul
"What your son did was right. But, now we can't help him out. He has confessed in the
court in front of the judges". Manish tells "There is only one way to help him out of
jail. We have to make him as if he was physically assaulted. So the case can be taken
as self defence". Hari calls one of the Jail guard and asks him to hit Rana on his
body before producing him to the doctor. The reason Hari was supporting Rahul now was
due to the Act of Rana, which moved his heart. Rana was hit and was produced in front
of the doctor. 8 days later, Rana is produced to court. Manish tells to the judge
"Your honor, Rana was firstly assaulted by John. The proof is his friend whom I would
like to produce in front of the court". John's friend who accompanied him that day
comes to the dock. John's friend Ramesh says "I was waiting outside that night. I had
a torch and was looking near the window. John broke the window and entered and I saw
him hit that boy, Rana first". The whole courtroom was in silence. The judge asked
for a break and meets Rana along with Rahul. The judge asks "Rana, You're a young boy
but what you did is not correct. Your motives were like that of a psychopath!". Rana
replies "When the police knowing John was a murderer and have been to jail once,
never tried to arrest him even with complete evidence, people like us become the
law!". Rahul says "I would have gone to jail if I knew it was Rana, I would have
taken the responsibility". Rana continues "This case is now self-defence but the mis-
take I did was cut him into pieces right?, John is dead but the pieces that were
found was someone else's. How could the police be so illogical?, does that trash bag
contain so much of weight as that of a human body?. There were only 2-3 pieces of his
body which was kept in the trash!". The public prosecutor records the conversation
and produces it in front of the court. The judge then asks SI Hari to find John's
body and the next hearing of the court would be in 2 weeks. SI Hari was in a turmoil.
He had 2 weeks time to find a body about which nobody knows. Hari decides to start
the investigation from beginning. In the trash bag, there were pieces of the victim's
hand ie John's hand. He asks the forensic team to find traces of his fingerprint. The
forensic team solves the puzzle and when examining, they find the fingerprint of a
man who had gone missing 3 months back and was found dead without legs and hands. The
man's name is also found to be John. Hari is shocked with this revelation and drives
to Rahul's home to confront Rana. Rana is sleeping on the couch. Hari breaks into the
house and pushes Rana down to the floor. Rana gets up and asks "Sir, why are you hit-
ting me? What happened". Hari replies "You want to know what happened?". Hari grabs
the TV remote and throws it on Rana. Rana angrily pushes Hari onto the table. Rahul
interferes and asks "Why are you beating my son?". Hari replies "First I'll have to
take you all to custody and speak!". Rahul tells "Sir! Cool down!". Hari tells "John
died 3 months back and now you are getting surrendered for that? And how was the body
still intact?". Rahul looks into Hari's eyes and tells "You are the Police and it's
your work to find that out!". Hari turns and finds Ramesh pointing a gun at him. Hari
kicks Ramesh and grabs the gun, Points the gun at Ramesh and says "I now understand!,
you are behind this!". Ramesh tells "I'll tell you everything".
Few months back
After Eva was assaulted and killed, Tina died and Eva's Father was killed, Due to the
horror caused by John, Rahul seeks help of a murderer named Ramesh. Due to lack of
response from the police, Rahul found that this method for better. It was a rainy
night. Rahul and Ramesh waited to find John. When John arrived at the location, Rahul
points Ramesh to John. John's face was not clearly visible due to rain and the dark-
ness of the night. When John finds two men waiting for him, he starts to run. Ramesh
and Rahul start chasing John. At a Point Ramesh pull out his cleaver and cuts John's
legs and hands. Kills John with poison intoxication through a syringe. When light
falls on John's face, Ramesh gets to know it was John, Ramesh's best friend. Ramesh
in anger for that starts to threaten Rahul and his family for making him kill his own
friend. Rahul unable to bear the threat decides to change his home. The night Rahul
changed his home, Ramesh breaks in. Ramesh points gun at Priya and tells "I'll kill
and assault her if you don't listen to me. My friend was killed 2 and a half month
back. Though his body was discovered by the police, his hands and legs are still with
me which I had chemically frozen. I want you to do as I say and I will stop threaten-
ing your family". The plan was, Rahul will throw the trash bag in the morning and get
arrested. Later Rana will go to the court and tell her is the killer. As according to
Documents, when John was killed, Rana was still a minor who was actually not, due to
the date of birth change in the documents it was considered a minor crime and the
punishment will be reduced. Ramesh will be the eye witness for the partially fabri-
cated story.
Present day
Hari listens to this and records the complete conversation. Hari informs to Ramesh "I
have recorded this conversation and will produce it to court in the next hearing".
Ramesh tries to grab Hari's phone. Ramesh pushes Hari down holds the gun and tries to
grab the phone. Hari skillfully kicks Ramesh. Ramesh falls down and tries to get up.
Hari kicks Ramesh. Hari grabs the gun and phone and Runs outside the house. Ramesh
starts to follow Hari. Rahul and Rana try to stop Ramesh. Hari enters his car. Ramesh
takes a spear from the garden and throws it towards Hari's car. The spear hits the
Car's engine and the car stops working. Hari gets out and starts to run. Rahul grabs
Ramesh by neck. Hari remembers something and runs towards the car. Hari takes out the
Hand-cuffs from the car and puts it on Ramesh's hand. Hari asks the control room to
get a car and Ramesh is taken to custody.
Three Days Later
In the Court, Hari produces all evidence. The judge punishes Ramesh to be hung after
21 years in prison. Rahul accepts in front of the court that he was the one who asked
Ramesh to kill John. Rana was cleared from the case. Rahul was sentenced for 7 years
in prison. The Judge then closes the case. Hari after the court session goes to
Rahul's house. Hari meets Rana, Priya and Tina. Tina was sad as her husband was sen-
tenced for prison. Manish arrives at Rahul's house. Manish tells "Did you all see the
news? Ramesh escaped from the prison bus!". Priya suddenly shouts from her room. Hari
rushes into the room and finds Ramesh pointing gun at Priya. Ramesh tells "You and
Rahul's family ruined my life and I will ruin yours!". Hari pulls out his gun and
shoots Ramesh on his head. He calls the police and tells "Ramesh is Dead". Tina asks
Manish "Is there any way we can get Bail for Rahul?". Manish replies "It tough be-
cause he Confessed in the Court he did the crime!". Hari tells "There is one way.
Impersonation and Manipulate his death. But that is very risky!". Manish replies
"Can't you all wait for 7 years?". Tina replies "No! We can't, Is there any other way
Hari Sir?". Hari responds "No!". Hari suddenly gets a call and is stunned hearing
"Sir! Ramesh killed Rahul before escaping from the bus!". Hari's phone falls down,
and he looks at Tina and Manish and says "Rahul is dead!".
The End

The Pharmacist
In the city of Mumbai, there is a pharmacy run my a man named Karthik
Raghavan about age 40, 6ft 4inch tall. He started this shop 2 years ago.
Daily, He Wakes up at 6am. Opens his shop at 7am and closes his shop at 1am
where he travelled using his car. He always is punctual and has never taken
holiday or breaks. He eats lunch inside the pharmacy itself. If he sees some-
body who coughing in front of him who is buying medicines for something else,
gives the medicine for coughing for free. One day, a man named Akash comes to
the Pharmacy. Karthik asks "What do you want sir?". Akash stands staring at
Karthik. Karthik asks "Sir! what do you want sir?". Akash tells "I'm having
fever. I thought you will look at me and give free medicines". Karthik gives
a glance at Akash and says "What you are doing is not right. I'll give you
the medicines wait". Karthik gives the medicine. Akash smiles at him and says
"Thank you!". Karthik gives a stare (a death stare). Akash was a auto driver.
He takes his auto and leaves. That night, Karthik closes his shop early
around 8pm. Goes to his home. Looks at a picture hanging on the wall. Goes to
the outhouse. There was a small box on the wall. He pulls out a double action
revolver out of it. There were 6 bullets in it. Karthik locks his house. Goes
to a printing shop and prints "SHOP CLOSED FOR 7 DAYS". He sticks this on his
shop takes his car and leaves to Delhi.
He reaches Delhi and books a hotel in marriot. He goes to chandini chowk for
shopping. While he was shopping, a man holding a cleaver runs towards Karthik
to stab him. Karthik dodges it and kicks the man. Grabs the cleaver from his
hand. Another man runs towards Karthik trying to punch him. Karthik holds his
hand and cuts it with the cleaver. Police come and arrest Karthik. [In phone
call]"So he returns to Delhi". The man on the other side replies "Yes sir,
Should i bring him to you". The man on the phone replies "Let him get beaten
by the police custody first. When that is done bring him to me". The man cuts
the call. After Karthik was completely beaten he was blind folded and taken
to the man. They open the blind fold and hands tied. Karthik smiles and says
"So, You Mr.Arjun Patel (A man with a long scar near his eye. Aged about 55-
60, 5ft 11inches tall) still remembers me even after killing my parents and
wife". Arjun replies "How can I forget you. Because of you my boss tried to
kill me. But now I am happy after knowing the name of my boss Mr.Deepak
Raghavan, your loving brother who went missing 20 years ago". Karthik amused
replies saying "My brother Deepak is still alive? We searched him for 3 years
when police declared he was dead". Arjun replies "I went to kidnap your
brother trying to find him somehow and bring you in front of me. But he in-
fact was the person who asked to kill your family (laughing), I then declared
him as my boss who didn't care about his own family. Now his order is to kill
you". Karthik gives a death stare, headbutts 2 men standing beside him. One
guy comes to stab him. Karthik dodges and the knife cuts the rope tied in his
hands. Karthik beats up Arjun. Arjun is fallen on the floor. Karthik sits on
a chair. "How was my acting regarding my brother's identity reveal?.
Impressive isn't it. I knew it was him the whole time, i couldn't believe the
story you created. Our rivalry behind with the search of my brother, 15 years
later, look I'm standing in front of you. You chased me from 6 cities and my
7th City was Mumbai. 2 years in each city for 14 years. You chased me for 14
whole years. Now, today you are going to die. How should I kill you? The way
you killed my parents or the way you killed my wife?. It would be right if i
keep the parents one for later. I'll kill you the way you killed my wife.
Drowned in swimming pool. But there are no swimming pools nearby" Karthik
says. Karthik then hits Arjun. Arjun starts to run. Arjun gets chased on the
streets of chandini chowk. People looking at Arjun laughing. Arjun looking at
people's reaction his emotions get triggered. Pulls out a knife from a shop
and points towards Karthik. He tries to stab Karthik. Karthik kicks his hand
and the knife flicks in the air. Karthik catches the knife and stabs Arjun's
back 3 times. Karthik ties Arjun's hands and takes him to yamuna river.
Drowns him there killing Arjun Patel.
[FLASHBACK]
In the City of Bangalore, Karthik Raghavan and his younger brother, Deepak
had differing personalities. They had a pharmaceutical business named
"Raghavan group of pharmaceutical industries (RGPI)" Run by their Father
Raghavan. Karthik remained focused on the family business and his ambition to

Saviour II: The Final Redemption
" The notion of a saviour reminds us that, even in our darkest moments, there is the
potential for light and deliverance, from within ourselves"
Black magic is a familiar word. The David fort is accustomed to it. The Ancestors of
the Fortress wrote a book on it using black magic. In the forest except the Kings,
the only people who knew black magic was the Forbidden Family of the kingdom. When
Ancestors of David fort understood about a family using 'black magic' they were ban-
ished from the kingdom sent to the centre of the forest. They built a hut there. They
put up a spell in the hut saying "Seules les personnes dont la famille connaît la
magie noire ne seront pas affectées par ce sort de folie. Les gens partiront en folie
meurtrière pour éliminer les derniers membres du royaume de David". Using the Black
magic with the kings they used it to see the future of the kingdom and note it in a
diary. They could only write it to a limit and the end could never be seen.
It was Rainy day in the forest. The David fort which had been completely burnt, was
now turned into a museum. The Hut in the middle of the forest was fenced and forest
guards were appointed all over the forest and mainly, near the hut. A young man,
about 25 years old, enters the forest. The hut in the forest covered with overgrown
moss and vines. The man walks towards the hut, Breaks open the door and Enters in-
side. The hut was completely electric fenced where no one was allowed to enter. This
man had cut the wires causing electric current through the fence. Cut it open in a
way he could enter. Inside the hut, He finds shotguns and its ammo. A forest guard
enters the hut points his gun at the man and says "it's forbidden to enter this
place". The man replies "It's forbidden for the people of the kingdom but I'm an out-
sider" he laughs and shoots the guard using shot gun which he had found inside the
hut. The man starts laughing loudly as of something had got inside him. When more
forest guards begin to come near the hut the man starts running and goes to the road
where his friend stood waiting for him. His friend, named Henry, asks "Did you go in-
side the hut?". The man replies "Yes but a forest guard came and I had to run". Henry
and the man drive to the David fort, now a museum to look at the history of the
place. For entry they had to fill a form giving their names. The man's name is re-
vealed to be Joseph. Joseph finds a father from the David Church standing outside the
museum and asks him "Father, here there are only inscriptions on the ancestors of the
kingdom, where are details of the last descendant Jackson David II son of Jackson
David I? How did the both Jacksons die?". The Father Francis responds "Jackson David
II or Jackie, we used to call him was killed by the forest devil. Jackson David I or
Jack, his father died in an accident later the same year". Joseph asks "Who is the
forest Devil?". Francis responds "We don't know who he is but after Jack's death the
forest devil has not killed anyone. There are few people saying that Jack was the one
who eliminated the Forest devil by becoming the Devil of the fortress while some be-
lieve Jack is the forest devil and Devil of the fortress". Joseph thanks the father
for the information and decides to tent in the forest near the David River. Henry was
looking at his phone when suddenly, Joseph felt something in his head as if someone
was calling him. His eyes become red, face sweating. There was a sharp stick near the
campfire. Joseph takes the stick and slices it through Henry's throat killing him.
Joseph shouts "I am the new Forest Devil!". Next day, the forest guards find Henry's
body near the camp and Joseph sitting beside his body. The forest guards take him and
ask "Who killed your friend?". Joseph pulls out a Cleaver and cuts the forest guards
head and shouts "I killed him". Joseph in anger and face filled with blood he picks
the cleaver and starts to walk towards the David's kingdom. One by one whomever
Joseph saw in front of him were killed. People in panic run to their home took what-
ever ornaments and cash they had and start to flee from the kingdom. Francis let a
few people inside the church and closes the doors to the Church. Few people get into
a bus and left for the Snowy mountains called the 'Frostwood Valley'. The Capital of
David's kingdom was 'Dark Valley Range' or simply 'Dark Valley'. People leave to the
places they could go as soon as possible away from Dark Valley and Joseph's lunatic
behaviour. Joseph was completely in rogue he broke open houses and vehicles trying to
find people of David's kingdom from 'Dark Valley'.
A Few men reach the Frostwood valley and try to find some shelter with the money they
have. While walking they find a man aged 55, who looked familiar to them standing on
the balcony of a house. One man from the crowd walks to the house and to his shock,
the man looked like Jackson David I aka Jack. The man approaches near the lookalike
of Jack and says "Oh King! You have been here the whole time. You didn't come to save
us!". The lookalike replies "I am not a king, my name is George Gate". Disappointed,
the man walks in search of shelter. George runs towards the families who were search-
ing for shelter and asks them to stay at his home. Happy with George's comment all of
them move to George's house. When everyone had settled, George asks one of the men
"Why did you people leave your hometown?". The man replies "My name is Jacob. We are
from the Dark valley. Our valley had seen two serial killers before, the Forest Devil
and The devil of the Fortress. Our King Jack who was considered either one of the
Devil, we don't know which one, died in a Car accident after which all the serial
killings had stopped. Now, An outsider named Joseph has claimed himself to be the
Forest Devil started a killing spree on whomever he saw from the Dark valley. To save
our lives we took what we have and left the place. And you look like our King who
Died". George listening to this tells "Micheal died, the forest Devil died! How is
this possible?". Jacob shouts "You are Jack!, you left the Dark Valley and left us in
darkness!". George shouts "Yes I am Jack! And I am the Devil of the Fortress who just
wanted to find the killer of his son. The Forest Devil was Micheal the descendant of
the Forbidden family of our kingdom!". Jacob says "You just go back and save our
kingdom, you are the King". Jack ignores the comment and says "You all can stay here
until you get a Shelter". Meanwhile, At the Dark Valley, the roads are filled with
blood splashes all over. Joseph walking all over the place finding the people belong-
ing to the kingdom. Francis had kept people safe in the church and Joseph was now on
the way to the Church. Joseph walking slowly to the Church. Francis through the win-
dow sees Joseph walking towards the church with the cleaver body soaked with red
blood. Joseph reaches the door of the church and knocks it. Knocks it harder, harder
each time. All the people seeking shelter in the church scared and in panic. Joseph
takes the cleaver and cuts the door. One cut after another. Suddenly the knocking and
the cuts stopped. Francis looked at the door. The door suddenly breaks open. Joseph
falling down. Jack stood in front of Joseph who had fallen down and looks at him.
Joseph grabs the cleaver, attempting to stab Jack. Jack holds Joseph's hand and

ily, Jack takes Joseph into his car and drives to the underground basement near the

have to clean this place". Joseph shouts "You are the Devil of the Fortress, You are
Jackson David I". Jack meets Joseph's gaze, his expression a mix of weariness and de-
termination. "Call me Jack," he responds, 'but there's more to the story than ti-
tles". Joseph looks down at the floor filled with blood. Joseph panics and tries to
remove the knot. Jack shouts "You take the knot out, You will never be seen again and
to say the truth, I am The Devil of the Fortress". Jack asks "What do you remember
the last?". Joseph says "I was in the Hut in the middle of the forest, after that I
don't remember anything!". Jack replies "You are now being controlled by Black magic
then!, Michael's family used it to preserve their legacy in black magic as from the
Diary". The Diary with the prophecy of Jack's ancestors which was burnt that day when
Micheal, still burning in the corner of the room. Micheal that day, was tied up the
same way Joseph is tied now, glimpse of the cleaver being thrown by Micheal to the
Diary and the Diary starts to burn.
[Interval]
Francis brings all the people from the church outside. The Dark valley had rivers of
blood flowing through the roads. Francis takes some Holy water and starts to sprinkle
it all over the Valley. Houses were broken, buildings were in ruins. Silence is some-
thing that prevailed in the valley. Joseph looks at Jack and says "Leave me alone!, I

ter treatment, Jack asks the people of Dark valley "My Dear Subjects, This place is
hell. Let's stop all of this here and go to Frostwood valley. All of the other people
are there, in my home. Don't consider it as a order or demand, take it as a request
of your king. Joseph ain't going to stop here". Listening to Jack everyone starts to

At Frostwood Valley
People start settling in Jack's house. Jacob comes towards Jack and asks "Will we
never be able to go back home?". Jack doesn't reply and shakes his head. A postman
comes to Jack's house and gives Francis a letter. The Letter was to George Gate.
Francis asks Jack "Who is George Gate?". Jack replies "I am Jackson David I of Dark
Valley, few months before the death of my son Jackson David II, I started building
this house with the name George Gate, after the death of my son and forest devil
'Micheal', I wanted to be away from royalty and every privilege and I took the Alias
of George Gate of Frostwood Valley forever". The Letter was from Dark Valley, Joseph
had written it " Dear George Gate, My brother Micheal was recieving Threat Calls from

Jack runs and locks the door once all had gone out though the window was broken.
Joseph starts to hit Jack with the hammer. Jack falls down bleeding. Jack tries to
get up but Joseph hits him again. Jack falls unconscious. Joseph walks out of Jack's
house and shouts "I 'Joseph' spare the people of Dark valley. I will be back if you
give your King a honorific cremation, You all will die because I'll be Back!". Joseph
starts walking towards the Frostwood Mountains. Jack pulls out a First-aid kit from
his house and bandages himself. Walks out and asks the people what happened, people
happy that Jack is Alive decide to keep the news he is alive a secret. Jack heals
slowly.
Few Months Later
Joseph comes to Jack's house in Frostwood Valley. He asks Francis "Father, what hap-
pened to Jack's Body after his death?". Francis stood silent. Joseph enters into the
house though people try to stop him from getting inside. Jack comes down from first
floor. Joseph is shocked and angry because he never checked if Jack was alive. Jack
pushes Joseph outside the house and locks the door. Joseph finds an axe outside
Jack's house. He takes it and cuts open the locked door and breaks in. Joseph runs
behind Jack. Francis catches Joseph. Joseph unable to relieve himself stabs Francis.
Joseph's eyes turn red and starts to show psychic tendencies like biting his teeth
and eyes wide open. Jack pulls out a gun from the drawer and shoots Joseph. Joseph
falls down Dead. Police arrive at Jack's house and Jack is arrested for killing
Joseph. Jack is sentenced for 8 years in prison and before that 2 months for a psy-
chological therapy. Jack there gets to know about Micheal, Joseph and their family.
Micheal and Joseph belonged to the Forbidden Family of Dark Valley. Micheal and
Joseph's Father was sent out of the Valley when he was too young though his parents
were stuck in the Hut in the middle of the Forest. Micheal's Father Zachariah aka
Zach was a worker for a small business company in the Frostwood city when people
started getting to know about Zach's past as a member of the Forbidden Family. Zach
was fired from his job. Due to this frustration, Zach suicides. Micheal and Joseph
were small kids when Zach died. Thinking Suicide is not the correct way, Micheal and
Joseph's mother raised them. The bedtime stories for Micheal and Joseph was how their
family turned forbidden creating hatred to the David Kings in the young hearts. When
they grew up Micheal, after losing their mother now, with at most hatred decided to
finish the last member of the David Family 'Jackson David II aka Jackie' by becoming
his friend and pull his plan off at Dark Valley, later they meet Jack during the Van
accident. Before he went to Dark Valley Dr.Xavier was their psychologist. For taking
the revenge for Joseph's brother Michael's death, Joseph goes back to Dark Valley to
kill each one from the David Kingdom. Dr.Xavier was also the person treating Jack
now. After listening to this story which had started before Jack's knowledge Jack de-
clared himself as the 'Devil of the Fortress' clearing all his deeds. Jack goes to
prison for 8 years. Meanwhile, the people who came from Dark Valley to Frostwood
Valley return back to their homes. Father Francis Dies after getting stabbed by
Joseph. The Dark Valley gets its light back. Everything was back to normal. David
fort started getting Moss grown all over it. The people of Dark Valley thinking the
Hut in the forest as the root cause of all problems blasts the hut.
8 years later
It was a rainy night. Dogs of Dark valley starts barking at a man walking on the
road. Jacob comes out with a torch. On's the torch to look at the man's face. Jacob
runs out without caring it is raining outside. The man was none other than Jackson
David I aka George Gate. Jack says to Jacob "Some things never change if you are a
king; You remain one. If you are a saviour; you remain one. If you are the devil; you
remain one. The only thing that changes is the respect you get and the thing you did
to most people maybe good or bad- La seule chose qui reste jusqu'à la fin est le re-
spect que vous obtenez en tant que sauveur". Jack continues "I am a Devil! and so are
you all".
The End
Written by Nivedh Sunil

THE SAVIOUR : The Echoes of Redemption
It's like you have to save your own life, nobody is going to be a saviour for
you, so we have to do what we have to do, no matter what it is.
Rainy night
A matador F307 is going through a forest. 4 friends are in the van. One is
singing song, the other playing guitar. The other two were in the front seat
one driving and the other speaking on his phone. A truck comes opposite to
the van. The van turns and hits a tree. All 4 get down. They were injured.
Smoke was coming out of the engine. They try fixing it and were unsuccessful.
They decide to stay there for the night and get into their car. One guy gets
a call from the name George Gate. When his friends asked he called George
Gate as a gangstar from the mountains. "He is trying to kill me. I don't know
for what. I am trying to tell him it's a wrong number. He ain't just leaving
me even for an instant".
Next day
Their phone's batteries had died and could not call anyone. There were light
showers. A car comes near their van. They ask to stop the car. The car stops.
The man comes out. He was about 45-50 years old. The man who was driving the
van introduces himself "My name is Robert and these are my friends. Our van
hit a tree and is repaired. Could you please help us". The man replies "My
phone is out of battery. If you want I can drop you nearby and ask for some
help". They agree and enter his car. The man introduces himself as Jackson
David. The singer introduces him as Arjun, the guitarist Dev and the last one
as Michael. Jackson asks where they were going. Robert replies saying "We
were going to David fort. We also had a friend with your name Jackson David".
Jackson asks "what do you mean by you had a friend?". Arjun replies "he is no
more.". Dev asks where Jackson was going. Jack replies "Sometimes we might go
to the same place with the people you might not know. You are going to a fu-
neral with a guitar?". Dev replies "It was a guitar given by Jackie on my
birthday and we were singing his favourite song while we were coming. How are
you related to Jackie?". Jack says Jackie is his son.
They reach David Fort
Dev asks "what should we do with our van if we already reached here?". Jack
says he had already arranged and the van has been sent for repair. During the
funeral, Dev takes the guitar and keeps it next to Jackie's body. There were
many visitors from places Jackie had gone. After the funeral got over Jack
asks the 4 to stay in their home untill their van had got repaired. They tell
him "We had come here once while you were away. We stayed in the forest for a
day. If we could get a tent for the day would be nice to reminiscent that day
with Jackie. Later tomorrow we will be back." Jack says he would like to join
them. Jack asked nobody from his bodyguards to accompany him like the days he
goes for a drive alone.
That night
There was slight rainfall. They were in the middle of the forest. Their camp-
fire had been lit before the rain had started. They eat their meal and go to
sleep. Jack was with Dev and Arjun, Robert and Michael were in another tent.
Jack wakes up hearing some sound. Arjun was asleep. Jack searches for dev. He
enters the other tent and Robert was asleep. Michael and Dev were missing. He
hears someone speaking behind a tree. Jack silently slips his body behind the
tree. Jack pulls out his gun from his back. It was Michael's voice. Jack
slides in front of Michael pointing his gun. Michael was on phone. A gun shot
is heard. Michael and Jack runs towards the tent. Arjun was shot. Robert
comes running from his tent. Dev comes running from one side. Dev and Robert
points at Jack's gun and blames Jack for shooting Arjun. Michael tries to
clear them but they start blaming Michael and Jack stating they had teamed in
killing Arjun. Jack pulls out his ammo and shows that his gun is fully loaded
and has not shot any bullet from that. All of them were confused. Jack says
he had come out to search where Michael and Dev were. Dev says "This whole
forest is cursed. Last time Jackie got shot before that Rony got shot. Now
Arjun." Jack "You knew how my son died and you didn't tell anybody and left
the place quietly. We searched 5 days to get his body in the forest. I knew
something was strange after Jackie and Rony's death. That's the reason i ac-
companied you". Dev replies "we wanted to stay away from problems and further
cases. That's why we left quietly". Jack hears these and asks "Why do you
guys after 2 deaths want to come here again and again?". Michael replies "af-
ter Rony's death we thought it might be another reason. After Jackie's death
we wanted to investigate after its case's heat had reduced". Jack pulls out
his gun and shoots Dev and Robert. Jack pulls out a Cigar from his pocket and
starts smoking. Michael in shock asks "Why did you kill them both". Jack
replies "I hate liers. I overheard them planning to kill Arjun. I wanted to
know if you were in the plan. But no you ain't". Michael faints. Jack puts
Micheal in his back seat and starts to drive his car. He turns towards David
fort. He sees that all his bodyguards had died. Someone had poisoned them. He
comes out gets in his car. Jack turns towards another road leading to a ceme-
tery. He stops his car just after the cemetery gets over. Jack gets out of
his car and opens an underground basement. Jack brings down Michael and ties
him up on a chair. It was a dark room. Jack on's the light, Pours water on
Michael's face. Michael wakes up. Looks around. There was blood all over the
floor. Jack grabs 2 cleavers and starts to sharpen them. Jack grabs an apron
with blood stains on it. Michael asks "Where did you bring me?". Jack says
"Stay quiet!". There was a body on the table. It was Dev's body. Beside it
there was another table with Robert's body packed in polyethylene. Micheal
keeps 1 cleaver down and cuts Dev's body. Michael is in shock. The blood
splashing all over the place and Micheal's face. Micheal puts the pieces in a
sack. He open's the polyethylene and starts cutting Robert's body into
pieces. Puts them in another sack. Takes his car and goes near a river open
the sack and throw it such that it floats.
Meanwhile
Micheal opens the knot. Looks through the area. The door was locked. He
open's the cupboards and finds a diary in one. Micheal opens the previous day
note "Jackson David tue Dev et Robert". On the same day it was written "La
force de David n'est plus" below it written "David, ses rois et ses sujets
devront faire face à une menace qui aura un impact durable sur le royaume de
David". Micheal reads and in shock drops the book down. The door behind him
opens. Jack was back. Micheal grabs the cleaver from the table ready to at-
tack Jack. Jack enters. Micheal throws the cleaver. Jack sees it and closes
the door. The cleaver gets stuck on the door. Jack slam opens the door. Jack
runs grabs a cleaver goes to attack Micheal, when he sees the diary fallen
down, Jack drops the cleaver. Jack says "This book was written by our ances-
tors in our local language but later it was translated by some french
philosophists". Jack grabs the book and says ""Le dernier descendant de la
famille de David est tué" - this was last week". Jack opens today's date page
and tells "This was not here the whole time. From where did this come "Le
royaume de David a son roi solitaire qui sauvera les jours sombres traversant
le royaume" it was not here the whole time". Micheal says "even I had not
seen it here. Today is the last day in the book. They made diary kind of book
with this year's dates written on it". A man enters the room. Jack grabs the
cleaver fallen down, jumps and cuts his head apart blood splashing on Jack's
face. Jack has blood all over face. He leans over to the wall and sits on the
ground. Throws the cleaver towards the book. The book starts burning.
[Interval]
Micheal pulls out the cleaver from the door and looks at Jack. "More bad days
are yet to come. You did plan something" Micheal says. Jack looks at Micheal.
Michael throws the cleaver towards Jack. Jack catches the cleaver. Jack says
"Are you with me?". Micheal "Yes". Cops are investigating the bodyguards
death at David fort. Jack and Micheal are called for interrogation. Jack says
"I don't know how. I took Micheal to the doctor as he wasn't well. When I re-
turned all of my bodyguards were dead". The police asks Micheal about his
friends. Michael responds saying "I was not feeling well my friends planned
reminiscing old times by camping in the forest. I couldn't go. I don't know
why they haven't arrived yet". The police man says "So your friends have gone
camping in that forest during the night were the people who die. And they
haven't arrived yet. People who went missing only few bodies have returned
the rest bodies went missing or were declared missing. I don't think they
will be back. Even though we will send a squad to check for your friends. How
did they go till there?". Jack replies "I sent a car to drop till wherever
they want and the car came back after leaving them within an hour".
Next day
The police informs Jack that Micheal's friends are missing and tells that he
also knows they won't be back. "The Forest Devil" on that day's newspaper
"People who enter the forest during the night. Only few return alive and only
few bodies arrive. The mystery seems a mystery even for the cops" were the
headlines. Jack asks Micheal to stay at fort and takes his car and leaves.
Evening when he was back, he found out that Micheal is missing. Jack takes
his car and goes to the forest. He finds a car of his, on the side of the
road. Jack gets down his car and goes inside the forest. He hears a sound.
Jack hides behind a tree and peeps. It was Micheal. Some tourists had entered
the forest. It was late evening around 5.45pm. Micheal grabs a cleaver and
cuts each one's throat apart. Micheal goes towards a small Hut in between the
forest which was considered forbidden. Cleans the cleaver. Turns back. He
sees Jack sitting on the chair. Micheal says "So you found out our.......
Sorry my little secret". Jack replies "I knew you and your friends were doing
this the whole time. I left you till the end because it was your forest".
Micheal says "We were the forbidden family of your kingdom. We started the
Forest Devil. Later my friends Robert and Dev joined me. Your son too got to
know about this. But sad we had to kill him before he could say anything to
anyone". Jack replies "You are the forest devil but I am the Devil of the
fortress. King of this kingdom. I also killed many and have flushed their
bodies through the river. I killed them because they were violating the rules
of the Forest. For you I give a last opportunity Micheal, finish it right now
and leave this kingdom for good or else I'll make you leave this kingdom for
good". Jack gets in his car and goes towards the fort. Micheal brings back
the car to the fort and leaves. "I am the Devil. Only one of a kind" Micheal
turns back. Jack hits him with his car.
Micheal wakes up in the same room "The underground basement" tied to a wooden
chair. Micheal shouts "Open this knot. I was leaving this kingdom. Now
what?". Jack replies "Once started cannot be finished so easily. I have expe-
rience". Micheal replies "Even you can't stop killing people. We are of same
kind. We are psychopaths whose paths have crossed eachother. You untie me! I
will save the whole kingdom". Jack replies "I and my ancestors couldn't save
the kingdom which became now a heritage site for many. I'm still living there
because of my family reputation. Every day visitors come to the fort. 'People
Of the New Generation' only want to see that stereotypical kings and Fort
that are exquisite. I'm a king only by blood not by work or my food deeds.
Even that ain't gonna change about us we also ain't. The Fire Starts when
there is a spark. But a spark can never stop the fire, it increases its heat,
strength". Jack takes a cleaver goes to stab Micheal. Jack drops the cleaver,
Shouts "I give you 30mins to leave. Take this cleaver from ground untie your-
self and leave. It's a difficult task. I'm sparing you life for it. Take this
chance". Jack gets in his car and leaves to fort. Jack eats dinner. Micheal
arrives at the fort. Grabs a fire torch outside the fort wall and searches
for Jack. Jack was in his room. Micheal stands behind Jack. Jack looks at the
reflection of Micheal on his mirror. Micheal tries to hit Jack with the
torch. Jack dodges the hit. Kicks Micheal. Micheal drops to the ground. Jack
punches Micheal. Micheal pushes Jack and rushes down the fort and gets in a
car. Jack follows him with another car. Jack races behind Micheal. Micheal
gets down the car and enters the forest. Forest guards were on duty that
night. The forest guards were ordered to shoot anyone they see in the forest
that night, animals to humans. Micheal in panic bumps into a forest guard.
Micheal had the cleaver tucked into his pants, which falls down. The forest
guard looks at the cleaver and aims at Micheal. Micheal starts running from
the forest guards. Jack was standing near the car with a cigar in this mouth
waiting. Micheal was in danger. Forest guards shooting Micheal and missing
it. Finally Micheal gets hit by a bullet on his shoulder bone. Micheal enters
his Hut in the forest. Micheal grabs his shotgun from the hut. Starts shoot-
ing the forest guards. He shoots all. Only 2 of them escape. Micheal goes be-
hind those 2 forest guards. The forest guard shoots at Micheal's hand.
Micheal in full range shoots the guard. By that time one guard had reached
the road and escaped. Micheal reaches the road where Jack is standing in
front of him. Micheal points the shotgun at Jack. Jack grabs his gun and
shoots his stomach. Jack goes to Micheal and says "You know why I shot your
stomach because once a wise man said ' It's like you have to save your own
life, nobody is going to be a saviour for you, so we have to do what we have
to do, no matter what it is. ' Which once started will have to end. Mine ends
with you". Jack shoots Micheal's head. Puts Jack's body in his car back seat.
Burns the car in which Micheal came. Jack starts his car and goes full speed
230km/h in his car and hits a rock. David fort is burning, Gas had leaked and
the torch helped the gas burn the fort.
[Showing past of Jack]
Jack had bought a house away from royalty for his son Jackie. He used to go
there frequently maintaining and arranging the new building house. Jack
didn't want royalty. He just wanted a peacefull life for him and his son.
After his son had passed away, Jack went for depression causing him a trau-
matic situation where he suspect anyone. The only way he could come out was
find his son's killer. He turned himself into the same kind of psychopath
just to find the killer of his son. He found him and successfully executed
him. His sins were paid with his death. "The great king from David Family
'King Jackson David' is no more. He saved the entire Kingdom and its people
risking his life and finally dying hit by a truck and his face flayed. May he
rest in peace!".
[That night when Jack was over speeding]
Jack reduces the speed. Gets down the car. keeps a stone on the accelerator.
Car starts moving down the road hitting a rock. Jack turns a truck hits him.
Body's face was flayed.
Jack looks at the truck driver taking Micheal's body thinking it was Jack's.
Jack completely blood bathed and exhausted gets a bus covering his face
leaves to a area filled with snow. Jack stays there with the name 'George
Gate'. He says "Somethings never change if you are a king, You remain one. If
you are a saviour, you remain one. If you are the devil, you remain one. The
only thing that changes is the respect you get and the name of the thing you
did to most people- La seule chose qui reste jusqu'à la fin est le respect
que vous obtenez en tant que sauveur".
The saviour
[A few years later]
The hut in the forest covered with overgrown moss and vines. A man walks to-
wards the hut. Breaks open the door. Enters inside. The hut was a electric
fenced property where nobody was allowed to enter. This man had cut the wires
causing electric current through the fence. Cut it open in a way he could en-
ter. Inside the hut, He finds shotguns and it's ammo. A forest guard enters
the hut points his gun at the man and says "it's forbidden to enter this
place". The man replies "It's forbidden for the people of the kingdom but I'm
an outsider" he laughs and shoots the gun pointing the shot gun at the forest
guard. The man laughs loudly.

The South Side Story
"High Shine Appartment, situated in Bangalore East. It will be almost near from your
workplace. What do you say?" Asked Manu To Jay. Jay replies "I'm fine with any area,
but traffic should be less while commuting". Manu replies "There is no place in
Bangalore without traffic! And the place our office is, is the place filled with
traffic!". Jay responds "Okay fine! I'll buy a 3BHK appartment in there! I can buy an
appartment instead of paying huge rent in Bangalore". Jay aka Jay Mohan, son of Mohan
and Maya had been living with his Friend and Colleague Manu since two years after
getting a job in Bangalore, and leaving his hometown Kerala. He was working as aIT
professional in IBM. Jay finalizes the appartment and shifts there. He Lived on 4th
floor. Daily, early morning he used to go for a walk around the appartment and the
park inside the appartment. People in the appartment thought he was too Arrogant as
he never spoke to anyone in the appartment, he used to not even smile at the people
who were smiling at him. He left for his work at 9 am.
At office, Jay shares sweet for buying a new appartment. Manu, Seetha and Rajguru
were his friends at work. Seetha Liked Jay and Jay knowing about this, usually kept a
distance from her. Rajguru said "So when is the party?". Jay replies "I just gave you
sweets! What else do you guys want as a treat?". Manu said "We want alcohol party".
Jay replies "Okay! Let's go to a nearby place tonight". After the party, Jay reaches
his appartment. His house number was 409. Jay completely drunk reaches in front of
410 and tries to open the door. The lock wasn't opening, as he was drunk, he tried to
push open the door. Suddenly, the door opens and Jay falls inside. A girl stood
shocked. Jay looks at the girl and says "Nice girl!". The girl's father comes up to
the door and asks "Who are you?". Jay inturn asks "You are in my House! Who are you?"
Quirkily. The man tells "You're that boy next door, right? You came inside the wrong
door, you are in 410!". Jay gets up and silently walks and slips, the man comes and
holds him. Jay looks at the house name "Mr. Manoj and Family". Jay then looks at the
man and tells "You are Manoj?". Manoj replies "Yes, I am Manoj, your neighbour!". Jay
opens the door of his house and enters inside. Manoj helps Jay get onto his bed and
comes out. Next day, Jay goes for walk and Manoj comes in front of him. Manoj asks
"What happened to you yesterday? You broke into my house and were flirting with my
daughter Raya". Jay's face gets red and says "Sorry Sir! I just came in here, and had
a party yesterday. That is why I, by mistake I came in". Manoj pats Jay's back and
says "Don't worry, when I want to drink, I'll come to your house. Don't worry, I
won't tell anyone out here". Jay smiles and nods his head. Jay then goes to his
floor. Looks at 410 and knocks the door. Raya comes out opening the door and asks
"Are you drunk again?". Jay's face gets red, he looks up and tells Raya "Look! I'm
sorry for commenting on you yesterday. I am not drunk! We had a small party yester-
day". Raya asks Jay to get inside and makes him a tea. Raya's Mother Jaya comes in
and asks "Where do you work?". Jay replies "I work in IBM. Sorry for yesterday
Aunty!". Raya was a online yoga instructor. Jay comes back home and leaves for work.
At work, Jay tells what happened the previous day to Manu, Seetha and Rajguru.
Rajguru and Manu start laughing listening to what had happened. Seetha sympathized
him and says "Manu and Rajguru, let's go to Jay's place tonight!". Manu and Rajguru
agreed for this. Later that night, Seetha reaches first to Jay's house. Manu and
Rajguru arrive late. Seetha opens the door for Many and Rajguru. Rajguru pulls out a
alcohol bottle from his back. Seetha tells "You know how much problems he got into
because of this yesterday, and now you guys are getting the same thing today?". When
Manu, Rajguru and Jay didn't listen to what she was saying, she walks out of the
house out of anger. All three get completely drunk. Manu and Rajguru after the party
decide to leave. Jay opens the door for them and stood outside waiting for them to
leave. Once they had left, Jay tries to get into his house but slips and rolls in
front of 410. He felt unconscious and slept in front of Manoj's house door. One of
the neighbour from 408, takes Jay's photo sleeping in front of 410's door and send
the photo in the appartment association group. Early morning his phone rang. It was
Jay's father Mohan. Jay was still laying in front of the door. He gets up and enters
into his room and attends the call. Mohan said "I'll be coming to Bangalore tomorrow.
First thing, I want to see your new house, but before that I'll be going to see a
girl for you for marriage, directly from railway station. I'll send you their loca-
tion and I'll call you when to come to their home!". Jay replies "Okay! Take care!"
And ends the call. Jay goes for work. Seetha asks "Stop going with this Manu and
Rajguru! They will make you drunk and ruin your life!". Jay responds "We were just
enjoying, Once or twice is my limit!". Seetha replies "I want to say you something,
Can you come and meet me evening at the coffee shop?". Jay agrees and looks at
Rajguru's face. Rajguru was making faces at him. Jay reaches the coffee shop in the
evening. Seetha comes in and they both order a coffee. Seetha tells "I don't know how
to start, but I really have a bit concern for you! Stop drinking! And I want to say-
". Jay interrupts and says "I know that you like me, but this ain't going to happen.
I can only see you as a friend!". Seetha gets emotional and Jay tries to console her.
Seetha gets angry, picks up her bag and leaves. Jay goes behind her, but she gets
into her car and leaves. Jay goes back in and the ordered coffee comes onto the ta-
ble. Jay tells to the waiter "Cancel my order!". The waiter replies "You should have
cancelled before we were making it, now you have to pay for this!". Jay takes the
coffee in a takeaway bag and gets into his car and leaves back home. After reaching
home he was sad for speaking to Seetha in such a rude manner. Jay keeps the coffee in
the refrigerator and opens his phone to see message of him sleeping on the floor at
the walkway in front of 410's door. The whole association was angry except a few,
mainly Manoj and family. Jay calls Manoj into his house. Both start drinking and get
completely drunk. Manoj after some time goes back to his house. Jay goes to lock the
door and this time falls in front of his door 409. Early morning, few guests arrive
at 410. It was Mohan, Maya and Jay's brother Rahul. Jay kept his face down and was in
a deep sleep. Rahul looks down and tells to Mohan "It looks like your son, his body
looks the same!". Maya replies "Your brother doesn't drink and if he has too, why
would he sleep down here? He has a own house!". Rahul murmurs to himself "She has not
seen her son drinking". Just out of curiosity, Rahul tries to wake the unknown man
up. Mohan, Maya and Rahul and shocked seeing Jay laying on the floor drunk. Jay looks
at his parents and brother is shocked. Jay gets up and opens his door and asks them
"How did you get to know my address?". Mohan tells "We didn't know where you live,
but the marriage broker gave this address of the girl. She lives in 410 and her name
is Raya!". Jay scratches his head. Mohan continues "When did you start drinking?".
Jay replies "I didn't drink I was tired and I slipped and fell down!". Mohan tells
"If you slipped and fell down out of tiredness, good, but if you fell down drunk, you
will see another face of mine!". Jay gets into his room, Takes a bath and comes out
before going to Manoj's home for the initial meeting. After some time, taking rest,
they go to Manoj's home for meeting Raya along with Jay. Jay looks at Manoj and makes
faces to not tell the truth about his drinking. Meena and Jaya go inside the kitchen.
Mohan and Manoj spoke about their children and Raya and Jay were sent to speak alone.
Jaya meanwhile shows Maya Jay's picture sleeping on the floor and a video of him
drinking with Manoj. Maya takes the photos and videos and shows it to Mohan. Mohan
and Maya gets angry but kept quiet. When Jay and Raya came out, Mohan and Maya kept
quiet. Manoj tells to Raya "Are you ok in marrying Jay?". Raya replies "He told me,
he likes me a lot. He is a unique character!". Manoj looks and Mohan and says "Though
your son drinks, he is well disciplined and has a good character and I am happy to
fix an alliance with your family". Mohan gets slightly happy listening to this. Mohan
and Manoj then exchange plates and fix Jay and Raya's Marriage.
[Interval]
Manu mockingly "Not even a week in the appartment and a arranged love marriage next
door!". Jay stayed quiet. Seetha goes to Jay and says "I've been working with you and
I am your friend for two years and you couldn't tell me about the girl next door?".
Rajguru tried to stop Seetha from getting angry. Seetha replied "Even I found another
boy! He just came in for an interview and will join for work tomorrow!". Jay reaches
home and Maya says "Go ask your brother how his interview went!". Jay replies "It's
his interview! Why would I ask him. I am very tired and am going to sleep!". Jay goes
into his room. Jay thought with himself "If my parents got to know I Drunk, by now it
should have been an issue!". Jay takes out a cigarette from his pocket and starts
smoking in his balcony. It was a joint balcony, so one could get inside from another
room. Mohan comes to the balcony from another room and finds Jay smoking. Mohan re-
moves his slipper silently and throws it on Jay. The slipper hits on Jay's face and

THE VIOLENT FUTURE
A two-story house stood in an area with empty space on both its left and right sides.
A few houses were situated opposite to this one. It was a rainy night, and the area
was surrounded by walls behind the house and to the left. More houses could be found
if one ventured to the right of the house. The house was isolated for about 3-4 plots
of land, with the next chain of houses beginning further down the lane. There was
only one road leading to this area. It was a rainy night. The owner of the house
Sanjay Samuel aged 35-40, comes out to lock his gate. The house had 2 gates. One gate
gave direct opening for the Sanjay's house and the bigger one gave way for the stairs
and car porch where the Sanjay's car had been stopped. He goes to lock the bigger one
when he hears the sound of someone from the next compound, opposite to his house try-
ing to break the wall. The owner thought it was the crackling sound of the thunder
ignores it locks all the gate and goes to sleep. In late midnight he hears sound of
his main door opening. Sanjay wakes up. Suddenly his room door opens. A man with a
gun in his hand enters the room and shouts "Give me whatever cash, gold and mainly
your phone". Sanjay walks hands raised up removes his phone from charge and gives it
to the robber. The robber looks at the phone and says "Button phone?!". By the time
the robber looks at Sanjay's face, Sanjay punches the robber on face. The robber
falls down. Sanjay dials 100. The police reaches the place to see the robber tied
outside the house gate with a letter saying "I have to go to office tomorrow early
morning as I have a meeting. I'll reach the police station by evening, I'm going to
sleep now and my gate is locked kindly arrest the robber considering this my state-
ment. -Sanjay Samuel (with sign)". The police catches the robber and puts him in
lockup.
Sanjay wakes up in the morning goes to work. He attends the meeting and takes half
day leave and goes to the police station. Sanjay enters the police station and asks a
constable "Police had caught a robber in my home today morning. I would like to raise
the FIR for it. Where should I go?". The constable says "There was no robbers caught
today morning. Can you check any other police station". According to Sanjay's knowl-
edge he had called the police station he had just entered. He goes to all nearby po-
lice stations and there was no robber caught. Sanjay goes back home in a mixed emo-
tion. He reaches his house. There were many people standing outside his house. All
looked like they had come to hit somebody. Sanjay stops his car in a distance from
his house and starts walking towards his house to ask to clear the crowd. The robber
was standing out of Sanjay's house with a hammer in his hand. The robber says "My
name is Amar Raj. This is my local friends who work with me in different localities.
You put me in jail. Now, I put you to death". Sanjay runs towards his car. Amar's men
start to chase him. Sanjay opens his car trunk. He throws the spare tyre burning it
using petrol from a extra petrol box from car towards the men. He grabs a bolt span-
ner and starts running behind the men to hit them. Sanjay starts hitting the men and
finally reach in front of Amar and says "This is your last day!". Sanjay takes the
spanner hit the rest of Amar's men. He kills Amar and He surrenders to police unknow-
ing the further consequences. Sanjay was fired after he got mingled with a murder
case. He was found guilty and sent to jail for 7 years even though he had killed Amar
for self defence.
7 years later
Sanjay comes out of jail. He decided to go for work. Nobody was ready to give a job
for him when he found an advertisement in a newspaper "Job vacancy, we would not ask
you your name or details. We just need an employee and we give monthly salary of 3
lakhs". Sanjay immediately joins in that work. The gave a box. Sanjay opened his lap-
top for 2 weeks and there was not a single mail regarding what work he had to do.
After 2 weeks, he got a mail stating
"Assignment 1:
(photo of a man)
main target should be killed with in 7 days.
Note:If not killed you will be killed on the 8th day.
Location of target: Milan, Italy
Tickets have been attached in this mail. Gun in the box right next to you. It's for
self defence, the gun you need will be given by Dev, Field executive.
Time starts: Exactly when you land at Milan"
In Milan, Italy
Sanjay says "Am I an assassin who has been sent for an assassination" to himself. A
man approaches Sanjay and says "You are Sanjay Assassin level: Amateur. My name is
Dev. I also work in your same company as field executive". Sanjay shakes hand and
goes to the hotel room at 16th floor. Dev gives Sanjay a sniper and says "I have been
ordered to give information about the target and you have to plot the plan to kill
him". Sanjay asks dev "Where will The target Christopher Edward be now?". Dev replies
"He is in the 8th floor of our hotel". Sanjay makes a plan to kill him the same day
itself. Christopher will go to a party that evening. He will use the hotel taxi. Dev
will be the driver for it. The speakers in the trunk must be removed so that Sanjay
can sit in the car's trunk and clean headshot Christopher. According to this plan
Christopher does the same things and takes an hotel taxi where Dev was the driver.
Sanjay takes his gun and tries to shoot but water comes out of hit. Christopher turns
back to see Sanjay hiding in the trunk of the car. Christopher pulls Sanjay to the
seat. Sanjay falls down of the back seat of the car. Christopher pulls out a gun from
his over coat. Sanjay starts kicking Christopher on his face. Christopher drops the
gun. Dev starts driving the car fast. Sanjay grabs the gun. Christopher open the door
and jumps. Dev drifts the car and takes a reverse turn. Sanjay comes out of the car.
Christopher starts running and his hit by a speed moving truck and blood is splashed
all over. Christopher's body turned into particles. Dev points a gun at Sanjay and
says "I am the field superviser of Assassination and co. We assassinate people who
find about our organisation. We bring prisoners who are in parole or left from jail.
Give them an assignment and kill them after the assassination has been completed. I'm
not only field supervisor but also the Managing director and the Assassin No.1 level:
professional. Now you are going to die". Sanjay says "My name is Sanjay aka Sanjay
Samuel. Used to work in an IT company but was fired after attempting a murder. You
just know this about me. Kill me!" Dev reloads his gun and starts shooting Sanjay un-
til the round gets over. Sanjay starts laughing and says "You know something called
Bullet proof vest". Sanjay takes his gun at head shots Dev. Dev dies. Dev's phone
starts to ring. Sanjay attends and hears "Our company has been here for many years,
Dev you did a good job killing Sanjay who killed our Gangstar Mark's brother Amar
Raj". Sanjay says "If I didn't know about Mark was better. My name is Sanjay Samuel
Inspector of Police who was on an investigative mission find Mark 'Mark Raj'. My pri-
mary target was to find Mark raj and you finally have given me his details. Thank
you". Sanjay cuts the call and throws the phone in a trash can. Sanjay calls to
Indian police department and says "Mark lives in Milan. But his brother Amar being a
robber and he being a gangstar doesn't match. I need proper details about it the day
I reach India". Sanjay walks towards his hotel packs his bag and waits for his flight
at airport when he gets a call. Sanjay picks the call and hears "hello Mr. Sanjay
Samuel. You have been undercover for more than 10 years now. I guess you should re-
ally look back because me Mark Raj is on his way to kill you!". Sanjay laughs and
says "You are scared that's why you are hiding in Milan. If you have true intentions
to kill me, Kill me in India" and cuts the call. Sanjay calls Indian police and says
"Mark Raj will arrive anytime in india keep a track as I have put petrol on his fire
to kill me".
[INTERVAL]
Sanjay was being chased by many people. Sanjay's face soaked in blood. Sanjay runs
down the lanes of Delhi. All of the men holding hammers, sickle and crowbars to hit
and kill Sanjay. Sanjay completely in panic running here and there. Suddenly he hears
" Air India flight going from Milan City to Delhi is delayed by 2 hours". Sanjay

airport untill the plane arrives.
Next day
Sanjay reaches Delhi. He gets in a cab. Sanjay decides to have a nap till he reached
his hotel. Sanjay wakes up in a snowy area. His bags open thrown in the snow. Sanjay
starts packing back his bags. He lifts them up. His hands were cold. Legs nearly
numb. Face pale and faded due to cold. He starts walking. The atmosphere was foggy
and Sanjay could hardly see any residential or commercial areas nearby. Sanjay's

hardly knew his was midway top of a mountain. Sanjay was completely exhausted. He
fell down. The snow in the mountain started sliding. The snow took Sanjay sliding
down the mountain. Sanjay completely buried in snow could not even shout or speak.
Even if he could no one was around him to even help. After the snow sliding was over
The police came to check for any casualties. They find a shoe. Two cops runs towards

ing is mine. You keep it in your station, I will have to bomb it. Many lives will
die. My men were too foolish to forget to bring back the gun I had given Sanjay. I'm
not a terrorist. Even I am an Indian. I need to make myself safe, you get the gun I'm
waiting in hotel whose location I'll be sending you now. Take urself some time untill
this evening. Decide wisely!". Sanjay was getting treated in hospital. He had slight
concussion and numbness all over his body. Anand stops his car. He was confused
whether he has to do his duty and file an fir with the gun and kill many of his po-
lice colleagues life or give the gun and maybe risk his own life. Anand searches
Sanjay's bag to find more details of his and finds Sanjay's flight ticket. He calls
the control centre and says "This is anand Fernando I would like to know details of a
man named "Sanjay Samuel"". The control centre cop says "He is an undercover cop from
Mumbai. He is on a mission to find international don 'Mark Raj'" Anand thanks him and
cuts the call. Sanjay was feeling better now. The other cop introduces him and says
"Hi sir, my name is Tariq bhat. Anand told me you are an undercover cop". Sanjay says
in sore throat voice "Who is Anand?". Tariq says "I forgot to introduce him he and i
rescued you from the avalanche. The doctor advised you to take rest for the day and
you can leave tomorrow". Sanjay says "I guess you may take a leave now as I am better
you have more job to do right". Tariq smiles and starts leaving when he says "Not
more bigger job than you sir, you are an inspiration. You can go to any extent to
complete your mission" he salutes and leaves. Sanjay drowsy hears Tariq speaking in
phone about the gun to Anand. Sanjay sleeps and Tariq goes to station.
Meanwhile, Anand was preparing to meet Mark Raj. He took some extra guns with him for
self defence. Evening Tariq takes Sanjay's dinner and enters into the room. Sanjay
was not there in the room. Tariq asks the hospital staffs to check for Sanjay. The
staffs say that he paid the bills and had left the hospital. Anand drives towards

location right now!". Mark's location is sent to Sanjay. Sanjay starts speeding to-
wards the location in Jammu. The location was not a hotel. It was a villa kind of
building near a river. Sanjay reaches the location. Mark's men do a check over
Sanjay's body for any weapons. After nothing was found Sanjay was sent in. Anand
reaches behind him. It was a dusky evening. Anand hands over the man checking the gun
mark had asked for and he had to give the men all the guns he had taken for self-de-
fence. Mark was in the first floor. He looks down at Sanjay and says "Where has this
brought to you. You have once been a police officer, a person sent to jail, an assas-
sin and finally death. Now your death is in my hand". Sanjay sits on the sofa as he
had gave up and says "I donate my body to you (smiles) and kill me right now! I will
be proud that I did my job before dying". Mark says "Ok so be it". 2 gun shots heard.
Mark and sanjay turns towards the door. Anand had killed the men who were checking
for guns. Mark shoots at Sanjay's right hand. Sanjay punches a man using his left
hand and takes the gun the man had. Sanjay runs upstairs. Anand sees a chekhov's gun.
He grabs it, loads it and starts shooting all the men. One by one all men are killed.

starts ringing. When anand checks it is a video call saved 'bro'. He attends the call

sent to Anand. That's why I went to him. I didn't know the other location belonged to
Max raj. That's why am on my way to your location". Sanjay and Anand sit in the car.
Sanjay starts speeding. Max starts packing for going back to Milan. Max decides to
take back his brother's body and appoints 2 men to get the body. Max drives towards

killed him". Sanjay spits out blood and says "If you kill 1, many are waiting for or-
ders to kill you. Prepare yourself to die!". Max starts laughing when he is headshot.

Victor Walter
"Far duller than a serpent's tooth it is to spend a quiet youth"
Bangalore
A man holds a gun and walks into a street, he knocks a door and shows his ID and says
"I am Victor, SI, Bangalore". The man who opened the door pulls him inside and ties
Victor to a chair and says "You have made a deal with a wrong person! Ashiq would
like to see you!". Victor says "Xavier! I've come to deal with the devil himself!".
Few black cars comes in front of the door and Ashiq with a black tuxedo enters into
the house. Ashiq asks Victor "I need you to do a work, remove all my casefiles and
join me into the syndicate! I have heard many great things on how you work, your bru-
tality towards the people opposite to your ideology!". Victor says "If you know my
ideology, then we won't be doing a deal here!". Ashiq asks "What do you want?" And
asks his guards to untie Victor. Victor walks to Ashiq and says "The thing I hate the
most is humiliation! Xavier pulled me inside holding my collar!". Ashiq shouts
"Guards! Kill Xavier!". Victor stops the guards and grabs a cleaver from on of them.
He keeps the cleaver on Xavier's neck. Xavier starts to plead and starts sweating.
Victor types a resignation letter and sends it to DGP. Xavier looks at Victor's eyes,
Victor pulls the cleaver back and slices out Xavier's head from his body. All the
blood splashes on Victor's face and shirt. Ashiq starts clapping and shouts "Victor!
Welcome to my Syndicate!". Ashiq opens the car's door for Victor and he himself sits
inside.
Northern Ireland
Zack waits while Victor lands with the helicopter. Victor asks Zack "What must I do
for Ashiq's syndicate?". Ashiq used be a small time black market arms dealer in
Russia, when legalization backstabbed the black market, Ashiq started his own legal
arms dealership. Ashiq had a right hand who was Zack, who dealed with accounts and
handling. Ashiq had another business, a fake medicine business which he bought for
cheap all over the world and sold at a high rate in India with his pharmaceutical
company named 'AU pharmaceutical'. Zack says to Victor "You're brought here to deal
with arms dealer directly, If they go other way, you will kill them!". Victor asks
"So I am your Assassin?". Zack says "Yes! More like a Right hand assassin!". Zack
gives Victor a ticket to Panama for a deal and says "You just need to sit in the car
waiting outside which will take you directly to the place of meeting!".
Panama, Central America
Victor gets down from the flight and enters into the car waiting outside. The Car
driver gives Victor two guns. They reach to an old factory, the car stops outside and
Victor walks inside. Charlie, International-drug kingpin was standing in front of
Victor. Chalie says "This is an illegal arms and drug trade! How much drug do you
need for the guns I need?". Victor asks Charlie to wait and calls ,Zack. Victor says
"You told me to speak about a deal, I thought it was cash! I don't deal with drugs!
It's against my ideology!". Zack says "We are intermediary for this drug trade, we
will take drug from them and sell it to another called Karos, the African mafia and
take cash from them! Say you need 20 Tons of drugs to finalize the deal". Victor cuts
the call, confused on what was going on. Victor then says "We need 20 Tons to final-
ize the deal!". Chalie slowly walks towards Victor gives his hands and says "It was a
good deal Mr..". Victor says "Victor! Victor Walter!". Charlie hugs Victor and says
"The drugs will reach Northern Ireland, tomorrow!". Victor says "The guns will reach
Panama by next week!". Victor walks into the car and leaves back to Northern Ireland.
Northern Ireland
Night, Victor goes to meet Ashiq in his office and says "I don't want to involve in
drug trade! I'm ready to deal with arms but not drugs!". Ashiq takes out a pack and
snorts cocaine and says "Arms is just a cover-up! My deals are drugs itself! We ex-

Niamey, Niger
Ashiq picks the call. Zack says "Victor's dead! What next?". Ashiq says "Kill his

Northern Ireland

Northern Ireland
A secret Syndicate meeting without Victor is planned at Ashiq's house. Xiao says "We
need people like him in our syndicate and our opponents will be finished!". Phil says

calm and waited. Once everyone finished speaking Ashiq says "Our Syndicate is a coun-
cil of equals, forged from many banners and voices. Let no tyrant fracture this union
with the fist of a despot. His shadow clouds all we have built, let it be cut down
before darkness spreads". The syndicate decides make a decision. Suddenly a black he-
licopter lands on top of Ashiq's house. With a black and purple tuxedo, Victor comes
out. Victor looks at Ashiq and says "I have come to give you a present, but it was a
surprise seeing you all here!". Victor gives Ashiq a photo with his family dead.
Ashiq shouts in pain and tears and holds Victor's collar asking him why he had done
that. Victor pushes Ashiq and says "You have done a mistake holding my collar in
front of the dignitaries!". A guard give Victor a shotgun. Victor points it at Ashiq,
but shoots Phil and says "He shall not doubt my abilities to control all of these na-
tions! If any contradictions must be addressed now!". Victor puts a dog's belt on
