me here in this syndicate! What is your plan?". Victor says "I am planning for Holy
Trinity that is Xiao, Fiesco and Victor!". Xiao asks "What about Ashiq?". Ashiq stops
eating and turns. Victor pulls out a biscuit packet from his pocket and throws at
Ashiq and says "Fetch!". Victor then looks at Fiesco and says "I have heard you have
many connections in India! Why not learn about me from there?" Saying this Victor
leaves along with Ashiq chained like a dog leading him in the front. Fiesco Contacts
a police officer from Bangalore and asks details of Victor.
Bangalore, India
The police officer explains about Victor Walter, The Most Respected Police officer of
India. Victor never goes under someone in any circumstances, if he has gone, then it
must be a part of a plan. He resigned few months back, but people say he might be un-
dercover. To all his opponents, he says never go against his ideology, but he doesn't
have any ideology like that. His Ideology is nothing but killing people whom he
thinks is wrong. Once his father was killed by a robber, who was a security guard in
the bank. Victor found the robber and brutally killed him with a Cleaver, with the
name 'Victor' in its handle, which is considered his weapon. Nobody can stop him if
he takes out his Weapon. Victor goes rogue when his loved ones are harmed. Fiesco
asked if any case is registered on Xavier's death or Victor's missing from India. The
police officer says that both have not been registered as it is wierd as a murder's
case file is closed without any investigation. Fiesco then asks what was the last
case he was handling. The police officer says, it was an operation related to drug
trafficking in India and primary suspect was Ashiq Umran, but the operation was dis-
banded abruptly. Fiesco understands that Victor is playing a game against the syndi-
cate and warns Xiao. Fiesco was unable to contact Ashiq. Ashiq was kept in a cage
where Ashiq's dog used to live. Ashiq's dog was left free to roam. Ashiq felt angry
and humiliated at the same time.
Northern Ireland
Fiesco and Xiao plan to kill Victor by calling him for a party at a old mansion.
Victor arrives in a casual dress with a leather jacket on and on leash was Ashiq.
There were girls, drugs, Alcohol and guns. People were free to use anything at the
Party. Xiao takes Ritalin to feel and kill Victor. Xiao walks to Victor and says
"Wanna dance?". Victor and Xiao start Ball dancing. While dancing Xiao pulls out a
deck of cards. The deck of cards was Xiao's special weapon that was make from real
steel and cut slice through anything. Xiao flicks a card towards Victor. The card
swipes through Victor's arm causing him to bleed. Fiesco frees Ashiq and Ashiq grabs
a screw driver from the Bartender's table. Xiao starts flicking the cards at Victor
continuously. Victor tries to dodge and takes a cover on a table. One of the card
cuts through the table and comes out but Victor dodges it. Victor throws the table of
Xiao. Xiao falls down. Suddenly, Ashiq stabs Victor from behind. Fiesco kicks Victor
from front, pressing him more to Screwdriver. Ashiq moves back and Victor falls down.
Xiao wakes up and kicks the screwdriver piercing it more. Fiesco and Xiao sets their
hair and says to Ashiq "Now we are the holy Trinity!". Victor slowly wakes up and
pulls out the screwdriver. He asks the bartender for some alcohol and pours it on the
would and drinks some. Victor grabs the screwdriver and runs towards Ashiq. Ashiq
holds his hands kicks Victor and throws him aside grabbing the screwdriver. Ashiq
takes the screwdriver and stabs it in Victor's left chest. Victor starts to vomit
blood. Ashiq then pulls out the screwdriver and says "My Ideology is somewhat same as
yours! Respect is always needed! And you turned me into a dog! You think I'll spare
you?". Victor looks at Ashiq and laughs out loud. He puts his hands into the jacket
and takes out his cleaver and puts it on the table. Victor removes the jacket and
takes the cleaver again. Victor looks at Ashiq. Fiesco finds 'Victor' written in the
handle. Fiesco says "Now there's no stopping him! Run!". Ashiq, Fiesco and Xiao start
running. It starts to rain outside with thunder. Victor starts to follow them walk-
ing, while the three ran. Once they felt, Victor was far, they stopped below a tree.
Suddenly a cleaver hits the tree. Fiesco reads the handle and 'Victor' was written on
it. Ashiq tries to take out the cleaver against Victor but is unsuccessful. Victor
walks towards them and they three start running again. Victor runs, pulls the cleaver
from the tree and throws it on Xiao and splits his head into two. Fiesco is horrified
and slips to fall down. Ashiq tries to wake him up but his leg was injured. When
Victor nearest, Ashiq started to run. Fiesco slowly gets up, Victor takes the cleaver
and says "We thought we were the Holy Trinity, but you shattered it!". Fiesco says
"You're a bloody Undercover Police office!". Victor says "So you know!". Fiesco
punches Victor on his face and Victor falls down. Victor gets up and kicks Fiesco
from behind. Takes the cleaver and cuts Fiesco's both arms apart. Victor says "This
is for the Youth, whose life you ruined with your drugs! Now, this is for myself!"
Saying this Victor beheads Fiesco. Ashiq pulls out his phone from the pocket and
tries to call the cops, the Cops dispatch their team. Victor runs to Ashiq and throws
the cleaver cutting Ashiq's leg. Victor says "You will get a call now!". Victor's
phone rings and the person on the other side says "AU pharmaceutical was bombed! The
whole factory and office!". Victor looks at Ashiq and says "The office you used to
use for distributing fake medicines and drugs is gone!". Victor says "I shall not
kill you with my cleaver!". Victor pulls out a small gun from his shoe and shoots
Ashiq Point-blank. The cops arrive at the scene and asks Victor to stay down. Victor
says "I am an Undercover cop from India! These three are International Drug-Lords!".
Since, there were no legal intimation regarding Victor's arrival to Ireland, the gov-
ernment decide to send him back to India.
Bangalore, India
Victor meets the DGP and says "The main heads are dead! Now the tails won't move un-
til the head works!". DGP congratulated Victor for his accomplishments and feels
sorry for the loss of his family. Victor goes to his house in a taxi and asks him to
wait outside. In his house he finds bullet holes and blood on the floor. Victor falls
down and starts crying out loud, and lies down. The taxi driver enters into the house
after sometime. Victor was still lying down. The taxi driver tries to wake Victor but
is unable to and finds out that Victor was dead. The DGP arrives at the scene and the
reason for death is found to be a heart attack. He already had multiple injuries and
the pain of the loss of his family killed him. After the funeral, DGP keeps a flower
on his tomb and walks.
